spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma/ slob dpon chen po Ar+ya de ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi khan po shrAd+d+ha ka ra varma dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ /'di la rgya gar gyi sh+lo ka stong sum brgya yod/ phyag dpe gnyis la gtugs so
sems kyi sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon Ar+ya de bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /A tsar+ya dz+nyA nA ka ra dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba//
slob dpon chen po ar+ya de bas mdzad pa'i bdag byis brlab pa'i rim pa rdzogs so//
mngon par byang chub pa'i rim pa 'bras bu dang bcas pa/ /slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa'i man ngag rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAd+d+ha ka ra war ma dang / dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gten la phab pa'o//
gsang ba 'dus pa'i ro bsreg gi cho ga 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAd+d+ha ka ra varma las lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rdzogs rim mthar phyin pa slob dpon ar+ya de bas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud las don dam pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par gzhag pa'i rim par phye ba ste bzhi pa'o/ /sgrub pa'i slob dpon klu'i blo'i zhal snga nas kyi mdzad par bzhag pa'i rim pa bzhi pa rdzogs so//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga nyi shu pa zhes bya ba slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bya sa'i gtsug lag khang du shung kye ston pa dar ma rdo rjes zhus nas/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po ti la ka ka la sha zhes bya ba pha rol tu phyin pa gsang sngags kyi theg pa la sogs pa mtha' dag chub pa'i zhal snga nas dang/ bod kyi sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po ban+de pa tsab nyim grags kyis bsgyur ba'o//
las kyi mtha' rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya ba rje btsun 'phags pa klu'i blo'i zhabs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma rje btsun ma Ni ka shrI dz+nyA na dang/ bla ma rje btsun chen po de ben+d+ra'i zhal snga nas gu par mnyan nas chags lo tsA ba shA kyi'i dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gten la phab pa'o//
rim pa khong du bsdu ba'i man ngag gi rim pa'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon chen po klu'i blo rig pa 'dzin pa'i dngos grub brnyes nas da rung dpal gyi ri la bzhugs pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /chos kyi gzhi dkon mchog gsum gyi rten dpal tshangs pa 'byung ba'i gtsug lag khang du/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po a lang+ka ka la sha'i zhal snga nas dang bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur ro//
rim pa lnga'i 'grel pa rnal 'byor pa'i yid kyi 'phrog ces bya ba rdzogs so// 'di ni dpyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po'i phyag dpe'i rgya dpe las bod kyi skad du / dge slong rin chen grub kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'i yi ge pa ni dge slong sgra tshad pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud kyi srid pa skye ba'i rim pas rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon zla ba'i grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gzhung 'di'i tshad ni rkang pa dang bcas pa'i rgya phrag gnyis pa'o/ /dpal bi kra ma shrI la'i gtsug lag khang chen por paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po ta thA ga ta rak+Shi ta'i zhal snga nas dang/ /lo tsA ba klog kya gzhon nu 'bar gyis bsgyur ro/ /slad kyis dpal dpe med lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang du rgya gar gyi mkhan po mkhas pa chen po dI paM ka ra rak+Shi ta dang/ khams pa dge slong lo tsA ba ba ris bcos shing de zhus nas gtan la phab pa//
rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /lI la badz+ra yi zhabs kyis mdzad pa'o/ /bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rgya dpe la bltas nas/ dge slong rin chen grub kyis/ dpa' bo'i lo smin drug can gyi zla ba'i tshes nyer bzhi la bsgyur ba'o/ /yi ge pa ni dge slong rin chen rgyal mtshan no/ /sngags kyi nges pa thog ma ste/ gnyis la dgod pa bstan pa'o/ rnam par bzhag pa yang gsum ste/ bzhi pa de nyid stan pa'o/ zhes pa sgrub thabs kyi go rim ste/ 'di'i don ni dang por sngags kyi tshig sgrub thabs las phyung nas sems kyi kun tu brtags pa nges par 'gyur ro/ /de nas phung po la sogs pa rnams su rnam par snang mdzad la sogs pa'i rnam pas dgod pa'o/ bkod pa'i lha rnams re re'i mthar gyis rang gi mtshan nyid yongs su shes shing nges par rtogs pa'i lha'i 'khor lo'o/ zhes pa ni rnam par bzhag pa'o/ phra mo'i rnal 'byor gyi gcig tu byas nas rab tu zhugs te gnas pa las langs te/ nges par byung ba'i sngags las dgod par 'gyur ro zhes so//
bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i rnal 'byor dang bgegs bsal ba'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /slob dpon shrad+d+ha ka ra barma dang/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'brel pa slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
zung du 'jug pa gsal ba zhes bya ba dbang gis cho ga dkyil 'khor chen po'i dngos grub brnyes pa'i mkhas pa chen po sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mkhas pa chen po bsod snyoms pa/ shAkya shrI b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas dang/ shAkya'i dge slong kun dga' rgyal mtshan bzang pos thob ste thos nas bsgyur cing zhus te gten la phab pa'o//
slob dpon nag po'i zhal snga nas bla ma'i man ngag la brten te mdzad pa'i dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po nag po'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po 'gos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje sems dpa' mchod pa'i cho ga/ slob dpon chen po nag po pa'i zhal snga nas bla ma'i man ngag las bzung ste mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po nag po'i zhal snga nas dang bod kyi lo tsA ba 'gos khug pa lhas btsas kyis bsgyur ba'o//
bdag drin bla ma'i rgyud dang ni/ blo dman rnams la phan gdags phyir/ bla ma dam pa'i man ngag bzhin/ gtor ma'i cho ga bris pa yin/ dpal ldan gsang 'dus gtor ma 'dis/ lam la gnas dang 'bras myong gis/ tshogs rdzogs sdug bsngal bsal ba'i phyir/ slob dpon nag pos mdzad pa yin/ rdzogs so//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga'i rim pa slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ rdzogs so/ pN+Di ta de nyid dang 'gos lhas btsas kyi bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje 'chang chen po'i lam gyi rim pai man ngag bdud rtsi gsang ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po sgra dbyangs bcu gcig pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI b+ha dra/ lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga/ za hor gyi mkhas pa chen po shAn+ta de wa/ zhes bya ba mngon bar shes par lnga dang ldan pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sbyin sreg gi cho ga rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrad+d+ha ka ra war ma dang / d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la sh+lo ka brgyad cu rtsa gsum yod//
mdor bsdus pa'i bsgrubs thabs kyi 'grel ba rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po karma badz+ra nyid kyis bsgyur zhing gtan la phab pa'o//
sgrub pa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/ /slob dpon chen po dpal dz+nyA na badz+ra bya ba//gsang ba 'dus pa'i rim pa gsum ngag dang ldan pa/ bcom ldan 'das mi skyod pa'i zhabs kyi ze'u 'bru spyi bos len pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ / rgya gar gyi mkhan po dge bsnyen chen po btsun pa ku mA ra dang bod kyi lo tsA ba lha btsun pas bsgyur cing zhus pa dge'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor kyi lha'i sku la bstod pa zhes bya ba rnal 'byor gyis dbang phyug mi gnas rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsar+ya shrad+d+ha ka ra war ma dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
byang chub sems kyi 'grel bshad 'di/ /bsgyur las 'gro ba thams cad ni/ /byang chub sems ni thob par shog//lho brag drma seng+ge yis/ /chos re'ang lam rings bgrod nas zhus/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtis bsgyur cing bshad nas gtan la phab pa'i byang chub sems kyis 'brel pa bshad pa rdzogs so//
rim pa lnga'i dka' 'grel don gsal ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po brtson 'grus bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta bir+ya b+ha drA nyid dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba 'bro dge bsnyen chen po she rab brton 'grus kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rim lnga'i dgongs 'grel zla ba'i 'od zer zhes bya ba/ /paN+Di ta chen po 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /shar phyogs dza ga ta la'i paN+Di ta bi b+hu ti tsan+d+rasa bsgyur ba'o//
sgrub thabs mdor byas kyi dka' 'grel/ /paN+Di ta bi b+hu ti tsan+d+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyis dpal bo'i lo mgo can gyi zla ba'i tshe bcu dgu la rgya dpe la bltas nas/ dpal ri phug gi dben gnas su bsgyur ba'o//
rim pa lnga'i dka' 'grel don gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma'i bshad pa shes rab mchog dang ldan pa'i slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje sems dpa'i bsgrub thabs kyis bshad pa/ slob dpon ta thA ga ta rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so//tho ling dpal dpe med lhung gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang du rgya gar gyi mkhan po mkhas pa chen po di paM ka ri rak+Shi ta dang khams ba ri lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
sdus pa'i rim pa'i dka' 'grel slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so// bal po'i dge bsnyen su'o 'di lta dang dge slong lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dad pa smra ba zhes bya ba'i bstod pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA shri gup+ta dang / sgra sgyur gyi lo tsA ba ban+de rin chen bzang pos sgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
notice of contents of the 19th volume of the bstan 'gyur dpe bsdur ma
rim pa lnga pa'i dka' ba btus pa'i bshad pa'o/ /slob dpon chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i rim pa lnga pa'i dka' bgrel/ slob dpon chen po b+ha bya kIrtasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po rgyal ba mchog gi zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya brtson 'grus kyis zhus shing bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
mdor byas pa'i sgrub thabs kyi rnam par bshad pa rdzogs so//
rim pa lnga pa'i bshad pa nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyi zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po rdo rje slob dpon chen po karma badz+ra'i zhal snga nas dang/ dge slong gzhon nu tshul khrims kyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
zung du 'jug pa'i rim pa'i dka' 'grel slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dam tshig rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kriSh+Na paN+Di ta dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
kha che'i mkhas pa chen po dpal lak+Shi zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i rim pa lnga pa'i 'grel pa gsal bar bed pa zhes ba ba rdzogs so// yon gyi bdag po dga' rab gza' yis zhus te/ rgya gar gyi mkhas pa paN+Di ta chen po tA ra ka sha'i sras man+tra ka la sha nyid kyis bsgyur zhing gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i sbas pa'i man ngag tu phyung ba rnams 'dor bsdus pa bstan pa slob ma la phan pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rab tu zhi ba'i ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud phyi ma zhes bya ba'i le'u bco brgyad pa'i phyed kyi tshig dang don rgya cher 'grel cing rnam par bshad pa/ /man ngag gi rgya mtsho thigs pa 'thor bas kyang gzhan dga' ba dang skrag pa skyed par byed pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon bi sho mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon tha ga na'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'o/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsar+ya shrad+d+hA ka ra war ma dang / d+harmA shrI b+ha dra dang/ zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de rin chen bzang pos bcos shing bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//

rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyud 'grel pa chen po/ rin po che ljon shing zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po tse lu pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gi mkhan po ka ma la gup+ta dang / bod kyi zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba chen po/ mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgyal bas byin pa sman pa'i dbus/ /bla ma sangs rgyas bka' drin gyis/ /dpal ldan 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi ni/ /dka' 'grel 'di ni byas pa yin/ /slob dpon rgyal bas byin gyis mdzad pa'i dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dka' 'grel las le'u bco brgyad pa'i bshad pa rdzogs so//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba/ /slob dpon dri med sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta su na ya shrI mi tra dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dkyil 'khor chen po slob dpon byang phyogs kyi lam la mkhas pa chen po'i zhabs la dran par byas pa/ /slob dpon zla ba'i 'od dang ming gzhan rin chen rdo rje'i myu gus mdzad pa/ /le'u bco brgyad pa'i rnam par bshad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po su na ya shrI mi tra dang / bod kyi sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba ge slong dar ma grags kyis mang yul skyid grong gi lha khang ke ru dang / ag rtsar sgang du bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
yang dag rig byed ces bya ba rgyud phyi ma'i rnam par bshad pa slob dpon bid+ya pa das mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang bod kyi lo tsA ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad sbyar snyim pa'i me tog ces bya ba/ slob dpon chen po rat+na A kar shAn+tisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po shAn+ta b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba chen po mgos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//

gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad sbyar snyim pa'i me tog ces bya ba/ slob dpon chen po rat+na A kar shAn+tisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po shAn+ta b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba chen po mgos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad pa/ /zla ba'i 'od zer zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rab tu dga' ba'i 'byung gnas go cha'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rim pa gnyis pa'i de kho na nyid bsgom pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhal gyi lung / dkyil 'khor gyi slob dpon chen po lha sangs rgyas dpal gyi ye shes zhabs kyis bsdus pa zhal nas zhal du brgyud pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal ldan o rgyan yul nas byung ba yi/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyi zhal snga nas kyi sgrub thabs man ngag go rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba dge slong khyung weng rin chen bzang pos bsgyur zhing zhus te tan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs kyi pad+ma'i ze'u 'bru'i rdul la reg pa/ slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar mkhan po A tsar+ya shrad+d+ha ka ra war ma dang/ /zhu chen lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
brnyen bsgrub yan lag bzhi'i sgrub thabs kun tu bzang mo zhes bya ba/ dkyil 'khor chen po'i slob dpon sangs rgyas dpal ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po smri ti dz+nyA na kirtisa bsgyur pa'o//
he ru ka yi sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rim par phye ba dpal he ru ka'i sgrub pa'i thabs kyi 'grel pa rdzogs so//
grol ba'i thig le zhes bya ba dkyil 'khor chen po'i rdo rje slob dpon sangs rgyas dpal ye shes zhabs kyis zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhon po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba chen po mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhu ste gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes kyi zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa bdag sgrub pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta shAn+ti b+ha dra dang lo tsA ba mgos lhas btsas kyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rje btsun dzaM b+ha la'i sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon mi bskyod rdo rje sangs rgyas ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shud d+ha ka ra b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ gsang ba'i dzam b+ha la'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /mkhas pa chen po dza ya se na'i zhal snga nas dang / btsun pa d+harmA yon tan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
rgya che ba'i dzaM b+ha la'i sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so//
stang stabs kyi bkod pa slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon mar me mdzad bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra war ma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mdzas pa'i me tog ces bya ba rim pa gnyis pa'i de kho na nyid bsgom pa zhes bya ba zhal gyi lung gi 'grel pa/ slob dpon chen po bi ta pA das mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
kun tu bzang po'i sgrub pa'i thabs kyi 'grel pa byang phyogs kyi dge slong yon tan 'byung gnas bzang po'i slob ma shrI pha la badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bir ya b+ha dra dang / sgra sgyur ba'i lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
dpal kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po tha ga na'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsaR+Ya shrad+d+hA ka ra varma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing gtan la phan pa'o//

yan lag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs kyi rgya cher bshad pa snying po snye ma zhes bya ba slob dpon dpal kun tu bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po n+ya ya na shrI dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po shAkya'i dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bal yul mthil du bsgyur ba'o//
grol ba'i thig le zhes bya ba'i rnam par bshad pa slob dpon chen po bi ta pA tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba chen po mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga 'jig rten snang byed ces bya ba sho lo ka bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhall snga mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bir ya b+ha dra dang / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po dge long rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
yan lag bzhi pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs kun tu bzang mo zhes bya ba'i rnam par bshad pa slob dpon chen po bi ta pA tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po mnga' bdag ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub pa'i thabs 'jig rten snang byed zhes bya ba'i rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon chen po bi ta pA das mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba mnga' bdag ye shes rgyal mtshan byis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa sgrub pa'i thabs/ dngos grub 'byung ba'i gter zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po bi ti pA das mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba lha btsan po mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sbyor ba bdun pa zhes bya ba/ dbang bzhi'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon chen po bi ta pA das mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma gu h+ya dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
gtor ma chen po'i rim pa slob dpon chen po pi ta pA das mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma lu gu hu dang / bod kyi lo tsA chen po mnga' bdag ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mi shigs pa'i rin po che zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon che po pe ta pA das mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bdag gi don 'grub par byed pa zhes bya ba/ rnal 'byor gyi bya ba'i rim pa/ slob dpon chen po pi ta pA das mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba/ dpal rnam par snang mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /su n+yA shrI'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba dge slong g.yung drung 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon chen po mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa'i/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i sgrub thabs kyi rnam par bshad pa/ dkyil 'khor chen po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon mkhas pa chen po/ dpal kun tu bzang po'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bod yul du bod ris kyi dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal lha btsan po khri mgon btsan gyis yon bdag byas nas/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti kirtisa bsgyur nas gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrAd+d+hA ka ra varma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te/ slad kyis kyang bcos nas gtan la phab pa'o//
dkyil 'khor bri ba'i cho ga slob dpon bsod snyoms pa yis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po/ dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba dge legs 'phel//
dga' ba'i sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon chen po rgyal bas byin pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta pad+ma ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur lags so//
dpal mi bskyod rdo rje sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon dpal rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'dus zhing rtogs pa sla ba'i 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ dpal mkhas pa chen po su na ya shrI mi tra paN+Di tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bsgyur byed kyi lo tsA ba klog skya lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'bar gyis sgyur cing zhus pa'o//
mdor bsdus pa'i dbang gi rab tu byed pa/ /slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal dga' ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gzhung tshang ni tshigs bcad sum brgya ste bam po gcig go/ tho ling gis gtsug lag khang du/ rje mnga' bdag btsan po/ rtse lde btsan gyi bka' lung gis/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong ba ris bsgyur ba'o//
gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang bskur ba'i cho ga mdor bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /'di ni paN+Di ta ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa/ bal po'i paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba klog skya gzhon nu 'bar ba'i zhal snga nas dang / mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
yan lag bdun dang ldan pa'i bsgrub par bya ba'i tshig su bcad pa gnyis kyi bshad pa rdzogs so/ /gzhung 'di mkhas pa rnams kyis ni/ /legs par rnam par btsi byas nas/ /brgya phrag rnam pa bzhi dag dang / nyi shur lngar yang dag ldan/ /slob dpon dag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa'i yan lag bdun dang ldan pa'i bzhi pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis rgya gar shar phyogs kyi dpe las zhu thug dbyar khral 'tshal ba lags so//
de kho na nyid rin po che snang ba slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
de kho na nyid rin po che snang ba'i bshad pa/ slob dpon ngag gi dang phyugs grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba mgos lhas btsas kyis rgya gar shar phyogs kyi dpe las zhu gtug dbyar khral 'tshal ba lags so//
rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon dpe med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bir ya b+ha tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi rim pas bsgrub pa/ slob dpon chane po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kye zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phan pa'o/ to long nyis brgya phul/ bo longs nyis shu la/ to long gcig/bo long bcu gnyis zhog cig/
'jig rten mgon po sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bstod pa slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
de kho na nyid bcu pa slob dpon rgyan pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga slob dpon zla ba'i dkyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pun+ya kIrti dang / bod kyi dge slong nams rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
'di ni bstan pa'i nor thams cad pa ste/ paN+Di ta chen po rat+na kirti mdzas pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta rat+na kirti dang / lo tsA ba chings yon tan 'bar gyi bsgyur ba legs so//

dbang bskyur ba'i rab tu byed pa ni de ltar bstan pa yin no/ /slob dpon mkhas pa chen po bsod snyoms pa dge slong 'od bsrungs gzhon nu'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzags so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ta thA ga ta rak+Shi ta dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban d+he rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i sbyor ba yan lag drug pa zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyi lugs/ paN+Di ta smi tis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ye shes zhabs lugs kyi sbyor ba yan lag drug pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
'jam pa'i rdo rje mchod pa'i cho ga slob dpon dpal sbyin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /shAkya'i dge slong blo gros seng ges zhu chen byas nas paN+Di ta chen po bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra nas das rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//

arg+ha'i cho ga snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon snang byed zla bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ba ren+d+ra ba'i zhal sna nas dang / lo tsA ba dge slong pradz+nyA kIrtasa bsgyur ba'o//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga ye shes snang ba zhe bya ba slob dpon snang byed zla bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ba ren+d+ra pa'i zhal nas dang / lo tsA ba dge slong pradz+nyA kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
paN+Di ta mi 'jigs pa'i phyag gis mdzad pa/ rab gnas kyi cho ga mdor bsdus pa rdzogs so//
zhes bya ba slob dpon dpal kA ca zhabs kyis mdad pa rdzogs so// 'di bod kyi skad du/ dri ma med pa mkhyen brtse'i dban gphyug / chos kyi rje chen po rgyal dbang sprul sku rin po che'i zhal snga nas kyis bka' bzhin/ zha lu lo tsA ba dge slong d+harma pA la b+ha dras/ sa skyong dam pa dpon chen kun dga' bsod nams rin chen dbang gi rgyal po'i bdag rkyen las/ dben gnas dpal e waM chos 'khor du bsgyur ba'o//
shi ba bde 'gror sbyar ba'i cho ga shin tu 'dod pa mchog tu gyur pa zhes bya ba'i ming can dpal stong nyid ting 'dzin rdo rje'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a ba d+hU ti bai ro tsa na badz+ra'i zhal snga nas dang/ bod kyi lo tsA ba khams pa ldi (ding) ri chos kyi grags pas bsgyur ba'o//
tha ma'i cho ga ming gi rnam grangs gshin po bde bar gshegs pa'i gnas la 'god pa zhes bya ba/ /paN+Di ta dpal ting nge 'dzin rdo rjes mdzas pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal phyogs dbang dga' byed kyi zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba dge slong pradz+nyA kirtisa bsgyur//
rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dgongs pa thams cad nye bar len pa'i 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na gar+b+ha / bod kyi lo tsA ba bai ro tsa nas bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa skad gsar bcad kyis byas pa'o//
dkyil 'khor gyi slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so།།
rdo rje bzhad pa'i slob dpon gyis/ sems can ye shes bskyed phyir ro/ dpal bde ba chen po'i bsgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /
dpal bde ba chen po'i 'grel ba slob dpon chen po bi mA la gar+b+hasa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gsang chen lhan cig skyes pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rdo rje sgeg pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i rigs kyi paN+Di ta chen po bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i 'grel ba bla ma'i man ngag nyid las bris pa dam pa rnams kyi spyi bos blangs pa paN+Di ta chen po smri ti dz+nyA kIrtis mdzad cing / paN+Di ta de nyid kyi rang 'gyur du mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po rdo rje slob dpon/ smi ti dz+nyA na kIrtis mdzad pa lha mo bzhis yongs su zhus pa'i rnam par bshad pa/ man ngag rgyas pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po rdo rje smri ti dz+nyA kIrti nyid kyis bsgyur cing zhus te bshad nas gtan la phab pa'o//
lha mo bzhis pa'i rgyud kyi bshad pa slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dran pa ye shes grags pas bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba zhes bya ba rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po dka' 'grel/ slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi dza ya shrI d+ha ra dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur te/ slad nas a tsar+ya shrad+d+ha ka ra war mas zhus te gtan la phab pa//
Colophon: dpal gshin rje nag po'i dka' 'grel/ lhan cig skyes pa'i snang ba zhes bya ba slob dpon shrI d+ha ras mdzad pa las/ rim par phye ba bco brgyad pa'i bshad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po shan+ta b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur te/ zhus nas gtan la phab pa//
dpal gshin rje dgra nag po zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po'i dka' 'grel/ rin po che'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rat+na ka ra shan+tisa/ nyung bar sbyar ba 'di yongs su rdzogs so/ /A tsaR+Yabi na ya tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi she rab kyis dad pas bsgyur cing zhus te btan la phab pa'o//
de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs gshin rje gshed nag po'i rgyud kyi rgya cher 'grel pa mngon par mthong pa lam gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po kriSh+Na chen pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dzA na kIrtis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
ma ga d+ha gyi shar gyi phyogs/ b+haM ga la zhes bya ba'i yul/ bi kram pu ri'i gtsugs lag khang / sku khrungs mkhas pa chen po las/ a ba d+hU tI bar gyur pa'i/ gzhon nu zla bas mdzad pa yin/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po li la badz+ra la/ bod kyo lo tsA bsod nams rgyal mtshan ni/ ru pa dpyal la mkhan ni ser rtsa yis/ rnyed dang grags pa'i don du 'di ma bsgyur/ rang gi slob ma rnams kyis gsol ba btab nas/ phan pa'i bsam pa 'di don legs par bsgyur/gal te lhag chad 'ga' zhig yod srid na/ rgya dpe gzhan dang mkhas pa gzhan dag la/ da dung bdag nyid zhus gtugs legs par bgyid/ sgra yi ming dang rnam rtogs sna tshogs pas/ lo tsA gzhan gyis bcos pa ma mdzad cig /mnyan cing shes na 'di la bshad pa mdzad/ dpal gshin rje gshed nag po'i dka' 'grel rin po che 'i phreng ba zhes bya ba / slob dpon gzhon nu zla bas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gshin rje nag po'i rnam 'grel ye shes sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon pad+ma pA Nis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi slob dpon pa ra me shwa ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rong zom chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//

tshig gi snang ba grub pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta dA na kIrti dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur//
gshin rje gshed nag po'i dkyil 'khor sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon mkhas pa dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dA na kIrti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i bstod pa slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba mar do chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur ba'o//
gshin rje gshed 'byung ba zhes bya ba slob dpon che po la li ta badz+ra'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a mo g+ha badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba cog gru shes rab bla mas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po la li ta badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gshin rje gshed nag po'i sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon nyin mor byed pa'i grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis/ rgya gar dpe phyi mo dang gtugs te gtan la bab pa'o//
gshin rje'i dgra nag po sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon g+ho Sha badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i mkhan po su ma ti tsan+d+ra'i zhal snga nas dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de tshogs chag chung bas bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o
dpal gshin rje'i gshed dgra nag po'i thabs 'khor lo'i don rgyas pa bshad pa dang bcas pa slob dpon mi bskyod rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa 'di yongs su rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsar+ya tsan+d+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gshin rje gshed nag po'i rgyud bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa las/ mkhas pa rnams kyis gsol ba btab pas/ dge slong bsod snyoms pa ka ma la rak+shi ta zhes bya bas bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
zhes bya ba ni maN+Dal gnyis gshegs su gsol ba'o/ /yi dam lha'i maN+Dal ni so so'i sgrub thabs kyi gzhung las shes par bya'o/ /slob dpon chen po rnyog med rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a du la d+hasa dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dngos kyi maN+Dala rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la rak+Shi tas/ /gshin rje gshed kyi rgyud bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa la brten nas maN+Dala gyi cho ga mdzad pa'o/ /lo tsA ba shrI pradz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
gshin rje'i dgra nag po'i sgrub pa'i thabs/ ku mu ta kha bye ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /A tsaR+Ya bi nA ya tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
nag po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i mdor bsdus pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so//
khro bo'i rgyal po gshin rje gshed nag po'i dus mthar phyin pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhas pa chen po shrI paN+Di tas mdzad pa'o/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtis rang 'gyur du bsgyur pa'o//
gshin rje gshed nag po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
gshin rje gshed nag por snang mdzad kyi mngon rtogs zhes bya ba/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po mkhas par grags pa dpal mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
gshin rje gshed rin chen 'byung ldan gyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba slob dpon po dpal mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
'od dpag tu med pa'i snying po 'dod chags gshin rje gshed kyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gshin rje gshed rdo rje rnon po zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA kIrtis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
rdo rje sems ma bde ba sgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba slob dpon mkhas pa chen po mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA kIrtis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
rdo rje mkha' 'gro rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon mar me mdzad pas mdzad pa rdzogs so
rdo rje bde rgyas dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
rdo rje las gau rI'i sgrubs thabs zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
rje btsun 'jam dpal gshen rje gshed mchod pa'i cho ga'i rim pa zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po kriSh+Na paN+Di tas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sangs rgyas gshin rje gsed nag po'i sgrub thabs/ nA da ku be ra las byung pa'i don/ kun da na ke ri na bzhugs pa'i mkhas pa chen po rnal 'byor pa nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA kIrtis rang 'gyur di mdzad pa'o//
dpal gshin rje gshed nag po sgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po ka ma la rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtis rang 'byur du mdzad pa'o//
khor bo tho ba gshin rje gshed kyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dbyug pa gshin rje gshed rnam par 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po di paM ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
ral gri gshin rje gshed gtum pa'i sgrub thabs zhes bya rdzogs so//
pad ma gshin rje gshed shes rab bde ba can gyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
gshin rje gsheg po'i maN+Dala gyi cho ga zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /zangs gleng rnal 'byor nA ga bu ra yis/ rnal 'byor ma ka ra tri ta nyid la/ gu tsha rgyal ba'i bu nyid btang nas kyang / ta ru pa ri du khrod tshal nyid du/ rnal 'byor 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis 'khor lo nang / gsol btab rnal 'byor rnams kyi zhal ngo ru/ maN+Dal cho ga bsod snyoms pa yis byas/ ding sang rnal 'byor lta spyod ldan pa yis/ dus rnams rtag tu maN+Dala 'bad par rigs//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka lA pa ma hA zhes bya bas mdzad pa/ mchod rten gyi cho ga rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA dz+nyA na yis rang 'gyur du byas pa'o//so ma pu ri gtsug lag khang chen du/ nag po zhabs zhes bya ba'i rnal 'byor pas/ rnal 'byor tshe 'phos de ba ba la yis/ yab mchog d+harmA pA la 'das gyur pa'i/ ched du gsol btab rgyal po'i zhal snga ru/ mchod rten cho ga me tog tshal du mdzad/ spros bcas spros med tshul gyi lam mchog 'di/ deng sang rnal 'byor rnams kyis gdab par rigs//
gshin rje gshed kyi ro bsreg gi cho ga zhes bya ba slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i rim pa slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bla ma nag po'i zhabs nyid chen po la// gser gling rnal 'byor gu Na dz+nya na yis// bram ze karma tsan+dra btang nas kyang // rnal 'byor nams kyis zhal ngor sbyin sreg 'di// dpal mchog rdo rje gdan du rnam par brtsams// rnal 'byor bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA dz+nyA na yis rang 'gyur du byas pa'o//
gshin rje gshed nag po'i rgyud las bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa nas phyung ba slob dpon nag po zhab skyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyuro//
'jam dpal gshin rje gshed khro bo chen po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal rdo rje'i blos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal gshin rje gshed nag po'i 'khor lo bri ba'i cho ga rdzogs so//
'di ni gshin rje dgra nag po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon kun tu bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon don yod rdo rje yis/ legs par bsal byed sgrub thabs 'di/ bsgyur ba'i bsod nams grangs med dang / gzhan yang smon lam 'di btab pas/ rgyud dang sgrub thabs mi 'bral zhing / de yi man ngag rjes 'brang bas/ bdag dang gzhan dag sems can kun/ gshin rje gshed kyi zhal mthong shog/
gshin rje gshed kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon 'gro bzang snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
nag po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon la li ta badz+ra mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal kriSh+Na ya ma a ri'i rgyud las/ 'o ma sgrub pa'i man ngag tu byas la/ A tsar+ya dzi mu Da pA tA las mdzad pa/ 'o ma sgrub pa'i man ngag rdzogs so/ /A tsar+ya badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur pa'o//
gshed nag 'khor lo'i man ngag slob dpon chen po nag po d+hisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba dge slong chos rab kyis bsgyur//
sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon chen po la li ta badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'chi bdag yi dags rgyal po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so//
lag pa'i mchod pa ni/ dA na shrI las bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi dgongs pa nye bar bsdus pa la/ gshin rje gshe nad po'i dkyil 'khor gyi bstod pa/ a tsar+ya kIrtisa zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje 'dzin pas gshin rje gshed po la bsod pa'i le'u'i rgyud las/ bstod pa'i le'u'o rdzogs so//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud kyi dka' 'grel/ rdo rje slob dpon mi bskyod pa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi nA ya tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong she rab kyi bsgyur cing zhu te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rnal 'byor gyi skabs kyi mdo mdor bshad pa// slob dpon so na shrIs mdzad pa rdzogs so// mkhas pa chen po ta thA g ta'i zhal nas brgyud pa'o//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rnal 'byor gyi skabs kyi mdo mdor bshad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi rjes su 'brangs pa'i slob dpon dpal chen po rdo rje grub pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal gzhon nu zla bas mdzad pa'i dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud chen po'i dka' 'grel rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po ta thA ga ta rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba dge slong ba ri rin chen grags pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po nag po pa nyid kyis rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma nyid las blangs nas mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po paN+Di ta bai ro tsa na rak+Shi ta dang bod kyi lo tA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i rgyud gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po rnam pa snang mdzad bsrung pa'i zhabs dang lo tsA ba dge slong ba ri d+harma kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
'jam dpal dbyangs kyes rab mdzad pa phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsar+ya A nan+da dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rdo rje grags kyes bsgyur ba'o//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub pa'i thabs mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon chen po shrI b+ha dras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bsnyen pa'i cho ga'o/ /rdzogs so//
sgrub pa'i cho ga slob dpon zhi ba'i ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs/ Atsar+ya don yod rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /nyid kyi rang 'gyur ro/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po many+dzu shrI dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rong zom chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur cing slar yang phyug 'tshams dbang phyug rgyal pos bsgyur//
dpal 'jam pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon chen po dpal don yod pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur ba'o//
la li ta badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon chen po ke ra li pas mdzad pa de kho na nyid grub pa rdzogs so//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dam tshig la 'jug pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga /dngos grub slob dpon chen po dpal la li ta badz+ra'i zhal snga nas mdzad rdzogs so/ /grub pa brnyes pa paN+Di chen po a mo g+ha badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba mar pa dge bsnyen chos 'bar gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
zhes bya ba rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+DI ta a mo g+ha badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje tsa rtsi ka'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so//
rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon a sho ka shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta d+harma shrI mi tra dang lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thab grub thob kyi 'khor los bsgyur ba'i slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal rdo rje 'phags mo'i sgrub thabs/ grub thob kyi 'khor lor sgyur ba'i slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta chen po rgyal ba'i sras dpal bi b+hu te tsan+d+ra dang / glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis chos kyi rgyal po'i pho brang sku mkhar nyi gzungs su bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal rdo rje dkar mo'isgruba thabs/ grub thob kyi 'khor lor sgyur ba'i slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta rgyal sras dpal bi b+hu tsan+d+ra dang / glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis chos kyi rgyal po'i khab sku mkhar nyi gzungs su bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta dar+pan A tsar+yas mdzad pa rdzogs so// paN+DI ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba zhe sdang rdo rjes dag par bsgyur ba'o//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed ma he'i gdong can dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs// slob dpon many+dzu badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i paN+Di ta b+ha ro phyag rdum dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal ldan rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi tshogs kyi 'khor lo/ slob dpon rat+na A ka shAn+tisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM kara rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur pa'o//
ts+tshu ts+tshuna da ra'i rtog pa rdzogs so/ /b+ha ro phyag rdum gyi phyag dpe las/ rwa rdo rje grags kyis phyis bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi drag pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga a mo g+ha badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rwa rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dpal rjo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon la li ta badz+ra'i zhabs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA tra shrI be de (ba) dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba cog gru ban+de shes rab bla mas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /sgrub pa'i slob dpon la li tas mdzad pa'o//
slob dpon chen po la li ta badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
b+hai ra ba'i zhi ba'i bya ba bdun pa/ paN+Di ta a mo g+ha chung pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rim pa bzhin du bya ba'i cho ga /dpal u rgyan yul du 'dug pa/ dregs pa can 'dul ba'i thabs nye tshe ba/ byang chub kyi sems dang ldan pas bsgrub par bya'o/ /rdzogs so//
gzhan la gus pas mchog tu bkur rdzogs so
dam rdzas rmad du bsgyur te bsten pa'i cho ga rdzogs so//
gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa rdzogs so//
mkhas pa chen po ta thA ga ta rak+Shi tasa mdzad pa'o/ U to pa ti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mal gro blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon dz+nyA na ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so// zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba'o//

de nyid lnga pa'i bstod pa rdzogs so//

dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bstod pa/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / zhang lo tsA ba she rab bla mas bsgyur ba'o//
jam dpal 'jigs byed mtshan gyi bstod pa/ slob dpon las kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs rdo rje 'od ces bya ba/ /slob dpon chen po bai ro tsa na rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mkhas pa chen po bai tsa na rak+Shi ta de nyid dang/ /lo tsA ba glan d+harma ma tis sgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rgya gar gyi mkhas pa chen po paN+Di ta bai ro tsa na rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta bai ro tsa na de nyid dang / lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa 'jams dpal gyi rtog pa thams cad bsdus par 'gyur pa/ rdo rje rab tu 'byed pa zhes bya ba'i cho ga zhib mo las/ slob dpon dpal ldan sgeg pa'i rdo rje yis/ /las dang dngos grub cho ga zhib mo slob dpon rigs pa bzang pos de la phan pa'i le'u gcig mdzad pa dang bcas pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal u pa ya shrI mi tra dang / rong zom chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur te gtan la phab pa
dpal gshin rje gshed nag po gdong drug pa'i 'khor lo'i bsgrub thabs mdor bsdus pa/ /slob dpon de ba A ka ra tsan d+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de ba A ka ra tsan+dra de nyid dang / /cog ro ban+de shes rab bla mas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa
dpal o rgyan gyis yul nas byung ba grub pa'i 'khor lo ji ltar rnyed pa klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
gshin rje mthar byed dmar po'i sgrub thabs rnal 'byor kyi dbang phyug bi rU pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma rje btsun chen po nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer gyis zhal snga nas dang / chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon shrI bi rU pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta dA na shi las rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po'i byin gyis brlabs pa'i man ngag 'od gsal 'char ba'i rim pa slob dpon mthu stobs kyi mgon po dpal bi rU pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta ba ren+d+ra pa'i zhal snga nas dang / chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
shin tu spros pa med pa'i de kho na nyid kyi man ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon dpal ldan mthu stobs kyi mgon po thugs spros pa med pa'i dbyings las ma g.yos bzhin du/ sku'i spros pa dpag tu med pas gdug pa can tshar gcod cing / /bcom ldan 'das kyis dngos su byin gyis brlabs pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po bi rU pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bstan pa bsrung pa'i lha rnams kyi bu gcig pa ltar bskyangs pas rgyal po gzhan gyi phyir rgol bas glags lta bar mi nus pa'i ljongs chos kyis rgyal po'i sku mkhar nyi ma gzugs su/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta dngos grub brnyes pa dpal dar+pan A tsA r+ya dang/ glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
dpal dpa' bo'i rgyal pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma rje btsun nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer gyi zhal snga nas dang / chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/
dpal o rgyan nas 'byung ba gshin rje gshed dmar po'i rgyud chen 'bum phrag gsum pa las byung ba slob dpon bi ru pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta dpal mkhas pa chen po dA na shI las/ yul dbus kyi grub pa thob pa'i gnas drang srong srin po rir bsgyur ba'o/
dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta chen po rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug phyag rgya chen po grub pa/ grub thob kyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po rje btsun nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer gyi zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba chag dge slong chos rje dpal gyis gus pas mnyan nas/ mang yul gyi bzo gnas chen por bsgyur cing zhus btan la phab pa/
dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga paN+Di ta chen po rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dpal 'dzin gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta rje btsun chen po dpal gshin rje gshed kyis rjes su gzung ba/ nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer gyi zhal snga nas/ chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
rnal 'byor bzhi'i de kho na nyid ces bya bar rang byin gyis brlab pa'i man ngag grub thob kyis 'khor los sgyur ba mthu stobs la mngal brnyes pa/ dpal ldan rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug bram ze dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dar paN A tsar+ya dang / glo bo lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sgrub thabs/slob dpon chen po dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lha'i skad la legs par zhugs pa'i shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos skad gnyis smra ba rnams kyi gdan sa/ dpal thar pa'i gling gi gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o/
gshin rje gshed dmar po maN+Dala du mchod pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba/ dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//lha'i skad la legs par zhugs pa'i shAkya'i dge slong nyi mas skad gnyis smra ba rnams kyi gdan sa dpal thar pa gling gi gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o/
gshin rje gshed nag po dang gshin rje gshed dmar po'i mchod pa'i cho ga/ slob dpon chen po paN+Di ta dpal/ dpal 'dzin gyi zhal nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//paN+Di ta nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang / chag chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
gshin rje gshed dmar po'i ting nge 'dzin gyi cho ga slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po dA na shI las rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma rje btsun chen po nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang / chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sgrub pa'i thabs dpal rnam par snang mdzad srung bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma rje btsun chen po nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer gyi zhal snga nas/ chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
rang byin gyi brlabs pa'i rim pa man ngag dang bcas pa gshin rje gshed dmar po'i mngon par rtogs pa rdzogs so//slob dpon chen po mkhas shing dngos grub brnyes pa blo gros bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen po bla ma rje btsun nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer gyis zhal snga nas/ gus pas mnyan nas chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
'khor lo'i cho ga nye bar bsdus pa paN+Di ta rdo rje gdan pa nis ka lam ka'i zhal snga nas dang/ /dpyal lo tsA ba dpal chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
dpal gshin rje gshed kyi las tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i de kho na nyid gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba/ sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta rdo rje gdan pa ni ska laM ka'i zhal snga nas dang / dpyal lo tsA ba dpal chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
slob dpon chen po blo bzang snying po zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i gshin rje'i dgra dmar po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /lha'i skad la legs par zhugs pa'i shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos skad gnyis smra ba rnams kyis gdan sa dpal thar pa gling gi gtsug lag khang du bsgrubs pa'o/ /gshin rje dgra dmar yon tan 'byung gnas sgrub thabs chos/ /rgya gar dpe 'di bod kyis mi rtogs pas/ /dam pa se tsa'i rig 'dzin skad gnyis pa/ /chos kyi bzang po'i dpe las gus par bsgyur/ /sa'i steng na nyi zla ltar gyur cig /
gshin rje dmar po'i rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor zhes bya ba/ mkhas pa chen po 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
dpal gshin rje gshed kyi 'tsho ba'i de kho na nyid ces bya ba/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta da r+paN A tsA r+ya'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta dngos grub brnyes pa dar+paN A tsA r+ya de nyid dang / glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis/ chos kyi rgyal po'i sku mkhar nyi zungs su bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
gshin rje mthar byed dmar po'i byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa grub thob kyi 'khor los bsgyur ba bram ze dpal 'dzin gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dar+paN A tsAR+Ya dang / glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis bsgyur ba'o/
ting nge 'dzin gyi bcud len gyi byin rlabs grub thob kyi bdag po mkhas pa chen po dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//rgya gar gyi mkhan po de ba A ka ra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba las//dus phyis rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta dar+paNa A tsar+ya dang lo tsA ba dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa zhe sdang rdo rjes bsgyur cing zhus te slar dag par byas so//snga 'gyur la 'di tshan che tsam gada'o/ gsung ngo o/
'od 'chang ma'i sgrub thabs ting 'dzin gyi bcud len gyi man ngag ting nge 'dzin la mnga' brnyes pa dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo pan snga ma dang 'dra/ 'di'i man ngag cig sngar yang snyan brgyud du byung 'dug ste/ gzhung sngar ma 'gyur gsung /
rang sems gong du 'pho ba'i man ngag slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi gdams pa de nyid kyis mdzad pa'o/ /paN+Di ta rgya gar mngon shes can dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba 'gos khug pas bsgyur ba las/ phyis sa'i steng na 'gran zla dang bral ba dar+paN A tsAr+ya dang / lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen gyis grong du bsgyur cing zhus pa'o/
'pho ba'i byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa bcom ldan 'das kyis dngos su byin gyis brlabs pa dpal 'dzin chen pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma shar phyogs pa chen po dar+paN A tsAR+Ya dang / glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong pradz+nyA rat+nasa sku mkhar nyi zungs su bsgyur ba'o/
dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sreg byed me'i cho ga zhes bya ba dpal 'dzin gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//rgya gar gyi mkhan po da r+paN A tsAr+ya dang dge slong shes rab rgyal tshan gyis mang yul du bsgyur cing zhus pa'o/
bdud rtsi lnga yi byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dpal bi rU pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po da r+paN A tsAr+ya dang / lo tsA ba zhe sdang rdo rjes mang yul gyi gtsug lag chen por zhus shing bsgyur ba'o/
phyir bzlog man ngag gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed dmar po'i zhal gyi gdams pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dngos grub mchog brnyes pa'i dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po a nu pa ma rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan gyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa/ dus phyis chos kyi rgyal po'i sku mkhar gnyis su rgya gar shar phyogs kyi mkhas pa chen po dar+paN A tsAr+ya dang/ lo tsA ba glo bo shes rab rin chen gyis bsgyur cing zhus so/ /'di'i dpe skabs su rgya gar bal po thams cad du rgyun chad pa las phyis u rgyan du mkha' 'gro ma rgya mtsho'i gos can las/ rnal 'byor sen+ta wa len+tas zhus te byung ngo/
'jam dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sngags btu ba/ slob dpon dpal 'dzin zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta dA na shI la dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba bsod nams seng+gesa bsgyur ba'o/
gshin rje gshed kyi yid bzhin kyi nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs b+hang+ga la'i paN+Di ta dA na shI la zhes bya bas gnas byin gyis brlabs pa drang srong srin po rir rang 'gyur du byas pa'o/
