gshin rje gshed kyi yid bzhin kyi nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs b+hang+ga la'i paN+Di ta dA na shI la zhes bya bas gnas byin gyis brlabs pa drang srong srin po rir rang 'gyur du byas pa'o/
bcom ldan 'das gshin rje'i gshed dmar po'i sgrub thabs lam gyi snying po zhes bya ba mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor pa chen po bud+d+ha dz+nyA na pA das/ ug ya na 'bar ba'i phug tu DA kI shA ri badz+ra wA rA hI nyid las dngos grub thob nas lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam par dag pas yi ger byas pa rdzog so/ /yul dbus kyi paN+Di ta A nan+ta b+ha dra dang bod kyi lo tsA ba se tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis grong khyer chen po ti ra ha te'i lho phyogs rang byung gi mchod rten rnam par dag pa'i drung du yul dbus kyi dpe dang mthun par bsgyur zhing bcos te gtan la phab pa/ /slar yang grub thob kar+Na shrI'i zhal snga nas gnas brtan nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyis shrI nA len dra'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o/
slob ma rjes su gzung ba lus ngag yid gsum byin gyis brlab pa'i man ngag slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /yul dbus kyi paN+Di ta A nan+da b+ha dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba se tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis grong khyer chen po ti ra ha te'i lho phyogs rang byung gi mchod rten rnam par dag pa'i drung du yul dbus kyi dpe dang mthun par bsgyur ci.inga bcos te gtan la phab pa'o/ /slar yang grub thob kar+Na shrI'i zhal snga nas mnyan te/ thar pa lo tsA ba gnas brtan nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyis shrI na lan+da'i gtsug lag khang chen por dag par bsgyur ba'o/
bcom ldan 'das gshin rje'i gshed kyi bskyed rdzogs zung du 'jug pa'i man ngag sems dpa' gsum gyi ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par gzhag pa zhes bya ba/ rdo rje phag mos dngos su byin gyis brlabs pa/ mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /yul dbus kyi paN+Di ta A nan+da b+ha dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba se tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis grong khyer chen po ti ra ha ti'i lho phyogs rang byung gi mchod rten rnam par dag pa'i drung du/ yul dbus kyi dpe dang mthun par bsgyur zhing bcos te gtan la phab pa'o//slar yang grub thob kar+Na shrI'i zhal snga nas mnyan te/ thar pa lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyis shrI na len+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang chen por dag par bsgyur ba'o/
bcom ldan 'das gshin rje tshe bdag nag po sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so/

khrus kyi cho ga sgrib pa sbyong zhing bar chad bsal ba rdzogs so/
dpal gshin rje tshe bdag nag po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dran pa gsal ba zhes bya ba/ dpal nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po nag po'i zhabs de nyid dang /lo tsA ba gnyan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta mngon shes can gyi phyag nas byung ba'o/ /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas dang / shes rab brtson 'grus kyis bsgyur ba'o/
tshul gsum bar byed pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba rdzogs so/

mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa mtshan don gsal bar byed pa'i sgron me zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad nas thugs kyi sras nyang ting nge 'dzin gyis zhus pa'o//gnyags dz+nyA nas bsgyur ba'o/
'grel pa rgyun gcod spu gri zhes bya ba dga' rab rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i nye bar bsdus pa rnam par rtog ge zhes bya ba mkhas pa chen po nges par sbyangs pa dpal gnyis su med pa'i rdo rje zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po shrI badz+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dpyal ser tsa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o/ /byang chung sems dapa'i rnam 'phrul gyis/ /gnas mchog sman lung gtsug lag khang / /rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i skal ldan mang / /de dag don du legs par bsgyur//
'jam dpal sgyu 'phrul dra ba khri drug stong pa ting 'dzin dra ba'i le'u las/ 'phags pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa phan yon dang bcas pa'i bshad pa/ nor bu'i gling du 'khrungs pa dpal ldan byang chub mchog gi skal pa can/ dpal sna tshogs gzungs kyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa/ sngags don rnam par gzigs pa dang / de'i rjes su 'brangs pa slob dpon chen po gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ nye bar bsdus pa'i rnam par rtog ge dang sbyar ba'i bsdus don mtshan gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /pradz+nyA gu rus mdzad do/
'phags pa 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ldan gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ /rnal 'byor pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nya na kirtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
'phags pa 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa' rin po che'i phyag rgya dri ma med pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ldan gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kirtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa snying po mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po dpal gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//rnal 'byor pa chen po pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du byas pa'o/
rang bzhin du gnas pa'i sngags kyi spyod pa bcu pa zhes bya ba dpal ldan gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
rmi lam brtag pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ldan gnyis su med pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
sangs rgyas kyi byang chub bsam gtan gyi dug sel ba'i mar me zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ldan gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i yid 'jug pa'i bsam gtan gyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ldan gnyis su med pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
thig le grub pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ldan gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
thig le gcig pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dpal ldan gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i snying po grub pa zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal ldan gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/
slob dpon chen po shrI mai tri'i gdams ngag nye bar bsdus pa rdzogs so/
dpal mai tri pas mdzad pa nye bar bsdus shing / zab cing rgya che ba'i 'grel pa/ mkhas pa chen po dril bu pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po many+dzu shrI sa twa dang / dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/
'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs zhi ba 'od kyi rim pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /sdom pa bzang po'i thugs dam/ lo tsA ba dar ma b+his bsgyur ba'o/
'jam dpal khro bo'i sgrub thabs rdo rje 'od kyi rim pa zhes bya ba/ bla ma sdom pa bzang po'i thugs dam/ bla ma lo tsA ba d+harmA b+his bsgyur ba'o/
rgyud kyi rgyal po 'jam dpal gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bla ma sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa rdzog so/
skyabs 'gro sems bskyed dbang bzhi'i gdams pa slob dpon sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
rdo rje glu'i gdams ngag rdzogs so/
phyi khrus nang khrus slob dpon sdom pa bzang po'i lugs 'bro lo tsA ba d+harmA b+his bsgyur ba rdzogs so/
gtor ma'i cho ga rdzogs so/
sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa 'bro lo tsA ba d+harmA b+his bsgyur ba ro'i rab gnas cho ga rdzogs so/
ro sreg pa'i cho ga slob dpon sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
sA ts+tsha gdab pa'i rim pa slob dpon sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga slob dpon sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
slob dpon sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa sbyin sreg gi cho ga rdzogs so/
mthun mong gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs kyi man ngag /slob dpon sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
bla ma'i maN+Dal yi dam gyi cho ga 'bro lo tsA bas bsgyur ba rdzogs so/
dpal bcom ldan 'das ral pa gcig pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ grub pa brnyes pa'i paN+Di ta chen po a dzi ta mi tra gup+tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po shrI dza ga ta mi tra A nan+da dang / de nyid kyi zhabs kyi pad+mo'i rdul spyi bos reg cing gsung gi bdud rtsi'i ro myong ba/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa dpal gyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
dpal bcom ldan 'das ral pa gcig pa'i man ngag khungs phyung ba/ slob dpon che po mi pham sbas pas bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug shrI mi tra dang / gnubs lo tsA ba mai tri shrIsa bsgyur ba'o/
dpal bcom ldan 'das ral pa gcig ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po rol pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug ma hA shrI dzA ga ta mi tra A nan+da rA dza dang gnubs lo tsA ba mai tri shrIsa bsgyur ba'o/
rgya gar gyi slob dpon chen po shrI badz+ra kIrti'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
dpal ral pa cig ma'i sgrub thabs 'khor lo gnod sbyin dang bcas pa rdzogs so/ /rje grub thob chen po'i thugs dam/ gnubs lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o/
rdo rje thogs pa'i bsngo ba nor bu'i sgron ma/ slob dpon mi pham zla bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta su b+ha shrI shAn+ti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o/
bcom ldan 'das dpal ral pa gcig pa la bstod pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po bud+d+ha shrI b+ha dra dang bod kyi lo chung gnubs byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
rnal 'byor pa rang gi sems ngal sos par byed pa'i man ngag tshigs su bcad pa nyi shu rtsa lnga pa zhes bya ba de kho na nyid rnal du mtshon par byed pa'i do ha rdzogs so/ /jo bo spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug las man ngag gi tshigs su bcad pa nyid dngos su gsan nas grub pa brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po shrI dza ga mi tra A nan+da dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis dpal gu lang gser khang gi nags khrod aM ba ra pa ra ta'i bsil khang du bsgyur ba'o/
rtogs pa brjod pa sum cu pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po mi tra dzo ki de nyid kyi spyan sngar gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o/
dpal 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sgrub thabs/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po shrI me tra'i gdams pa rdzogs so/ /gnubs lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o/
dpal gnod sbyin spun gnyis kyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon a dzi ta mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug mi tra A nan+da'i 'phrin las kyi lha'i rigs gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o/
dpal ldan rje btsun rigs kyi 'jig rten mgon po'i sgrub thabs kyi snang ba rje btsun ma hi mas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA d+ha ra dang / yar lungs pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis dpal ldan sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o/
'di ni rigs kyi 'jig rten mgon po'i lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa mdor bsdus pa ste/ kha che'i paN+Di ta dri med dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du mi chen lha rje ma ga ling gis zhus shing / yar lungs pa shud ke grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o/
ku la lo ka nA tha'i byin rlabs dang rjes gnang bya ba'i rim pa kha che'i paN+Di ta bi ma la shrI'i zhal snga nas bris pa rdzogs so// sangs rgyas lnga yi rnam dag pa'i/ /ma rig pa yi rim pa las/ /dbang bskur byed pa'i rim pa yis/ /ye shes lnga ni thob par 'gyur/ /zhes rdo rje phreng ba las gsung pas/ /ma rig pa lnga bsal nas rig pa ye shes lnga rtogs par byed pas na rig pa'i dbang ngo / lo tsA ba blo brtan gyis bsgyur ba'o///
rigs kyi 'jig rten dbang phyug bsgom pa'i rim pa paN+Di ta chen po bi ma la shrI'i zhal nas 'byung ba bzhin bris pa 'di rdzogs so//
ku la lo ka nA tha'i byin rlabs dang rjes gnang bya ba'i rim pa kha che'i paN+Di ta bi ma la shrI'i zhal snga nas bris pa rdzogs so//
lo tsA ba blo brtan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
rigs kyi 'jig rten dbang phyug sgrub pa'i thabs/ /slob dpon b+hring+gi ra bram zes mdzad pa 'jam dpl sgeg pas bsgyur pas bsgyur ba rdzogs//
dpal spyan ras gzigs yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs/ /gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o/
spyan ras gzigs kyi rgyud pad+ma zab pa dang pad+ma rgyal po'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba'i rab tu byed pa 'di/ dpal dzA lan+dA ra pas mdzad pa'o/ /mnga' bdag mai tri pa'i phyag dpe las/ rgya gar phyag na'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba pra dz+nyA kirtis bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
ma gcig grub pa'i rgyal mo nas brgyud pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi gsang ba'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/
bcom ldan 'das mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bzang po yongs bzung zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta zla ba bzang po dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba glan dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur zhing zhus te dag par byas so/
dpa' bo rta mgrin sgrub pa'i thabs/ /'od dpag med kyis lung bstan pa'i/ /mkha' 'gro grub pa'i rgyal mos brtsams/ /dge bas rta mchog sku thob shog /paN+Di ta zla ba bzang po dang glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing zhus te dge'o/
rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta zla ba bzang po dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba glan dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur ba'o/
sbyin sreg las kyi 'bras 'byin 'di/ /mkha' 'gro grub pa'i rgyal mos brtsams/ /dge ba 'di yis 'gro ba kun/ /tshe dpag med pa rnyed 'gyur shog/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po wa la tsan+d+ra bla ma dang / lo tsA ba glan dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur ba'o/
bcom ldan 'das tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma grub pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
bcom ldan 'das mgon po tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i dbang bzhi bskur ba'i cho ga'i las khrigs 'chi med ye shes bdud rtsi'i bum pa zhes bya ba/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma grub pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
drag po gsum 'dul zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyis 'grel pa bdud rtsi myu gu zhes bya ba/ dngos grub brnyes pa'i dzA pa ri pas sa ba ri ba la man ngag tu zhus pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / paN+Di ta de ba pu nya ma ti dang / lo tsA ba chos kyis bzang pos bsgrur ba'o/
slob dpon chen po dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs 'khor lo chen po zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de ba pur+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi gzungs kyi sgrub thabs bdud rtsi thigs pa zhes bya ba/ nam gru'i rigs las byung ba dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i mkhan po de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
dpal phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ nam gru'i rigs las byung ba/ dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon chen po dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i paN+Di ta de ba pur+Na ma ti dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
slob dpon dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa'i klu sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /bal po'i paN+Di ta de ba pur+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
gnod sbyin gyi sgrub pa'i thabs nam gru'i rigs las byung ba dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i mkhan po de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba ban de chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
nam gru'i rigs las byung ba'i slob dpon dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa'i bdud bzlog pa'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /bal po'i bla ma de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
dpal phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi gzungs kyi gtor ma'i cho ga zhes bya ba nam gru'i rigs las byung ba dngos grub brnyes pa/ slob dpon chen po bram ze'i btsun pa dzA pa ri pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba she'u badz+ra de bas bsgyur ba las/ slad kyis bdag dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bla ma la shin tu legs par zhus te/ phran bu tsho bcos pa lags so/
rim pa drug pa zhesa bya ba rtags gsal bar byed pa/ nam gru'i rigs las byung ba dngos grub brnyes pa dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de ba pu N+Ya ma ti dang chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
bsang ba gso ba'i cho ga rdzogs so/
phyag na rdo rje'i mchod pa'i rim pa rdzogs so/
slob dpon dzA ba ri pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i khro bos gsad pa'i phrin las paN+Di ta de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bcos pa'o/
klu rigs bzhi'i mnan pa nam gru'i rigs las byung ba'i slob dpon dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
dpal phyag na rdo rje'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga nam gru'i rigs las byung ba dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i paN+Di ta de ba pur+Na ma ti dang lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur zhing zhus so/
phyag na rdo rje'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba nam gru'i rigs las byung ba dngos sgrub brnyes pa'i slob dpon dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i paN+Di ta de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
dpal phyag na rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga nam gru'i rigs las byung ba'i dngos grub brnyes pa slob dpon dzA ba ri pa'i zhal nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i mkhan po paN+Di ta de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
mdze nad kyi mtshan nyid ces bya ba/ nam gru'i rigs las byung ba/ dngos grub brnyes pa dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i paN+Di ta de ba pUr+Ne dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur zhing gtan la phab pa'o/
gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can 'khor lo chen po'i lha tshogs la bstod pa zhes bya ba/ nam gru'i rigs las dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon dzA ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta chen po de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i bsrung ba zhes bya ba/ nam gru'i rigs las byung ba/ dngos grub brnyes pa dzA ba ri'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de ba pUr+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba she'u badz+ra de ba'i 'gyur/
slob dpon chen po 'phags pa phyag na rdo rje'i dngos grub brnyes pa de'i sku sprul nus pa phyag na rdo rjes mdzad pa rdo rje me lce'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa de kho na nyid snang ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po many+dzu shrI dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
slob dpon chen po phyag rgya'i dngos grub brnyes pa phyag na rdo rjes mdzad pa me lce'i phreng ba'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/
lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa'i man ngag rdzogs so/
slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs chen po rdzogs so/
gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa/
slob dpon chen po b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba tshul khrims gzhon nus bsgyur zhing gtan la phab pa/
rdo rje las kyi tshogs rim par phye ba'i cho ga/ slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba khu ba bIr+ya dang /dge slong gzhon nu tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa lags so/
sbyor ka chen po'i man ngag slob dpon chen po b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dge slong tshul khrims gzhon nus bsgyur ro//
slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims gzhon nus bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims gzhon nus bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o/
sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so
slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa'i maN+Dala gyi sbyor ka rdzogs so/
las kyi rim pa mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po rdo rje slob dpon bIr+ya gu pa su tra'i zhal snga dang / lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing zhus te/ dur khrod nags tshal du brgyud pa'i slob dpon la/ shin tu gsang zhing zhus ba'i don lags so/
rdo rje lce babs kyi 'grel pa mu tig gi phreng ba zhes bya ba'i rim pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po rgyal bu sprin gyi shugs can gyis mdzad pa'o/ /slad kyi paN+Di ta dza yA ka ra dang / lo tsA ba mar pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
rgyal po sprin gyi shugs can gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /slad kyi bla ma dza ya kA ra dang / mar pa lo tsA bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
lce dbab pa'i bya thabs rdzogs so/
rten 'brel gyi mthus bsrung ba rdzogs so/
phyag na rdo rje lce dbab kyi sngon du 'gro ba'i yan lag /rnal 'byor gyi spyod lam brgyad pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rgyal bu sprin gyi shugs can gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon rgyal bu sprin gyi shugs can gyis rgyud dang mi 'gal bar mdzad pa'o/ /dza yA ka ra dang /mar pa lo tsA bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
gsang ba'i bdag po lag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
phyag na rdo rje gtum po lha lnga pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
phyag na rdo rje'i lam yan lag brgyad pa zhes bya ba/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
rdo rje skor gyi nang sgrub yid bzhin gyi nor bu zhes bya ba/ phyag na rdo rje zhal mngon sum du gzigs pa/ slob dpon las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po wa la tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa'i gsang ba thugs kyi phur gcig ma'o/paN+Di ta wa la tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims kyis bsgyur ba'o//
rigs sngags bcad pa dang mnan pa'i cho ga'o/
slob dpon las kyis rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/
bya khyung sa ma ya tan+tra'i rgyud las btus pa/ lo tsA ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur ba'i klu gtor rgyas pa rdzogs so/
gtum chung khra thogs ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgyal po zla ba'i snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba sgeg pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o/
rdo rje khyung gi sgrub pa'i man ngag slob dpon rdo rje pad+mas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta sa'i snying po dang /lo tsA ba rma ban gyis bsgyur ba'o/
rdo rje gtum po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bzang po mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon las kyi rdo rje mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta zla ba bzang po dang / bod kyi lo tsA glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur ba'o/
'phags pa gos sngon po can gyi rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /skye ba lnga brgyar blo rab sbyangs/ /sngags kyi theg pa'i bstan bcos 'di/ /dbu ma'i lta bar yang dag ste/ /mkhas btsun rnams kyi yongs su gzung / /sgrol ma gsal ba zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa dge slong klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
rtog pa thams cad bsdus pa'i sgron ma/ slob dpon chen po shrI b+ha dras mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'phags pa lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi rgyud kyi rgya cher bshad pa/ slob dpon chen po mchog rab snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rgyud kyi rgyal po rdo rje be con gos sngon po can gyi rgyud/ /gu ya rU pa'i zhal snga nas ni legs bsgyur bas/ /mkha' 'gro'i gling nas dum bu brgyad du legs bris pa/ /de yi bshad rgyud 'bum phrag phyed dang sum stong las ni phyung ba yin/ /rtog pa drug pa'i rgyud rdzogs so//
de kho na nyid sgron ma zhes bya ba'i rgyan/ bla ma'i man ngag rgyun ma chad pa/ de kho na nyid nyi zla snang ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs chen po dge slong klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta gu ru pad+ma 'byung gnas dang / lo tsA ba glang dpal gyi seng ges bsgyur ro/ /slad kyis kyang paN+Di ta rgya gar phyogs nas sgra rang 'gyur du bsgyur ro/ /bi las badz+ra las bla ma sman btsun khros pa la gnang / des dngos la gnang pa lags so/
dpal ldan gos sngon can gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ slob dpon nA gA rdzu nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
sngags kyi rgyan nA gArdzu nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
dge slong nA gArdzu nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
gtor ma'i rgyan gyi man ngag dge slong klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
dam tshig gi rgyan rdzogs so//
dge slong klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
sngags kyi rgyan gyi 'grel pa/ mchog rab kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma dam pa'i man ngag snyan nas snyan du thob pa rdzos so/
dam tshig rgyan gyi 'grel pa mchog rab ma rdzogs so/ /zangs dkar tshul khrims gzhon nus bsgyur ba lags so/
klu'i byang chub kyi sgrub thabs kyi rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /slob dpon nA gArdzu na zhes kyang bya/ klub sgrub snying po zhes kyang bya/ klu yi byang chub zhes kyang bya/ klu sgrub snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
mchog rab snying po rtsa ba'i man ngag pad+ma 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa rdzogs so/

de kho na nyid sgron ma'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon dpa' bos byin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//

lha dang lha min la sogs pa ma lus pas/ zhabs kyi pad+ma zung la me tog gi phreng bas mchod pa dpal mgon po bde ba chen po pad+ma badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kriSh+Na paN+Di ta dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/
thabs dang shes rab rnam par gtan la dbab pa'i sgrub pa slob dpon chen po yan lag med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po shan+tI b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lha btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/
dpal u rgyan nas byung ba ye shes grub pa zhe ba ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mhan po shrad d+da ka ra warma dang/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur/ slad kyis nags tshos kyang bcos so/
gnyis su med par grub thabs zhes bya ba 'di ni u rgyan gyi che ba rnal 'byor gdan gyi sgrub pa'i lha'i gnas nas phyung ba bcom ldan 'das ma lak+ShI'i zhal snga nas byung ba rdzogs so/
dpal o rgyan nas byung ba gsang ba chen po de kho na nyid kyi man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon chen po dA ri ka pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
dngos po gsal ba'i rjes su grub ba de kho na nyid grub pa zhes bya ba/ lhan cig skyes pa'i rnal 'byor ma tsi tos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po zhi ba bzang po dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
dpal dgyes pa rdo rje'i rgyud kyi lhan cig skyes pa grub pa las/ lhan cig skyes pa bstan pa slob dpon chen po dpal DoM bi he ru kas zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dpal sa ra ha chen po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa do ha mdzod ces bya ba de kho na nyid rnal du mtshon pa don dam pa'i yi ge rdzogs so/
phyag rgya bzhi gtan la dbab pa slob dpon chen po klu sgrub snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma d+hi ri shrI dz+nyA na'i zhabs dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
shes rab ye shes gsal ba zhes bya ba/ mkhas pa chen po de ba tsan+d+ra'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba d+harma kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o/
gnas pa bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon chen po dpal ldan lhan cig skyes pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bla ma d+ha ri shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyis bsgyur ba'o/ /phyis bar ston gyis zhus nas bla ma rgya gar ba dang /mtshur lo tsA bas dpe phyi mo la gtugs te gtan la phab pa'o/
bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhes bya ba phyag rgya chen po thob pa'i slob dpon tog rtse zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bde ba'i myu gu dang 'gos kyis 'gyur ro/
slob dpon mkhas pa chen po nges par sbyangs pa/ gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa lta ba ngan pa sel ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma badz+ra pA Ni'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mtshur ston ye shes 'byung gnas kyis bsgyur ba'o/
dbu ma drug pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mkhas pa mai tris mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma badz+ra pA Ni dang / nag 'tshos bsgyur ba'o/
lta ba ngan pa sel ba'i dka' 'grel dpal ldan nges par sbyangs pa gnyis su med pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /badz+ra pA Ni dang mtshur gyis bsgyur ba yin no/
lhan cig skyes pa drug pa bla ma mai tri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma badz+ra pA ni dang mtshur gyis bsgyur ba'o/
rmi lam nges par bstan pa/ slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma badz+ra pA Ni dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/
sgyu ma nges par bstan pa slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/
rab tu mi gnas pa gsal bar ston pa/ slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /badz+ra pA Ni dang / nag tshos bsgyur ba'o/
de kho na nyid bcu pa/ slob dpon gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma phyag na dang / mtshur gyis bsgyur ba'o/ /phyis lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ro/
zung du 'jug pa rab tu gsal ba bstan pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon a ba d+hU tis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /badz+ra pA Ni dang / nags tshos bsgyur ba'o/
dga' gcugs lnga pa/ slob dpon mai tri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma phyag na'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba rma ban gyis bsgyur ba'o/
mi phyed pa lnga pa slob dpon mai tri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba rma ban gyis bsgyur ba'o/
bde ba chen po gsal ba slob dpon a ba d+hU ti pa dpal gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma badz+ra pA Ni dang / rma ban gyis bsgyur ba'o/
de kho na nyid rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon a ba d+hU ti pa gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /nags tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/
de kho na nyid rab tu bstan pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/
de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i phyag rgya rnam par bshad pa slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po phyag na rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyis bsgyur ba'o/
dbang gi dgos pa mdor bsdus pa mkhas pa chen po nges par sbyangs pa gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma badz+ra pA Ni'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba mtshur ston gyis bsgyur ba'o/
dbang gi cho ga mdor bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /dpal gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa'o/
'di ni rdo rje sems dpa'i rang bzhin lnga pa/ dpal gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /a mri de bas zhus te gsol ba btab nas brtsams/
thabs dang she rab brtse ba lnga pa slob dpon a ba d+hU tI pa gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjesa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po badz+ra pA Ni dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mtshur dz+nyA na A ka ras bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
do hA ti zhes bya de kho na nyid kyi man ngag rdzogs so/ /a ba d+hU ti pas mdzad pa/ rje btsun d+hi ri shrI dz+nyA nas bsgyur ba'o/
theg pa chen po nyi shu pa slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /pa ri pa ta pradz+nyA sha ra sa ma d+h+ya na/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po de bA ka ra tsan+d+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya brtson 'grus kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la dbab pa'o/
yid la mi byed pa ston pa bdag med pa gsal ba slob dpon chen po gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po badz+ra pA Ni dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba gnyan chung gis bcos pa rdzogs so/
a ba d+hU tI pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rje btsun d+hi ri shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba seng kar shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o/

dbang bskur ba nges par bstan pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rgyal ba mai tri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kriSh+Na paN+Di ta dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur/
dbang bskur ba nges par bstan pa'i bka' 'grel/ slob dpon dga' ba skyong gis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /sa man+ta b+ha dra dang / nag tshos bsgyur ba'o/
de kho na nyid bcu pa'i rgya cher bshad pa paN+Di ta chen po slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po badz+ra pA Ni las mnyan te/ slad kyi paN+Di ta kA l+ya warma dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong dz+nyA na A kA ra mtshur gyis bsgyur ba'o/
rdo rje slob dpon badz+ra pA Ni'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ rdo rje'i tshig rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba mtshur ston dge slong dz+nyA na A ka ras bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
do ha mdzod kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon chen po dpal gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar lho phyogs yul ko sa lar sku 'khrungs pa'i rnal 'byor pa chen po shrI bai ro tsa na badz+ras bsgyur ba'o/
mi zad pa'i gter mdzod yongs su gang ba'i glu zhes bya ba'i rgya cher bshad pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyung chen po dpal sa ra ha pa'i dgongs pa mkhas par grags pa dpal ldan gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
