'dzag pa gcod pa'i man ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon ku ku ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mu stegs kyi gtum mo zhes bya ba/ slob dpon a tsin+tas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gser 'gyur rtsi'i gdams pa/ slob dpon na lis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sems dang sems nyid 'dul ba'i man ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon shAn+ta de ba nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon me ko las gsungs pa rdzogs so//
lha kun gyi rdzogs pa'i rim pa/ g+ha d+ha ris mdzad pa rdzogs so//
nyi zla bcing ba'i thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon bi rU pa nas brgyud pa/ ka ma ris mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sems nyid kyi thig le'i hUM nyid bsgom pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dzA lan+d+ha ris mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshad med bzhi bsam gyis mi khyab pa sgom pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rA hu las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
hUM yig sems nyid thig le bsgom pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon nag po pa nas brgyud pa'i slob dpon d+harma pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rang bzhin grub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rdo ka ris mdzad pa rdzogs so//
lhan skyes zung 'jug gi gdams pa/ slob dpon me d+hi nis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bla med sbyor pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon bAng+ga dzas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
A li kA li'i rnal 'byor zhes bya ba/ slob dpon g+han+d+has mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ka phreng bsgom pa'i lam zhes bya ba/ slob dpon d+ha ma d+hu mas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
a phreng ka phreng bde mchog 'khor lo'i rnal 'byor chen po bsgom pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon sA ga ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rlung gnas nad kyi brtag pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon a dzo kis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sems nyid kyi de nyid bcing ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ko d+ha les mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gtum mo thig le bkram pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon lu rtsi kis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
lus kyi rtsa thig mnyam pa nyid kyi man ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon ni ku nis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'byung ba bzhi'i srid pa'i cha lugs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon tsa ra pa tris mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rang rig ye shes kyi nyams len zhes bya ba/ slob dpon tsam+pa kas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'jigs pa brgyad rmongs par byed pa'i thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon b+hi Sha nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
phyi nang nad sel gyi gdams pa/ slob dpon ti los mdzad pa rdzogs so//
g.yung drung 'khyil pa gsum gyi zhal gdams/ yum kang+ka la me ka las gsungs pa rdzogs so//
lhan cig skyes pa'i rang bzhin zhes bya ba/ slob dpon kan+tha ris mdzad pa rdzogs so//
a ti rnal 'byor gyi bsgom pa'i man ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
byang chub sems kyi rlung rgyu ba'i man ngag bsgom pa zhes bya ba slob dpon su tai lis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
lta spyod skye med kyi sgom pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon pa na has mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshe sgrub pa'i gdams ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon ko ki las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dug sel bsgom pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba slob dpon a rang gis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gnyis med kyi rtsa bsgom pa zhes bya ba slob dpon nag po nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon ni la khan d+has mdzad pa rdzogso//
phra ba'i rnal 'byor gyi nyams les zhes bya ba/ slob dpon sa mu dras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon b+h+ya ris gsungs pa'i phyin nang gi bdud rtsi'i bcud len gyi gdams pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta rat+na pha las rang 'gyur du mdzad nas/ bshad rgyud kyi gdams pa bar ma chad par gsungs s'o//
do ha spyod pa'i glu'i lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon lU yi pa nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon ki ra pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
stong pa nyid kyi lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon sha ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bde sdug gnyis bral gyi lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon shAn+ti pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon kaM pa la'i 'brel med kyi lta ba 'di/ rnal 'byor rtogs tshad kyi lta ba rdzogs so/ /bla ma rat+na pha las rang 'gyur du bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon kaM pa las mdzad pa/ zhen med kyi lta ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
stong nyid snying rje'i lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ar+ya de ba nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon tsa ta pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sems nyid rin chen gyi lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ka na pa nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon d+he ta nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
de nyid brgyad kyi lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon in d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
sems nyid kyi rtogs pa 'joms pa'i lta ba zhes bya ba/ kaM ka la dang / me kha la nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon lak+Sha mI yis gsungs pa rdzogs so//
mya ngan gyi lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ma hi la nas brgyud pa/ d+ha'u ris mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sems tsam gyi lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon sa ra ha nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon mai tri pas gsungs pa rdzogs so//
snying rje thod pa spyod pa'i lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon d+ha ri ka pa nas brgyud pa/ slob dpon sa ra b+ha khas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ 'brel med kyi lta ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
de bzhin nyid kyi lta ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dA ri ka pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sangs rgyas gnyis pa ltar grags pa/ bla ma rgya gar nag gu'i zhal snga nas/ bod kyi ban+de zha ma lo tsA bas byin rlabs kyi gnas mchog ding rir bsgyur te/ bla ma byang chub sems dpa' kun dga' la gtad pa rdzogs so//
phyag rgya chen po'i man ngag rdo rje gsang ba'i mgur zhes bya ba/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal sa ra ha'i zhal nas gsungs pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la shI la dang / bod kyi ban+de lo tsA ba zha ma ston pa seng ge rgyal pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
makha' 'gro ma brda'i mgur chung/ gsang mdzad 'phrul gyi rgya/ khyad par du brgyud pa/ zha ma lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
mkha' 'gro ma'i brda bam po lnga pa zhes bya ba/ gsang mdzod na shog dril du gnas pa las/ dbyings kyi gtso mo rnams kyis bka' bgros nas/ rje dam pa rgya gar la gnang / slad kyis ding ri glang 'khor du/ zha ma lo tsA bas bsgyur nas/ bla ma byang chub sems dpa' kun dga' la gtad/ 'di khyad par gyi brgyud pa chen po brgyad las/ brda skor rnam pa bzhi rdzogs so//
thig le dag pa'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ grub thob pho mo brgyad bcu'i rtogs pa brjod pa/ mkha' 'gro mas yi ger btab ste/ gsang mdzod na gnas pa las/ dbyings kyi gtso mo rnams kyis bka' bgros nas/ rje dam pa rgya gar la gnang ba/ zha ma lo tsA bas legs par bsgyur ba'o//
grub thob lnga bcu'i rtogs pa brjod pa thig le 'od kyi phreng ba zhes bya ba/ mkha' 'gro ma'i gsang mdzod nas phyung ste/ rje dam pa rgya gar rin po che la gnang ba/ zha ma lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
le phran lnga bcu rtsa lnga pa/ phyag rgya chen po rin po che brda'i man ngag /rje dam pa la mkha' 'gro mas gtad de zha ma lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
mkha' 'gro ma'i gsang mdzod na gnas pa las/ dbyings kyi gtso mo rnams kyis bka' bgros nas/ ka ma la shI la la gtad/ zha ma lo tsA ba ston pa seng ge rgyal pos bsgyur ba'o//
rngon pa chen pos ka ma la shI la la gnad kyi gdams pa bstan pa'o//
zab mo brda'i glu gsang ba'i bdud rtsi zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /sha ba ri dbang phyug gis dam pa la gsungs pa/ dam pa'i zhal snga nas zha ma lo tsA bas gtan la phab ste/ dpal ding ri mkhan pa'i khrod du bsgyur ba'o//
dpal u rgyan du tshogs 'khor byas pa'i dus su rdo rje'i mgur bzhengs pa/ nyams kyi man ngag /thig le gser gyi phreng ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma sum cu rtsa lnga'i rtogs par brjod pa/ mkha' 'gro ma'i gsang mdzod na gnas pa las/ dbyings kyi gtso mo rnams kyis bka' bgros nas/ rje dam pa rgya gar la gnang ba zha ma lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
mkha' 'gro ma'i 'byam glu ring mo zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
bcom ldan 'das bdag med ma'i brda rin po che dbang gi 'khor lo zhes bya ba/ dur khrod rgyu skar dpal gyi rol par gsungs pa rdzogs so//
rgyal sras mi'i seng+ge rje dam pa rgya gar rin po che'i zhal snga nas/ rang 'gyur du mdzad pa/ phyag rgya chen po dum bu khrigs/ /tshigs tu nyung la don du 'gril/ /nyams myong skyes pa rdo rje'i mgur/ /ma rig mun sel sgron me 'di/ /skal ldan mig gi dbang po yis/ /lta bas mi ngoms blos mi 'khyud/ /sgro 'dogs glags pa tsam gyis chod/ /e ma ngo re mtshar rdzogs so//
phyag rgya chen po do rje'i glu/ rin po che gser phreng zhes bya ba/ grub pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor pa dang/ paN+Di ta mang pos gsungs pa rnams/ rje btsun mnga' bdag mai tri pas/ gzhung gcig tu bsdebs pa'i gdams pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
shes rab kyi 'phrin yig slob dpon chen po pad+ma rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po shAn+ta b+ha dra dang / bod kyi zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rnal 'byor pa'i rtogs pa'i gegs sel ba zhes bya ba/ dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon mkhas pa chen po sangs rgyas gsang pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dug lnga sbas pa'i mchog tu gsang pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rnal 'byor gyi mtshan nyid bden pa/ mkhas pa chen po dpal byang chub bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
shes rab brtsam pa dus kyi gtam zhes bya ba/ b+hang+ga la'i mkhas pa dpal nges par sbyangs pa dpal ldan gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes bram ze b+ha lo la gdams pa rdzogs so//
ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs kyi le'u/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'jig rten las 'das pa'i yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis/ dpal bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang chen por mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa rin po che'i gru bo zhes bya ba/ grub pa brnyes pa'i paN+Di ta chen po a dzi ta mi tra gup+tas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal 'ching ba rnam grol gyi bstan bcos/ rgya gar gyi slob dpon chen po grub pa brnyes pa'i dpal ni ska lang+kas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po shrI dza ga ta mi trA nan+da'i zhal snga nas/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po bud d+hA shrI b+ha dras gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo chung gnubs tshul khrims shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
lta spyod rnam dag gi man ngag ces bya ba kha che'i rigs kyi paN+Di ta chen po dpal chos kyi rje shAkya shrI b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mkhas pa chen po de nyid kyi spyan sngar lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis khro phu bzang lung du bsgyur ba'o//
kha che'i rigs las bal yul du sku 'khrungs pa'i paN+Di ta chen po dpal lnga rig pa'i mchogs bud d+ha shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas gsungs pa/ sems rin po che sbyang ba'i lam 'bras zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /mkhas pa chen po de nyid kyi spyan snga lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bal yul yam 'gal gyi gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
'ching ba rnam grol gyi man ngag ces bya ba rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug shrI dza ga ta mi tra A nan+da'i zhal snga nas gsungs pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug de nyid kyi spyan sngar lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bal yul gu lang gser khang du bsgyur ba'o//

rang gi sems kyi mdud pa 'grol ba'i gdams pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma mi tra A nan+da zhes bya ba sbas pa'i sangs rgyas de nyid bod yul kha ba can gyi mthil bkra shis kyi tshong 'dus chen po 'gur mo rin po che'i gling du byon pa'i tshe mdo sngags kyi bdag po chen po/ rgya 'bre/ lam/ lo/ dro/ gshen drug gis zhus pa'i don du gsungs pa/ phyag rgya chen po chig chod kyi do ha gnubs lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
dpal rnal 'byor rnam pa bdun gyi lam rnam par nges pa/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug chen po shrI dza ga ta mi tra a nan+da'i thugs kyi 'khor lo dam pa/ bkra shis kyi tshong dus chen po dpal mgur mo rin po che'i gling du/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po/ rgya/'bre/lam/lo/dro/ gshen/ drug gi don du mdzad pa'i bstan bcos/ de kho na nyid rnal du mtshon pa'i man ngag rdzogs so//
ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bskur rdzogs so/ /gnubs lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
pha rol dbang du bya ba gnubs lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
rin chen 'khor lo'i dbang gi man ngag gi rim pa/ slob dpon in+d+ra b+hu ti'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dbang gi rim pa bstan pa rje btsun klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ga ya d+ha ra'i zhal snga nas dang/ bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong ye shes bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
dbang gi don bsdus pa slob dpon dpal shes rab gsang ba'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//

dbang bskur ba'i nges par bstan pa/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
dbang gi don nges par brjod pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rgyal ba bzang po dpal sbas pa zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ru lag rgyang gi gtsug lag khang du rgya gar gyi mkhan po a ba d+hU tI pa'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya brtson 'grus kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rdo rje theg pa'i rtsa ba'i ltung ba bsdus pa slob dpon chen po rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ltung ba sbom po bsdus pa/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ltung ba bco lnga pa rdzogs so//
yan lag gi nyes pa bdun pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje theg pa'i sbom po'i ltung ba/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra barma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ /slad kyis rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma rje btsun paN+Di ta chen po ma Ni ka shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas dang / chag lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong chos rje dpal gyis zhus te dag par bgyis so//
yan lag gi dam tshig ces bya ba rdzogs so//
rdo rje theg pa'i ltung ba'i snye ma zhes bya ba mkhas pa chen po a b+h+yA ka ra gup+tasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ma ga d+hA'i mkhas pa chen po de nyid dang / mang du thos pa'i dge slong bsod snyoms pa sangs rgyas grags pas/ nA len d+rar bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon chen po dpal lak+Sh+mI ka ra'i zhal nas mdzad pa/ rtsa ba'i ltung ba bcu bzhi pa'i 'grel pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon chen po snying po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon b+ha bi pa'i gdams ngag mngon par bkod pa rdzogs so//
gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi bslab pa gsal bar byed pa'i man ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon rgyal ba'i lhas mdzad pa'i rtsa ba'i ltung ba'i 'grel pa/ mkhas pa chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas gsungs pa rdzogs so/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje theg pa'i rtsa ba'i ltung ba'i rgya cher 'grel pa lam gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba de la phan par byed pa'i yan lag dang bcas pa/ slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /myang ro stag tshal du dI paM ka ra bod du byon tsam na bsgyur/ pu ri sha'i grong khyer du a tsar+ya u pa d+ha shrI badz+ra shI la dang / lo tsA ba dge slong brtson 'grus seng ges legs par mnos te gus par bsgyur ba'o/ /bal po'i khyim du du ma'i lo/ /rin chen grags pa bdag gis 'ongs/ /'grel dpe rnying pa la yang btugs/ /shin tu yang ni dag par bgyis//
lam thams cad kyi dag byed kyi thabs dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i yi ge brgya pa'i sgrub thabs/ bla ma mngon shes can rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /yul dbus kyi dpe ji lta ba bzhin lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos gtsug lags khang chen po dpal thar pa gling du gus pas bsgyur ba'o//
gsang ba thams cad kyi spyi'i cho ga'i snying po rgyan zhes bya ba/ slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i mkhan po ka na ka shrI dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/ /slad kyis rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta ha s+ya badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong nyi ma rdo rjes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
ma hA paN+Di ta a b+h+ya ka ra gup+tasa mdzad pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /ma hA paN+Di ta shrI rat+na rak+Shi ta'i zhal snga nas so//
tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i mchod pa'i cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kriSh+Na pa de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
paN+Di ta bzang po sbyin pas tshogs kyi 'khor lo mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAkya shrI b+ha drA dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
tshog kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta pa'i zhal snga nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa grub pa dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga rim par phye ba zhes bya ba/ A tsaR+ya he ru ka bdz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta'i zhal snga nas lo tsA ba grub pa dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
sku dang gsung dang thugs rab tu gnas pa zhes bya ba/ dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra dang / lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng ges bi kra ma shI lar bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gdugs la sogs pa rab tu gnas pa dang rnying pa 'byin pa'i cho ga 'di'i rgya dpe gnyal gyi phyogs nas rnyed do/ /bstan pa rin po che la phul du byung ba'i gces spras su mdzad pa mtshungs med chos kyi rje rin po che zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa bzhi pa'i zhal snga nas bsgyur cig ces bka' bstsal pa bzhin zha lu lo tsA ba dge slong chos skyong bzang pos dpal sne'u gdong rtser bsgyur ba'o//

dbyig gi phreng ba zhes bya ba cho ga'i bya ba bcu pa rdzogs so/ /gzhung 'di lha dang bcas pa'i skye dgu'i 'dren pa dma pa chos kyi rje sprul sku rin po che'i zhal snga nas kyi bka' lung bzhin/ lo tsA ba dge slong chos skyong bzang pos sa skyong ba mkhyen pa'i spyan ldan dbon chen kun dga' bsod nams rin chen dbang gi rgyal po'i bdag rkyen las dpal e waM chos 'khor du bsgyur ba'o//
'dod pa'i bstan bcos mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon gzugs bzang gis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa de kho na nyid bsdus pa las/ rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen por gsungs pa'i ye shes sems dpa' mnyes par bya ba'i cho ga bsdus pa ste/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'jam dpal go chas bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen por gsungs pa'i ye shes sems dpa' mnyes par bya ba'i cho ga rgyud don la 'jug pa'i tshig gi don la rnam par dbye ba slob dpon pad+ma badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//


de kho na nyid bsdus pa'i rgya cher bshad pa ko sa la'i rgyan mang du thos pa'i slob dpon chen po shAkya bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po dharmA shrI bha dra dang zhu chen gyi lo tsa ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rnam par gzhag pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mu ti ta ko Shas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra barma dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dkyil 'khor gyi thig gi cho ga mdor bsdus pa slob dpon shrad+ha kA ra barmas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pra ta ka ra barma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos skad gsar chad kyi zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
yul kha cher skyes pa'i rdo rje slob spon shrad d+ha ka ra barmasa rang nyid kyis mdzad pa'i thig gdab pa'i cho ga'i 'grel pa/ bod yul du skyes pa'i dge slong rin chen bzang pos gsol ba btab nas 'grel pa byes pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrad d+ha ka ra barma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos skad gsar chad kyi zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
thig gdab pa'i rim pa dka' ba gcod pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon shud+d+hi pra b+has mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon d+harma kIrtis mdzad pa thig gi cho ga rdzogs so//
'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i 'grel pa mu ti ta ko Shas byas pa rdzogs so//

'jig rten gsum gyi 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'grel pa rdzogs so//


mchog dang po las shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dum bu'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra barma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cingzhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsAr+ya shra d+d+ha ka rabarma dang / ka ma la dup+ta dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa nam mkha'i snying po'i rtog pa'i bshad pa rdzogs so//

dpalmchog dang po'i rgya cher bshad pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogso//
rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgya cher bshad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon mkhas pa chen po kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgyud kyi rgyal po sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i dka' 'grel / slob dpon rab tu zhi ba'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rdo rje snying po'i rgyan gyi rgyud kyi dka' 'grel/ slob dpon rab tu zhi ba'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyi rgya dpe la bltas nas bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen po'i cho ga rdo rje thams cad 'byung ba zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po kun dga' snying po'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bdag gis sgrub thabs legs bsgyur ba/ bsgyur bas bsod nams gang thob pa/ de yis 'jigs rten ma lus 'dir/ dpal ldan rdo rje 'byung 'grub shog / rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsar+ya bud+ha shrI shAn+ti dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa'i rdo rje sems dpa' 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po kun dga' snying po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /'di'i gzhung tshad rgya phrag gnyis dang / rkang pa gcig dang cas pa yin no/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su bud+d+ha shrI shAn+ti dang / lo tsA ba rma dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa'i dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su bud+d+ha shrI dang / lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//


spyan dbye ba'i cho ga slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
spyan dbye ba'i cho ga slob dpon prany+dzA ba li tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI ba dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+d+he rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
thugs rje 'byung ba zhes bya ba sgom pa dang bzlas pa'i cho ga slob dpon chen po ye shes rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrad+d+ha ka ra varma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slon rin chen bzang pos bcos shing bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
sbyin sreg gi cho ga rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi makha po shrad+d+ha ka ra varma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal ldan rgya che ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdzogs so//
kun tu bzang po'i zhes bya ba'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga rdzogs so//
rnal 'byor gyi rgyud kyi rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga/ rab gnas kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
'phags pa de kho na nyid bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdo rje 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i bsdus pa'i don A tsar+ya mu nI na b+ha dras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /A tsar+ya mu nIna dra b+ha dra dang bod kyi lo tsA ba che ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rdo rje dbying kyi dkyil 'khor gyi don bsgom pa'i don bsdu pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mA ra ka la sha'i zhal snga nas bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
ces pa ni paN+Di ta chen po niH saM ga A tsar+ya dpal ldan rigs kyis byin pas mdzad pa bya ba bsdus pa'i piny+dza kA las rab tu byed pa brgyud pa rdzogs so/ / bla ma paN+Di ta chen po kIrti tsan+d+ra'i zhal snga nas zhus shing gzhung sum gnyis bal po'i mi thil du bsgyur zhing / sum cha gcig dus 'khor ba chen po shes rab seng ges bskul zhing sbyin bdag mdzad pa la brten nas/ shAkya'i dge slong yar lungs pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis yos lo dpo'i zla ba'i/ dkar po'i phyogs kyi chos brgyad la gzhu'i kun dga' ra ba'i gtsug lag khang chen por yongs su rdzogs par bsgyur nas bris so//

mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon chen po 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi zhal snga nas kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrad+d+ha ka ra varma dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa mtshan gsang sngag kyi don du rnam par lta ba zhes bya ba rgya gar gyi mkhan po sgeg pa'i rdo rje nyi ma can gyi rin po che gling na bzhugs pa dpal ldan byang chub mchog gi skal pa dang ldan pa gang gi mtshan dpal sna tshogs gzugs can du grags pa des mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur te bshad pa gtan la phab pa'o/ phyi rgya gar gyi mkhan po phyag na rdo rje dang / klog kya shes rab brtsegs kyis bcos nas gtan la phab pa'o/ 'di la gzhung tshad sh+lau ka nyi stong lnga brgya'o/ phyis gnyan gyis bcos pa'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon chen po 'jam dpal grags pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsar+ya shrad+d+ha ka ra varma dang / ka ma la gup+ta dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing shus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon chen po zla ba bzang po grags pa'i dpal gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po shrI ma hA dza na dang / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po dge slong 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi 'grel pa bsdus pa'i gsal ba/ o rgyan gyi slob dpon chen po a ba d+hU tI pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI mi tra dang / bod gyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos mdzad kyi sgom pa ye shes grags pa'i don du bsgyur ba'o/
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa/ mtshan don gsal bar byed pa zhes bya pa/ slob dpon chen po gnyis su med pa'i sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA shrI mi tra dang / bod kyi dge slong chos kyi bzang pos u rgyan gyi dzam bu d+ha ra zhes bya ba'i mthar bsgyur ba'o//
'jam dpal mtshan brjod kyi 'bum paN+Di ta smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid kyis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i man ngag gi 'grel pa zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po gzhon nu grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de ba rA dza dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba shes rab bla mas bsgyur ba'o/
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon chen po dbu ma dga' bas mdzad pa rdzogs so// zhwa lu ba dge slong chos skyong bzang po skad gnyis smra bas rgya dpe lsd tshig don khong du chud par byas te bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi dka' 'grel rat+na A ka ra gup+tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kA la tsakra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / 'brog jo sras dang / chos kyi brtson 'grus la sogs pas bsgyur ba'o//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon chen po phyag rgya chen po dngos grub bsnyes pa Dom+b+hi he ru ka'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /sa pho spre'u dpyid zla tha chung yar gyi ngo chos bco lnga la/ gza' mig dmar gyi nyin par dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal/ lha btsan po khri dbang phyug rin po che don thams cad sgrub pa'i bka' lung gis/ rgyal mo sum bu bra lun gyis 'do zer gyi sku gnyer mdzad nas/ bkra shis kyis gdan sa chen po tsong kha ser to bla mkhar gyi nang du bod kyi lo tsA ba khyung grags kyis 'jam dpal sgyu 'phrul dra ba bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//

mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i dkyil 'khor cho ga nam mkha'i dri med ces bya ba/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su b+ha dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chaso kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/
slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
byang sems rdo rje dbugs dbyug ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/
slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ rnam par snang mdzad dbugs dbyung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdzogs so/
mi bskyod pa dbugs dbyung pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ slob dpon chen po 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/
snang ba mtha' yas dbugs dbyung pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ slob dpon chen po 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/
slob dpon chen po 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa/ rin chen 'byung ldan dbugs dbyung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdzogs so//
don yod grub pa dbugs dbyung pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ slob dpon chen po 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i khrus kyi cho ga slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i chu sbyin slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i zas kyi rnal 'byor slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'byung po'i gtor ma slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i maN+Dala gyi cho ga slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i bskor ba bya ba'i thabs slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i yon lag bdun pas tshogs bsags pa'i thabs/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'jam dpal gyi mtshan brjod gdon pa'i man ngag slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba sngo ba/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i mi rtag pa bsgom pa slob dpon dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i mi rtag pa 'khor ba las yid byung ba/ slob dpon dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i shes pa dug gsum las bzlog pa'i man ngag slob dpon dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
skyabs su 'gro ba'i cho ga rdzogs so//
sems bskyed pa'i cho ga slob dpon dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa'i man ngag slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
tshad med pa bzhi bsgom pa'i man ngag rdzogs so/
dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas la blta ba rdzogs so//
slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa'i mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rjes su dran pa drug bsgom pa'i man ngag rdzogs so//
slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i sgo nas brten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i yan lag bcu gnyis bsgom pa'i man ngag rdzogs so//
dbang po rab kyis de kho na nyid bsgom pa slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/
slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i tsha tsha'i cho ga rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga bsdus pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i mnyam par gzhag pa'i rim pa'i man ngag rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i cho ga mdo don mdor bsgyur pa'i cho ga sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud le'u khri drug stong las rdo rje glur blangs pa'i le'u yi sgrub thabs mdo dang bsras pa/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyis mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i ngan sngags byad kyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i tshe 'phos pa la phan pa'i bdun tshigs kyi cho ga slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi bsgyur ba'o rdzogs so//
slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i 'jam dpal gyi ro (ma) sreg gi cho ga /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyis shes rab kyis bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
tshe las 'das pa'i sgrib pa sbyong pa'i cho ga/ 'gro ba rigs drug nas gdon pa dang /dkyil 'khor drug tu gzhug cing dbang bskur ba dang / lam bstan cing smon lam gdam pa/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa don bcu gnyis bstan pa lung gi rjes su 'brangs ba'i sing+ga gling gi slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i tshigs bcad bzhi bcu pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i gsang ba dang ldan pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po dpal ldan byang chub mchog gis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa bklag pa'i sgom khog /slob dpon dpal ldan byang chub mchog gis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rim pa gnyis kyis phye ba'i sbyin sreg cho ga rgyas pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon chen po rin chen gling ga gnas pa dpal ldan byang chub mchog gis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gi mkhan po smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga yon tan 'byung gnas zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dpal ldan byang chub mchog gi skal pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba/ gzhan yang skye ba gcig la mtshan lnga thob pa'i slob dpon de'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyis mkhan po smri ti dz+nyA kIrtisa bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o/ phyis slob dpon 'phags pa mchog gis kyang zhus nas gtan la phab te/ 'gyur phyi ma yang yin no//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga 'di/ bdag gi rang bzor byas min te/ sgyur 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud las 'ongs/ kun gyis 'jam dbyangs thob par shog /slob dpon shAn+ti gar+b+has mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i gsang ba dang ldan pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs kyi 'grel ba ye shes gsal ba zhes bya ba/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sgrub thabs gsang ba dang ldan pa'i thig gi cho ga /paN+Di ta smri ti dz+nyA kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga /paN+Di ta smri tis bsdebs nas sgra rang 'gyur du mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dge bsnyen ma snyan grags dge mas mdzad pa/ /'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal rin po che'i sgrub thabs/ dge bsnyen ma grags sbyin mas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /smri ti dz+nya na kIrtisa bsgyur pa dzogs so//
'di ni dril bu mtshan nyid do/ nam mkha' dri med dkyil 'khor legs bris pa'i/ rnam par dkar ba'i dge ba gang yin des/ 'gro kun lta ngan sprin tshogs rnams gsal te/ phyogs rnams kun tu nyi zla ltar gyur cig /
sems can thams cad la bde ba bskyed pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdzogs so//
rdzogs so/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad do/
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i cho ga mdo'i don mdor bsdus pa'i cho ga / slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud le'u drug stong pa las/ rdo rje glu gar blangs pa'i le'u'i sgrub thabs mdo dang bsres pa rdzogs so//
gsang ba'i bka' 'grel bshad pa don bsdus sgron ma rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de wA ka ra tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba klog skyas bsgyur ba'o//
gsang ldan gyi tho yig /paN+Di ta smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga /paN+Di ta shAn+ti gar+b+hasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i sgrub thabs gsang ba'i sgron ma/ slob dpon chen po pradz+nyA gu rus mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'khor lo'i rim pa/ bla ma dam pa'i cho ga chen po'i gzhung rnams las/ blo zhan pa'i don du mos pa tsam las 'jug pa 'di dag gi rim pa phra mo rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal rigs bsdus pa dang / phye ba'i cho ga yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba/ slob dpon zla bzangs grags pas mdzad pa/ kha phyi'i mkhan po paN+Di ta ma hA dzA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims gzhan nus bsgyur te gtan la phab pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub thabs/ u rgyan gyi slob dpon shrI a wa d+hu tI pa chen pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA shrI mi tra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga ye shes gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon gnyis med sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
de kho na nyid ces bya ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon gnyis su med pa sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta d+harma shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sbyin sreg slob dpon mya ngan med pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon a wa d+hu tis mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /d+harmA shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
a ba d+hu tis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs mya ngan med pa'i dpal gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a shwa shrI ri / lo tsA ba 'a zha rgya gar brtsegs gyis bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon a sho ka shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta d+harma shrI mi tra dang lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
gshin rje'i gshed kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon a sho ka shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta d+harmA shrI mi tra dang lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
mi g.yo ba'i bsgrub thabs/ /slob dpon a sho ka shrI mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta d+harmA shrI ma ti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
'jam pa'i mgon po'i gtor ma'i cho ga zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po a shwa ka shrI mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /shAkya dge slong chos kyi bzang pos gro mo d+ha ra dang nye ba'i rtsar zhus te bsgyur ba'o//
dpal 'jam pa'i mgon po'i bum pa'i cho ga slob dpon chen po mya ngan med pa'i dpal gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal u rgyan gyi mkhan po chen po d+harmA shrI mi tra'i zhal snga nas dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba bod kyi shAkya'i dge slong dpal gyis bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon gnyis su med pa'i sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon mi g.yo seng+gesa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mar pa do pas bsgyur ba'o//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i sgrub thabs mkhas pa chen po pra b+ha ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos dge slong gzhon rin chen gyi don du dpal thar pa gling gi gtsug lag khang du legs par bsgyur ba'o//
mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /dar ma grags kyis rang 'gyur byas//
mtshan brjod klog pa'i man ngag kha che'i paN+Di ta shAkya shrI b+ha dras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rnam pa nyi shus byang chub pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs/ dpal ldan so ma shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ma hA dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'od kyis bsgyur//
bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal gyi sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon so ma shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po paN+Di ta ma hA dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga /slob dpon so ma shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ma hA dz+nyA na dang /lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu 'od kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i dkyil 'khor thams cad la bstod pa/ slob dpon so ma shrI mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ma hA dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu 'od kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
gtor ma rdzogs so//
dpal thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud kyi bshad sbyar gsang ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po padz+nya ka ra warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos sgyur cing zhus te gton la phab pa'o//
don gyi 'bru 'grel slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba zhes bya ba/ cho ga zhib mo'i rgyal po chen po'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ snying po rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba/ dza laM d+ha ra'i rdo rje slob dpon/ ka ma d+he nu ba zhes bya ba'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /A tsaR+Ya bi na ya tsan+d+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis/ 'phan yul rgyal gyi lug lhas (slas)su bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa rdzogs so/

bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i 'grel ba mdzes pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po rdo rje go chas mdzod pa rdzogs so/ /'grel ba 'di yi tshad gyur pa/ tshig su bcad pa drug stong dang / bcu bzhi dag ni yod pa ste/ yi ge mkhan la phan phyir ro/ dpal ldan ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rgya cher 'grel ba 'di dpyad zlar ba'i yar gyi ngo'i gza' phur bu skar ma rgyal gyi nyin par mchog gis rje btsun rgyal po chen po mchog gi dbang phyug dpal lha 'od zer go cha yis/ mdzad pa'i dpal rgyal po'i lha khang du shAkya'i dge slong rin chen 'byung gnas bzang po rang gis lag pas bris te/ lo lnga brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga lon no//
ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba gzi brjed kyi rgyal po brtag pa snang ba'i rgyan zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su bid+ya ka ra warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dbang phyug rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba gzi brjid kyi rgyal po sku gsum gyi gtsug gtor gyi rgyud las/ rgyud phyi ma'i bshad pa gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon sangs rgyas kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mA ra ka la sha dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba khyung po chos brtson gyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon su ra b+ha dras/ dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi spyi'i rim pa zhal dang 'dra bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rig pa gzhon nus bsgyur ba'o//
ngan song thams cad rnam par sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur cing bshad nas gtan la phab pa'o//
yul sing ga la'i rdo rje slob dpon chen po/ rdo rje go cha'i slob ma rdo rje slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud dpal ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i cho ga zhes bya ba rdzogaso so/ /rgya gar gi mkhan po ki ri Na ka ra ba ra dang / lo tsA ba dge tshul khyung grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
slob dpon chen po kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa/ ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i ro'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka na ka war ma dang / dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
ro bsreg pa'i cho ga mdo danng bsres pa slob dpon chen po kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa/ ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i ro'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrd+d+ha ka na ka war ma dang / dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
zhes bya ba dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon skal bzang dga' bas mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhas pa chen po slob dpon ni na shi dang / lo tsA ba dge slong g.yun gdrun g'od kyis bsgyur ba'o//
ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon kun dga' snying po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa dzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsar+ya bud+d+ha shrI shAn+ti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sangs rgyas gsang ba dang / many+dzu shrI war ma dang / bran ka mu tis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa rdo rje gtsug gtor gyi rgyud las btus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon d+harma kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po Ar+ya d+harma pA la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis gtan la phab pa'o//

ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i cho ga'i bya ba mdor bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a nan+ta pa ra he ta'i zhal snga nas kyis//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po klu sgrub snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bai ro tsa na rak+Shi ta dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba glan chung gis bsgyur ba'o/ slad kyis stag lo tsA bas bcos pa'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po dA ri ka pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag rdo rje lta bu zhes bya ba dpal kam pa las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas dang bod kyi sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis zhus pa/
de kho na nyid gsal bar byed pa'i sgrol ma zhes bya ba/ dpal kam+pa la'i yum gyis mdzad pa'i rim pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon chen po kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon chen po rat+na kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po ma hA pA Nasa bsgyur ba'o//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga mdor bsdus pa slob dpon dad po'i 'byung gnas go chas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka na ka war ma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa tshul brgya lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
yi ge brgya pa'i bshad pa/ slob dpon pad+ma'i rdo rje lcags kyus/ stong phrag brgya pa las ji snyed pa rnams brjed du dogs nas bris pa yin no/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi snying po'i sngags / ye ge brgya pa'i cho ga rdzogs so//
yi ge brgya pa'i cho ga rdzogs so//
bzlas pa'i phreng ba'i mtshan nyid rdzogs so/ paN+Di ta pa ra he ta dang / lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
'di ni khrus kyi cho ga'o/ /paN+Di ta pa ra he ta dang / lo tsA ba nag tsho dge slong shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
bi ma la uSh+NI Sha'i gzungs las/ mchod rten sgrub pa'i cho ga rnal 'byor gyi rgyud dang sdebs te/ slob dpon zhi ba'i snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bcom ldan 'das mi 'khrugs pa'i sgrub thabs rgyas pa slob dpon dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bcom ldan 'das mi 'khrugs pa'i sgrub thabs dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon dpa' bo rde rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mgon po mi 'khrugs pa sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon dze tA ris mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma gnyan gyis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
bcom ldan 'das mi 'khrugs pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so//
sbyin sreg gi cho ga di paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa rdo rje chos kyi rnal 'byor gcig pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po s+thi ra ma tis yo ga'i gzhung rgyud phyi nang las nges don mdor bsdus te mdzad pa/ rgyan dam pa'i le'u bam po gcig tu byas pa rdzogs so/ /cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis skad phyi mo dang thug pa'o//

rnam par snang mdzad mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus pa'i don slob dpon bud+d+ha gu h+yas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ /'di la sh+lo ka ni nyis stong sum brgya yod do//
rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa rnam par sprul pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyi rgyud chen po/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas phyin ci ma log par bshad pa rdzogs so//
rnam par snang mdzad mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa rnam par sprul pa byin gyis slob pa'i rgyud chen po slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas phyin ci ma log par bshad pa rdzogs so/ /rnam par snang mdzad mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i tshig 'grel zhes grags pa 'di ni dpal snang thang gi gtsug lag khang du bstan bcos bdo kyi yul du 'gyur ba ji ltar rnyed pa bsdus pa'i tshe/ 'grel ba 'di'i dpe phyi mo ma dag cing gong 'og 'khrugs la bar bar nas cung zad ma tshang ba zhig la brten pa bstan 'gyur thams cad du ma dag pa rgyud pa dang / skad gsar bcad kyis gtan la ma phab pa'i 'gyur yang mi bde ba zhig snang ba las/ skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po skab dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur ba'i rgyud kyi tshig dang bstun te/ skad gsar bcad dang mthun par bcos pa 'di ni yul dbus kyi ban+de gzhon nu dpal zhes bgyi bas/ dpal rtse thang gi gtsug lag khang du lcags mo sbrul gyi lo la bris pa'o//
rnam par snang mdzad chen po mngon par byang chub pa dang 'brel pa'i mchod pa'i cho ga / slob dpon dpal bzang rab dgas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rnam par snang mdzad kyi sgrub pa'i thabs kyi cho ga /slob dpon rgyal ba'i 'od kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon lhas sbas kyi mdzad pa sgrub thabs gyi gter zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra war ma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rig pa gzhon nus bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ lho phyogs kyi yul be ta rar sku 'khungs pa/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po slob dpon gyi mchog klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas bsdus pa'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal gsang ba'i rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga / slob dpon don yod pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bcom ldan 'das khro bo chen po rnam par rgyal ba'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga'i rim pa dang / dngos grub kyi tshul nges par bstan pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon don yod zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//

bsam gtan phyi ma zhes bya ba/ rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra pra b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa dpung bzangs kyis zhus pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus pa'i don slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'phags pa dpung bzangs kyis zhus pa'i rgyud tshig gi don bshad pa'i brjed byang rdzogs so//
'phags pa dpung bzangs kyis zhus pa'i rgyud tshig gi don bshad pa'i brjed byang rdzogs so//
dpa' bo gcig sgrub pa'i 'grel pa gtsug lag khang dza gad+da lI lan gyi su b+hA ka ra zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'phags pa lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi cho ga zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa de kho na nyid gsal bar byed pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon klu grub kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA dang bod kyi lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng+ge shrI na len+t+ra'i sgo 'gram du bsgyur ba'o//
dpal phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi gzungs kyi 'grel pa/ rig pa'i gnas thams cad la mkhas pa'i paN+Di ta chen po karma badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon bzang skyong kyis mdzad pa'o// 'di'i sho+lo ka'i grangs ni tshigs su bcad pa bdun brgya'o// rgya gar gyi paN+Dita pA NI ni yongs su rdzogs pa'i snyan dngags dang tshig gi sdeb la mkhas pa non ni paN+Di ta dang bod kyi lo tsA ba u rgyan pa rin chen dpal gyis ri bo chenpo sbu tra'i mgul du bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon bo d+hi sa twas mdzad pa'i 'grel pa phyi ma rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa/
rdo rje rnam par 'jom pa'i gzungs kyi rnam par bshad pa/ rdo rje sgron ma zhes bya ba/ gsang sngags mtha' dag la mnga' brnyes pa'i/ slob dpon chen po pad+ma 'byung gnas kyi mdzad pa'o/
'phags pa rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i 'grel pa rin po che gsal ba zhes bya ba/ bya ba'i rgyud kyi grub pa sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mkhan po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dpa' many+dzu shrI war mas bsgyur ba'o/ phyis paN+Di ta jon+te ta du la dang / lo tsA ba 'og bsod nam mos pa bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i don rnam par phye ste bshad pa/ rgya gar gyi slob dpon chen po bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi don rnam par bshad pa rgya cher 'grel pa/ bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/
slob dpon chen po rdo rje go chas mdzad pa rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po shd+ha ka ra warma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi don rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon bde ba'i myu gus mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi 'grel pa jo bo smri tis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po de nyid kyis sgyur/ phyi dang nang de kho na nyid kyi khrus gsum ni theg pa gsum dang ji bzhin du sgyur ro//
sems can thams cad 'jil bar byed pa dang zhi ba dang bsrung ba ste/ las gsum dang 'brel ba'i zhi ba'i 'khrul 'khor gyi rnam par dbye ba rdzogs so//
rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i 'grel pa rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po sha ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de pa puN+ye ma ti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs zhes bya ba'i rim par phye ba/ rgya cher 'grel pa gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba slob dpon ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag /rgyal po chen po dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po theg pa chen po gsang sngags la mkhas pa/ slob dpon bud+d+ha gu h+ya dang / bod kyi zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ska ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa las/ slad kyis rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po/ shrad+d+ha ka war ma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mkhas pa chen po rin chen bzang pos rgya dpe dang gtugs nas bcos so/ /rdzogs so//
kun nas sgor 'jug pa'i 'od zer gtsug tor dri ma med par snang ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po dang dam tshig la rnam par blta ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon dngos grub thob pa lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa dzogs so/ /gsang sngags rig 'dzin sde snod la/ mkha' ltar shes rab dang ba ni/ nyi ma lta bur ma mongs pa'i/ mkhas pa dza la de ba la/ langs ban+de tshul brtsegs kyis/ gus bcas mang du gsol btab nas/ spu rgyal bod las khyad par du/ nad med sa gsang mdo khams su/ yid bzhin nor 'dra'i gzungs mchog gi /'grel pa dpag bsam shing 'dra 'di/ bsgyur ba'i dge bas dad ldan rnams/ gzungs 'di rgya cher spyod par shog /paN+Di ta dza yaM de ba dang / lo tsA ba langs ban+de tshul khrims brtsegs kyis bsgyur ba'o/
'phags ma de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug tor nas byung ba gdug dkar mo can gzhan gyi mi thub pa phyir zlog pa chen mo zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa slob dpon shU raM ga bor ma badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur/
stong chen mo rab tu 'joms ma'i 'bum 'grel dag pa lnga pa/ stong chen mo rab tu 'joms ma'i 'grel pa/ las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rig sngags kyi rgyal mo rma bya chen po'i mdo'i 'bum 'grel rgya gar gyi slob dpon chen po las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po a mo g+ha badz+ras rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
rig sngags kyi rgyal mo gsang sngags rjes su 'dzin ma'i mdo'i 'bum 'grel/ slob dpon chen po las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rig sngags kyi rgyal mo gsang sngags rjes su 'dzin ma'i mdo'i 'bum 'grel/ paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po mi mnyam rdo rje'i sras/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rdzes/ jo mo sgrol mas zhabs kyis bcags pa/ tshangs pa'i 'byung gnas/ rdo lung dgon par rang 'gyur ro//
rig kyi rgyal mo bsil ba tshal gyi mdo'i 'bum 'grel/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /smon lam stobs kyi grong khyer mu gyer btsal/ mkhas par grags pa'i mi mnyam rdo rje'i sras/ skye ba lnga brgyar sbyangs pa'i 'bras bu yis/ rig pa'i gnas lnga dag la ma rmongs shing / gsang sngags gdams pa ma lus thugs la mnga' ba can/ mtshan yang don yod rdo rje zhes par grags/ sngon gyi smon lam dbang gyi bod yul dbus su byon/ smon lam stobs kyis dam pa'i 'bro lo'i bla mar gyur/ 'dzam gling byang phyogs brag dmar dpal gyi bsam yas su/ rgyal po khyad par 'phags pa khri pa'i rdung rgyud sras/ lha gcig khyad par 'phags pa lha tsam dar sgron gyis/ bkra shis pho brang rdo lung dgon pa ru/ lo paNa zhabs nas btegs nas dam chos 'di bsgyur pa/ bsgyur pa'i bsod nams gang thob bsags pa des/ bdag dang mtha' yas sems can kun/ bla med byang chub myur du thob par shog/

'phags pa sgo drug pa'i gzungs kyi rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'phags pa sgo mtha' yas pa sgrub pa'i gzungs rnam par bshad pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA war ma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
'phags pa sgo mtha' yas pas bsgrub pa'i gzungs rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA war ma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de yes shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
dam tshigs gsum bkod pa'i rgyal po'i yi ge brgya pa sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon chen po ke d+ha ra Na d+hisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta dpal go mi 'chi med dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
byang chub sems dpa' dze ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa'o/ 'di'i rgyud pa ni tshe dpag med/ grub pa brnyes pa'i snying po zhabs/ dze ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal ba/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ pa ri lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge /rgya nag phug pa/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'du ma/ bla ma dge bsdings pa/ bla ma bsam gtan bzang po'o//
'phags pa tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon mkhas pa dze ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta/ 'jam dpa'i dbyangs dang / lo tsA ba lce dga' dpal gyi bsgyur ba'o/
slob dpon dze ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal pas/ bram ze nam mkha' dbyangs kyi bu'i ched du mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI many+dzu dang lo tsA ba lce dga' ba'i dpal gyis bsgyur pa'o/
'jam dpal rdo rje blo gros 'phel zhes bya ba kun gyi thun mong ma yin pa slob dpon klu sgrub zhabs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'jam pa'i dbyangs dpa' bo gcig tu grub pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
rje btsun dam pa rgya gar gyi gdam spa rdzogs so//
rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs shes rab 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+rA ka ra gup+tasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang phyes pa dpal gyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa 'jam dpal g.yo ba'i 'khor lo'i man ngag / kha che'i paN+Di ta shAkya shrI b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ngag gi dbang phyug la bu mo brgyad kyis stod pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'jam dpal la khye'u bcu drug gis bstod pa rdzogs so/
'phags pa ngag gi dbang phyug gtso 'khor lnga pa'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta thig le bum pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
gur kum gzhon nu lta bu bstod pa/ slob dpon seng ge mi g.yo bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o/
bcom ldan 'das 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi bstod pa byin rlabs dang bcas pa snyan ngags mkhan rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can mkhas pa chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po mkhas pa chen po su ma ti kIrti'i zhal snga nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab dang / mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur ba'o/
dpal ye shes yon tan bzang po zhes bya ba'i bstod pa slob dpon rdo rje mtshon chas mdzad pa rdzogs so// rdog lo tsA ba'i bsgyur//
bcom ldan 'das 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi bstod pa/ rtog go ba rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu slob dpon phyogs kyi glad pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shra d+d+hA ka ra war ma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs kyi cho ga /slob dpon shrad+d+hA ka ra war mas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs/ dngos grub brnyes pa'isloba dpon mi pham pa'i bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bo b+hu ti tsan+d+ra dang / chag lo tsA ba dge lasong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//


'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i paN+Di ta chen po ma tis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs dza ga tA la'i paN+Di ta chen po dA na shrI la bod yul gyi dbus dang srong srin po'i rar lha'i skad las bod kyi brdar 'khrul pa med par bsgyur ba'o//

'phags pa a ra pa tsa na'i mchod pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /lung du ston pa'i bstan bcos kyi skad cung zad rtogs pa'i/ shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ grub pa'i zhing dam pa mang yul skye grong 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang po'i gtsug lag khang las/ cung zad mi rang pa'i chon po rnams kyi gdan sa/ dpal shes rab kyi gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i lha lnga'i bstod pa/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mi mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha bcu bdun la don rtags kyi sgo nas bstod pa dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba rdzogs so//
'jig rten dbang phyug gi bstod pa yid 'phrog sdig 'joms zhes bya ba/ shar phyogs ba reN+Di'i slob dpon mkhas pa chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs ba raN+Di'i dzA ga ta la'i paN+Di ta chen po dA na shrI las bsgyur ba//
thugs rje chen po la bstod cing bskul ba nyer bzhi pa/ dge brnyen chen po zla bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pa ra me shwa ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi zhabs la/ tsar+ya Di pa zhabs kyis bstod pa rdzogs so/ /sgra mkhan chen po rgyal ba snyan gyi zhal snga nas/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa don yod zhags pa lha lnga'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta chen po e ra pa tis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba ba ri rin chen grags pas bsgyur ba'o/
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi bstod pa grub thob chen po tsarba pa Tisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po nags kyi rin chen gyi zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba 'gos gzhon nu dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//

'jig rten dbang phyug gi bstod pa brgya pa/ snyan ngag mkhan chen po shrI badz+ra de ba zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /yon tan phul du byung ba dpag tu med pa dang ldan pas spras pa bla ma dam pa chos kyi rgyal po dang / mi'i dbang po dpon chen shAkya bzang po'i bka' lung gis/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po snyan ngag mkhan chen po ma hA paN+Di ta lak+Sh+mi ka ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shong ston gyis bsgyur ba'o//
'jig rten dbang phyug la bstod pa/ dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
nor bu gling gi thugs rje chen po lha lnga la bstod pa/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug 'khor dang bcas pa la bstod pa/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis bstod pa smre sngags su gsol pa rdzogs so/
byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la smre sngags kyi sgo nas bstod pa byin rlabs can 'di nyid/ lnga brgya pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu lta bur gyur pa/ mthong lam rgyud la skyes pa'i gang zag / slob dpon chen po zla ba grags pa'i zhal mnga' nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
snying rje la bstod pa/ dge bsnyen kun sbyin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
bcom ldan 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang bstod phyag 'tshal/ dge slong ma zla mdzes kyis bstod pa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /'di ni rgya gar shar phyogs kyi btsun pa tsan+d+ra shrI'i dag las 'byung ba dang rgya dpe bstun nas dge slong bsod nams rnam rgyal gyis bsgyur ba'o/ /spyan ras gzigs dbang po mgon po mchog la bstod pa' yi/ bsod nams gang zhing zla ba dung ltar dkar ba des/ rgyal ba kun gyi sras kyi thu bo de ltar bur/ sdug bsngal 'gro ma mi 'jigs rtsos ba nyid gyur cig /ral pa 'chang zhing shin tu zhi ba yangs pa'i spyan/ rtag par rab tu dang ba zla ba'i dkyil 'khor zhal/ lha dang lha min rnams kyis zhabs kyi 'dam skyes la/ phyag byas nor bu pad+ma la byung mgon por 'dud/ 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug la/ klu'i rgyal po nor rgyal kyis bstod pa/ dpal nags kyi rin chen gyi zhal sngar bsod nams rnam par rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//

slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub bdag nyid chen po mi 'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rje ldan pa sa drug pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yin yang / sa dang po'i byang chub sems dpar byin gyis brlabs pa/ dper na da'i nye gnas kun dga' bo sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' yin yang so so'i skye bor byin brlabs pa lta bu'o/ zhes bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la/ 'jig rten khams bde ba cen du gshegs te/ sa brgyad pa la gnas nas lus gnyis su byas te/ gcig ni de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag tu med pa la mchod par byed/ gcig ni dga' ldan du byams pa la mdo 'di nyid kyi don 'dri'o zhes gsungs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams dang ba'i 'od ces bya bar de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes 'byung gnas 'od ces bya bar lung bstan par mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi slob dpon pad+ma'i zhal snga nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba btsun pa rgyal ba mchog dbyangs kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs zhal bcu gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la bstod pa/ dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi bstod pa/ dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rje btsun thugs rje chen po la bstod pa dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa rdzags so//

thugs rje chen po kha sar pa Ni'i sgrub thabs tshigs su bcad pa bzhi pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
thugs rje chen po ye shes sems dpa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
spyan ras gzigs 'khor lo gsum bsgom pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
thugs rje chen po lha lnga'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
dpal 'jig rten mgon po tshad med bzhi'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
dpal 'jig rten mgon po ye ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
sems ngal so ba'i thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
thugs rje chen po yi ge med pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
stong pa nyid bsgom pa'i man ngag rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
dpal kha sar+pa Ni mar me 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
dpal kha sar+pa Ni'i sku gsum gyi gdams pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
thugs rje chen po mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
thugs rje chen po nam mkha' dri med kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
thugs rje chen po nam mkha' mdzad kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
spyan ras gzigs bcu gcig pa'i zhal can gyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon a dzi ta mi tra gup+tasa mdzad/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI dza ta mi tra nan+ta zhal snga nas dang/ kha che'i paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas gtan la phab nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/

thugs rje chen po kha sar+pa Na'i sgrub thabs tshigs su bcad pa bzhi pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon shrI dza ga ta mi tras mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o/

rig sngags drag po'i gzungs sngags kyi 'khrul 'khor zhes bya ba/ slob dpon su pA gI shwa ra kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya bod gnyis la grags par gyur pa yis/ mdo sngags don la mkhas pa'i di paM ka ra la/ sgra sgyur bod na mkhas pa'i rgyal po brtson seng ges bka' bas nyams su blangs nas rin chen gser gyis zhus//

khro bo rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /slob dpon ba su d+ha badz+ra mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga rdzogs so/ /slob dpon ba su d+ha badz+ra mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje 'dzin pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga zhes ba rdzogs so/ /slob dpon ba su d+ha badz+ra mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
bsrung ba'i cho ga las thams cad pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /slob dpon ba su d+ha badz+ra mdzad pa rnal 'byor pa bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
khro bo'i rgyal po phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon su tsan+d+ra b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi na tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon chen po blo bzang skyong gis mdzad pa'o/ 'di'i shwa lo ka'i grangs ni tshigs su bcad pa bdun brgya'o// rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta sgra pA NI ni yongs su rdzogs pa'i snyan dngags dang tshig gi sdeb la mkhas pa non ni paN+Di ta dang bod kyi lo tsA ba o rgyan pa rin chen dpal gyis ri bo chen po spu tra'i mgul du bsgyur ba'o//

'phags pa rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i cho ga zhib mo dang cas pa/ bram ze rig sngags 'chang grub pa mkhas pa chen po ku mA ra se nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bud+d+ha gup+ta dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dbang many+dzu shrI war mas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ phyis paN+Di ta dz+nyA na teng ha du dang / lo tsa ba da 'og bsod nams mos pa shes rab kyis gsan nas zhus pa'o//
'phags pa rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi sgrub pa'i thabs dpa' bo gcig pa zhes bya ba mkhas pa chen po sangs rgyas gsang bas rigs can du mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mkhan po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dpa' many+dzu shrI war mas bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gtor ma slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dpa' many+dzu shrI war mas bsgyur ba'o//

rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi rin chen snang ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po sa ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po'i bla ma de ba pur+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//

klu sgrub rin po che dbyig sgrub ces bya ba/ dpal mar me mdzad kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/
