klu'i gdon las thar bar byed pa'i las klu'i srog me dpal gyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba/ klu'i rnam par 'joms pa'i snying gzer du bkod pa/ slob dpon chen po mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mi bzad pa'i nad zhi bar byed pa gser gyi rgya mtsho zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshe 'phel ba'i sgrub thabs rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/
bsod nams 'phel bar byed pa'i dpal ye shes kyi phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sgra la gnas pa'i bsam gtan zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sgra la mi gnas pa'i bsam gtan zhes bya ba rnal 'byor pa'i dkyil 'khor rkyen drungs nas 'don pa/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/
sgra mthar gyis rnal 'byor pa'i lus sems kyi 'brel ba gcad pa/ slob dpon chen po mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs pa'i rim pa phyogs gcig tu sdebs pa rdzogs so/
them yig gsang ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon pad+ma 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /d+harma kIrti b+ha dras yang zhus byas so//
khro bo'i rgyal po rde rje gnam lcags 'bar ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ klu 'dul ba'i ngan thabs/ bal po'i man ngag rgya gar gyi bla ma mai tris mdzad pa rdzogs so/
khro bo'i rgyal po rdo rje gnam lcags 'bar ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga /rgya gar gyi slob dpon chen po lho phyogs dpal gyi ri la bzhugs pa'i bla ma mai tri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta bal po de ba pur+Na ma ti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi bzang po'i bal po'i yul du bsgyur cing zhus te gten la phab pa'o//
'phas pa gshin rje gshed nag po'i rgyud la gsungs pa'i phyogs gcig pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon jo bo rje dang bod kyi lo tsA ba nag tsho tshul rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
dpal rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dge slong ba ris bsgyur ba'o//
rtog pa bdun brgya pa nas gsungs pa'i rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar bA ra NA si'i paN+Di ta pu ru Shot+ta ma'i zhal snga nas mnyan te/ lo tsA ba shAkyi'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos nyang ro 'khris kyi gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
rtog pa bdun brgya pa'i rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi yul bA ra NA si'i paN+Di ta pu ru Shot+ta ma'i zhal snga nas mnyan te/ lo tsA ba shAkyi'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos bla ma dam pa'i bkas gtsug lag khang chen po dpal thar pa gling du legs par bsgyur ba'o//
rgyud thams cad kyi snying po bla med pa rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta pra b+ha ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi yul bA ra NA si'i paN+Di ta pu ru Shot+ta ma'i zhal snga nas legs par mnyan te/ lo tsA ba shAkyi'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos bla ma dam pa'i bkas gtsug lag khang chen po dpal thar pa gling du bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ bla ma gser gling pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas rang 'gyur du mdzad nas/ dge slong dbang phyug rgyal mtshan la gnang ba'o//
khro bo rgyal po mi g.yo ba la bstod pa/ paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa khro bo'i rgyal po mi g.yo ba la bstod pa/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
khro chen gtum po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon pra b+ha ka ra kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /thugs rdzes chen po'i rgyud gsum pa/ mkhas rtogs 'dzom zhing yi dam mthong / spobs pa brtsod pa snyan dang mkhas/ sbyin pa tshul khrims kyi rang 'gyur//
khro chen gtum po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta puN+ye shrI dang / lo tsA ba glog skya gzhon nu 'bar gyis bsgyur ba'o/ slob dpon dze tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa'o//
gtum po khro bo chen po'i shes rab blo 'phel gyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta dA na shrI las rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po dA na shrI las rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
legs par grub par byed pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs bsdus pa/ bde bar gshegs pa'i sras po slob dpon byang chub mchog gis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dge ba'i 'dod 'jo zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon chen po klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po nag po'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mgos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mchod rten lnga gdab pa'i cho ga slob dpon chen po bo d+hi sa twas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa kun nas sgor 'jug pa'i 'od zer gtsug tor dri ma med par snang ba'i gzungs bklag cing mchod rten brgya rtsa brgyad dam/ mchod rten lnga gdab pa'i cho ga mdo snge las btus pa/ slob dpon chen po bo d+hi sa twa mdzad pa rdzogs so//

mchod rten gdab pa'i cho ga'o/





sangs rgyas kyi sku bshad pa rdzogs so/
mchod rten gyi cha dbye ba 'dul ba las byung ba'i mdo rdzogs so//
de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig bsrung ba byes bya ba'i sgrub thabs rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/
mchod rten lnga gdab pa'i cho ga/ dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//

slob dpon dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi mdzad pa'i gtsug tor dri ma med pa'i gzungs kyi cho ga rdzogs so//

'phags ma gdugs dkar mo can gyi gtor ma'i cho ga /slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /tho ling gi gtsug lag khang du dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs dkar mo can gzhan gyis mi thub pa phyir bzlog pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa'i bsrung ba'i 'khor lo rdzogs so/
slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa 'khrul 'khor rdzogs so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba bzangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/
dus ma yin par 'chi ba bzlog pa'i thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
bgegs bzlog cing gzir ba'i thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dmag dpung gzhom pa'i thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dngos grub bsgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'jigs pa las skyob pa'i thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
ser ba bsrung ba'i thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/
nad gdug pa can gso ba'i thabs slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/
'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs dkar mo can gyi cho ga'i man ngag /slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzags so/ /bla ma zangs dkar lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
rims bsrung ba'i cho ga /slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/
gor bsrung ba'i cho ga /slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//

zhi ba'i sbyin sreg /slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba zangs kar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
mngon spyod kyi las/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba zangs kar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//

slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mi'i man ngag /sbyin sreg rdzogs so/
dngos grub sgrub pa'i sgo nas sri'u gso ba/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba zangs kar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
bzlogs pa'i zor bya ba'i cho ga slo dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba zangs kar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
mchod rten sgrub pa'i cho ga'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba zangs kar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs dkar mo can ma zhes bya ba'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga /slob dpon rdo rje rnon pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bcom ldan 'das gtsug tor gdugs dkar mo can gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga /slob dpon mkhas pa pad+ma'i lcags kyus mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
tsha tsha'i cho ga bya ba slob dpon pad+ma'i lcags kyus mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /zangs dkar lo tsA bas tho ling gi gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o/
gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs dkar mo can gyi gzungs 'don pa'i cho ga / slob dpon shu raM ga barma badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa gdugs dkar can la bstod pa rdzogs so/
'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs dkar po can gzhan gyis mi thub pa zhes bya ba'i nye bar bshad pa bla ma rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong ba ris bsgyur ba'o//
bcom ldan 'das kyi gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs dkar mo can gyi cho ga'i rim pa/ slob dpon g+hi ri wa tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
gtsug gtor gdugs dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mang du thos pa'i slob dpon pad+ma'i lcags kyus/ rigs ldan ha ra pa'i slob dpon kA ma la d+he nu pa'i rjes su 'brangs nas sbyar ba rdzogs so/ /A tsar+ya bi na ya tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa gdugs dkar mo can gzhan gyis mi thub pa sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra dang /klo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis bsgyur ba'o//
gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma'i bstod pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa gdugs dkar can la bstod pa/ slob dpon gi ri wa tas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa rig pa'i rgyal mo so sor 'brang ma'i 'khor lo'i sems sbyang / slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ paN+Di ta chos kyi sde dang / lo tsA ba dge tshul nam mkha' rdo rjes bsgyur ba'o/
so sor 'brang ba'i bsrung ba'i 'khor lo bri ba'i thabs/ slo dpon rat+na A ka ra shAna tis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
so sor 'brang ma'i sgrubs thabs rdzogs so/
'phags ma rma bya chen mo'i sgrubs thabs rdzogs so/
stong chen mo rab tu 'joms ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba d+harma kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o/
'phags pa gsang sngags rjes su 'dzin ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/
slob dpon chen po dzo ta'i dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
so sor 'brang ma chen mo'i bsrung ba/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ gdams ngag dus da lta byed pa'i tshul paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti'i zhal snga nas gzhung du bsdebs pa rdzogs so/ /lag pa reg cing dza zhes brdzod pas gshegs su gsol/ lo tsA ba chen po d+harma kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o/ gzungs gzhan gyi cho ga pyed/ gra la lnga gang yin pa'i mtshan ma dbus su bris la/ gzhan rdul tshon dang gtor ma dang dbus kyi bum pa gzhan dang rten dang / cho ga'i rim pa thams cad gong ma dang 'gre'o/ de ltar byas pas gzungs ga'i dkyil 'khor du 'gyur ro/ yang dang yang du bla ma la gtugs pa'o//
'phags pa so sor 'brang ma chen mo'i rig pa'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /rgya gar yul ba ra NA sir paN+Di ta pu ru Shot+ta ma'i zhal snga nas legs par mnyan te/ lo tsA ba dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ gtsug lag khang chen po thar pa gling du bsgyur ba'o//
bsrung ba lnga'i cho ga slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po mu di ta shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba ban+de bkra shis rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o/ /chag lo tsA bas bsgyur te bcos pa'o//
so sor 'brang ma chen mo'i 'khor lo bri ba'i cho ga slob dpon dza ta ris mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti kIrti'i zhal sngar dge slong pradz+nyA kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
bsrung ba lnga'i mchod pa'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po/ nags kyi rin chen gyi zhal snga nas dang / gzhon nu dpal gyis bsgyar ba'o/ 'di ni dze tA ri'i rjes su 'brang pa yin no zhes gsungs so/
zhes pa gza' dgu'i mchod pa'i cho ga'o/ 'di ni rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen gyis/ nyid kyi slob dpon hang sa zhes bya ba'i gsung zin bris pa'i yi ge las gzhon nu dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa drA bi da'i bum pa'i cho ga rim par phye ba rdzogs so//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga slob dpon ngag gyi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang / khams pa lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi sngon gyi smon lam gyi khyad pa rgyas pa'i mdo sde'i man ngag slon dpon bo d+hi sa twas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi sngon gyi smon lam gyi khyad pa rgyas pa'i gzungs bklag pa'i cho ga mdo sde las bsdus pa/ slon dpon bo d+hi sa twas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi sngon gyi smon lam gyi khyad pa rgyas pa zhes bya ba'i mdo sde bklag cing de bzhin gshegs pa bdun mchod de/ smon lam gdab pa'i mdo sde las btus te rim pa par bklag pa/ slon dpon bo d+hi sa twas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rin chen grags pas mdzad pa gzungs 'dus spyi'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /bal po'i lo tsA ba ma hA pa las bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rin chen grags pas mdzad pa gzungs spyi'i cho ga kun gnang gsal ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /bal po ma hA pa na'i rang 'gyur ro//
slob dpon chen po rat+na kIrtisa mdzad pa sgrub thabs thams cad kyi las ka gsal byed ces bya ba rdzogs so//
rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i snying po'i cho ga zhib mo/ mkhan po ner ban rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga thun mong pa paN+Di dpal su ma ti kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mkhas pa de nyid dang lo tsA ba pradz+nyA kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//

dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rdo rje phreng ba zhes bya ba paN+Di ta chen po gnas brtan chen po a b+ha yA ka ra gup+tasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba khe rgad ban+de 'khor lo grags kyis bsgyur/ bstan bcos kun gyi spu ti gcig /phyogs kun mi 'jigs seng ge dang /khe rgad ban+de 'khor lo grags kyis bsgyur/ /dus phyis khams pa ban+de shes rab dpal gyis/ bi kra ma shrI la'i gtsug lag khang du mkhas pa chen po de nyid kyi spyan sngar legs par gtugs shing bcos nas gtan la phab pa'o/ /slad kyis bla ma rje btsun paN+Di ta chen po mkhas btsun grub chen brnyes pa rat+na rak+Shi ta'i zhabs dang /bla ma chos rje paN+Di ta gnas brtan chen po ra hu la shrI b+ha bra'i zhal snga nas dang / bla ma rje btsun chen po nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer gyi zhal snga nas dang / paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po ma Ni ka shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas/ chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis legs par zhus shing gtugs te gtan la phab pa'o/ /slad yang lo tsA ba dge slong dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa sgra dang don la legs par dpyad nas/ mi bcos su mi rung ba rnams bsgyur te/ cung zad dag par byas so//
rdo rje 'phag mos mngon sum du byin gyis brlabs pa'i paN+Di ta chen po 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor gyi phreng ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /'di'i gzhung tshad ni stong nyis brgya bzhus so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta chen po thams cad mkhyen pa'i dpal bzang pos 'gyur rnying pa la brten nas smon 'gre'i gtsug lag khang du sgra rang sgyur mdzad pa'o/ /paN+Di ta de nyid kyis lan gnyis su zhus shing gtugs so/ slad kyi rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta chen po mkhas btsun mchog gi grub pa rnyes pa/ bla ma rje btsun chen po rat+na rak+Shi ta'i zhabs dang / bla ma rje btsun paN+Di ta chen po re wan+d+ra'i zhal snga nas/ chag lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong dpal gyi mtha' can gyis zhus shing dag par bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
sbyin sreg gi cho ga 'od kyi snye ma zhes bya ba/ rje btsun ma rdo rje rnal 'byor mas byi gyis rlabs pa'i paN+Di ta chen po a b+ha yA ka ra gup+ta'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po thams cad mkhyen pa'i dpal bzang pos/ bod yul gyi dbus drang srong srin po rir rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/ slad kyis paN+Di ta chen po rig pa'i gnas rnams thugs su chud pa'i mkhas pa dag dang /grub pa rnyed pa'i skyes bu chen po rnams kyi gsung gi bdud rtsi'i rgyun gyis thugs gtams zhing de kho na nyid la gzhol ba'i slob dpon nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang / chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis legs par bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa/ dus phyis shong lo tsA ba dge slong blo brtan gyis legs par bcos shing dag par byas so//
'phags pa sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa/ pa tshab tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
dam tshig gsum gyi rgyal po'i sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po ku mu da 'byung gnas blo gros kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa'o/ /paN+Di ta a b+ha yA ka ra'i zhal snga nas/ pa tshab kyi rgyud kyi dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje 'dzin pas legs par gsungs pa'i bstod pa/ dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
bstod pa'i phan yon dang bcas pa 'di nyid ni rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi brgyan las gsungs pa yin no/ dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
paN+Di ta chen po rin chen 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa'i dam tshig gi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
gdams ngag gi rim pa'i bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gdan gyi sgrub thabs yongs su rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po a b+ha yA ka ra'i zhal snga nas/ dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
zhes bya ba 'di ni rdo rje gdan gyi sgrub thabs te rdzogs so//
'phags pa yi ge drug pa rig pa chen mo'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//

bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/
dpal 'byung po 'dul byed kyi sgrub thabs mdor bsdus pa rdzogs so/
mdor bsdus pa yongs su rdzogs shing rgyas par gyur pa 'byung po 'dul byed kyi sgrub thabs kyi cho ga dam pa thams cad 'dran pa'i 'jig rten gsum gyi rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/
dpal ldan nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/
nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /lha so so'i sgrub pa'i thabs rgyal mtsho zhes bya ba 'di rnams ni dpal ldan sa skya'i gtsug lag khang chen por paN+Di ta chen po gau taM shrI las brgyud cing paN+Di ta chen po kIrti tsin tra'i zhal snga nas zhus nas/ slob dpon chen po d+harmA pA la rak+Shi ta'i sku skyabs dang / dpon chen po kun dga' gzhon nu dang / ma gcig pas sbyin bdag mdzad pa la brten nas/ de shAna ta ri yo gi grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis/ bya lo zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes gsum las dben gnas dam pa chu mig khar yongs su rdzogs par bsgyur ro//
de bzhin gsheg pa klu'i dbang phyug rgyal po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon bdag nyid chen po klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
yi ge brgya pa'i cho ga slob dpon pad+masa mdzad pa rdzogs so/

'phags pa byams pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon thog med kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /jo bo chen po dang / dge bshes ston pas bsgyur pa las dus phyis paN+Di ta chen po bud+d+ha shrI dang / gnubs lo tsA bas dag par bcos so//

'phags pa kha sar+pa NI 'jig rten mgon po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/

mgon po gnod gnas kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/

lha mo 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/
lha mo 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon mya ngan med pa'i dpal gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'di ni rdo rje lu gu rgyud kyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po dze ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar mkhan po paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba mkhas pa mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
seng ldeng nags kyi sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal rnam par snang mdzad rdo rjes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
lha mo sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs brgya rtsa brgyad pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/ slad kyis rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta dA na shrI dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba blo gros grags pas bcos te gtan la phab pa'o/
sgrol ma tshe spel ba zhes bya ba'i rig pa/ slob dpon tsan dra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ma hA paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta'i zhal snga nas/ lo tsA ba zhang grub pa dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
paN+Di ta chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa'i dpal chen mo sgrol ma'i bstod pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po rgyal ba'i snyan gyi zhal snga nas/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi lo tsA ba blo gros rgyal pos bsgyur ba las cung zad dag par byas so//
rje btsun 'phags ma sgrol ma la bstod pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa tshigs su bcad pa bcu gnyis pa rdzogs so//
'phags ma sgrol ma'i bstod pa/ phrin las thams cad sgrub pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon tsan dra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
me tog phreng ba'i bstod pa 'di ni/ rje btsun ma la lnga brgya pa rnams kyis thams cad mkhyen pa'i khur che ba'i yon tan du ma dang ldan pa/ slob dpon tsan dra go mi zhes bya bas bstod pa rdzogs so//
'phags ma sgrol ma'i bstod pa slob dpon chen tsan dra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'phags ma sgrol ma 'jigs pa brgyad las skyob pa zhes bya ba'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba las/ slad kyi rgya gar gyi mkhan po byang chub sems dpa' dA na shrI dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mal gyi blo gros grags pas bcos te gtan la phab pa'o//
sgrol ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpan ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa'i slob ma thu bos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba khams pa dge slong ba ris bsgyur ba'o//
dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa'i cho ga mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon ba pa b+ha dras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rje btsun ma 'phags ma sgrol ma'i dkyil 'khor la 'jug pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba/ dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon chen po b+ha ba b+ha dras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ma hA paN+Di ta shrI bi ma la kIrti'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa zhang grub pa dpal bzang pos bal po'i grong khyer nas yam bu'i nub phyogs nyi ma'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur cing zhus nas gtan la phab pa'o//
sgrol ma yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon b+ha Tas mdzad pas rdzogs so//
sgrol ma'i khrus kyi cho ga slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha Tasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/
gso sbyong rang gi blang pa'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /sgrol ma'i dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha Tasa mdzad pa'o/ ma hA paN+Di ta shrI rat+na rak+Shi dang /lo tsA ba zhang grub pa dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
sgrol ma'i maN+Dala gyi cho ga snyan ngag mkhan po snying rje che bas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sgrol ma mchog sgrub pa zhes bya ba/ dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon bsod nams pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'jigs pa brgyad las skyob pa'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshas gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta ta thA ga ta b+ha dra dang / dge slong 'phags pas rgya'i yul cong du'i mkhar du bsgyur ba'o//
dpal sgrol ma dkar po 'chi ba slu ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal chos kyi rje sa'i steng na 'gran zla dang bral ba'i paN+Di ta chen po shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / sgra sgyur gyi lo tsA ba gnubs byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/
sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs d+ha byang chub sems dpa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta ta tha ga ta rak+Shi ta dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba ba ri rin chen grags pas bsgyur ba'o//
rje btsun sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po dpal ldan mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nya na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags ma lha mo sgrol ma bsgom pa'i cho ga rgyas pa slob dpon chen po mar me mdzad bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dul ba'i lha dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'jigs pa brgyad las skyob pa slob dpon mkhas pa dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/
rje btsun ma sgrol ma la bstod pa/ dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/
'phags ma sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs dpal ldan mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa'o/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bud+d+hA ka ra warma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
chom rkun bcing ba zhes bya ba'i rig pa rdzogs so/ /ma hA paN+Di ta shrI rat+na rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba zhang grub pa dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
'phags ma sgrol ma'i rjes su spyod pa'i gnod sbyin mo'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bai ro tsa na'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o/
me tog phreng 'dzin sgrol ma'i bstod pa dang bcas pas bsgrub pa rdzogs so/ /ma hA paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta pA dA'i zhal snga nas dang / zhang lo tsA ba grub pa dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/
rje btsun ma la bstod pa/ slob dpon ma tri tsi Tasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/
rje btsun 'phags ma sgrol ma la chos kyi rje paN+Di ta 'bum phrag gsum pas bstod pa rdzogs so//
'phags ma lha mo sgrol ma la bstod pa rdzogs so/
(bla ma) mkhan po shAkya shrI b+ha dras mdzad pa rje btsun sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs dza ta la'i paN+Di ta chen po bi d+hu ti tsan+d+rasa rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o/
dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs bram ze phur bus mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshangs pa'i bu mo dbyangs can ma la bstod pa 'grub pa ngag gi 'od zer zhes bya ba bram ze phur bus mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs snyan ngags mkhan chen slob dpon zla ba gzhon nus mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnam par bshad pa'i paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
rdzogs so
'phags pa nor rgyun ma'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa rdzogs so/
bcom ldan 'das nor rgyun ma'i sgrub thabs dang mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa dang smon lam dang bstod pa rnams rdzogs so/ /tshul 'di ni dpang lo tsA ba dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas zhol phug tu/ rgya dpe las bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'i yi ge pa dang bskul ba po ni dge ba'i bshes gnyen rin chen mtha' can yin no/
gtsang pa lo tsA ba'i phyag dpe las bris so//
dbyangs can gyi bstod pa 'di ni/ lho phyogs kyi rgyud du byung ba'i mkhas pa chen po paN+Di ta nag mo'i khol gyis dbyangs can ma'i zhal gzigs pa'i dus su dgyes te bstod pa rdzogs so/ /gang zhig 'di 'don pa la shes rab stsol bar khas blangs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta dz+nyA na shI la dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos 'bar gyis bsgyur ba'o/

slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ dkyil 'khor gyi chos mdor bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sangs rgyas gsang bas/ dbas many+dzu shrI dang / bran kha mu ti ta gnyis la brdzangs pa/ bod yul du lo tsA ba ka ba dpal brtsegs la sogs pas bsgyur ba'o//
gzhal yas khang gsal ba'i mngon rtogs mun sel sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon pad+ma 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshul gsum gyi sgron ma slob dpon chen po mtho btsun tri pi Ta ka ma la'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra varma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
de kho na nyid grub pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon zhi ba'i 'tsho'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ slad kyi paN+Di ta ku mA ra ka la sha dang / 'bro dge slong shAkya 'od kyis tshad ma'i skabs bcos shing gtan la 'phab po//
de kho na nyid la 'jug pa zhes bya ba bde gshegs pa'i bka' ma lus pa mdor bsdus te bshad pa'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon dpal ye shes grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma kA ra warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gsang sngags kyi tshul gyi snang ba zhes bya ba/ rdo rje slob dpon chen po mtho btsun btso yags kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma kA ra barma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
de kho na nyid kyi snying po bsdus pa/ slob dpon chos kyi dbang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza na rdA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
theg pa gsum rnam par bzhag pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po kr-iSh+Na pa dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud kyi don la 'jug pa bsdus pa slob dpon shrad+d+ha kA ra varmasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrad+d+ha kA ra varma dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje theg pa'i mtha' gnyis sel ba zhes bya ba slob dpon dz+nyA na shrIs bkod pa rdzogs so//
de nyid mthong ba'i lam dpal ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rngog bud+d+ha pA las bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o/ dpal shin kun tu tshogs 'khor sar gsol ba btab nas lha khang bi ha rar bsgyur ba'o//

theg pa chen po'i lam gyi rim pa zhes bya ba slob dpon bskal pa bzang po'i rdo rje zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ga ya d+ha ra dang / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gsang sngags la 'jug pa'i rab tu byed pa drug cu pa slob dpon dz+nyA na A ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta dz+nyA na A ka ra nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gsang sngags la 'jug pa'i rab tu byed pa drug pa'i 'grel ba paN+Di ta a tsar+ya dz+nyA A ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na A ka ra nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
theg pa chen po'i don bsdus pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kr-iSh+Na pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bla ma lnga bcu pa slob dpon chen po rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma kA ra war ma dang /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bla ma lnga bcu pa'i dka' 'grel 'di ni rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi mkhas pa chen po dpal nags kyi rin chen gyi bka' drin las/ legs pa sbyar ba'i skad kyis cha shes rig pa gzhon nu dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i dben gnas lha khang steng du bsgyur ba'o//
spyi'i dam tshig mdor bsdus pa/ dpal sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dam tshig chen po'i mdo rdzogs so//
tshul khrims dang sdom pa dang dam tshig mi 'gal ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po ye shes dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i mkhan po dz+nyA na shrI b+ha dra de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong blo gros snying po dang / dge slong rab zhi bshes gnyen gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
dam tshig thams cad bsdus pa zhes bya ba mkhas pa chen po dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rje btsun bla ma chen po de nyid kyi zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//

rgya gar shar phyogs dzA ga ta la'i paN+Di ta chen po bi b+hu ti tsan+d+rasa mdzad pa de rang 'gyur du mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje theg pa rtsa ba'i las kyi cho ga rnal 'byor gyi srog ces bya ba/ bla ma rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a b+h+yA ka ra gup+ta dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba tsa mi sangs rgyas grags pas glen skad du bsgyur ba'o//
zhen log sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mkhas pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon chen po 'gro bzang snying pos mdzad pa'i rnam thos sras kyi bde byed rtog pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta te sta ba dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong 'phags pa'i shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
slob dpon chen po 'gro bzang snying pos mdzad pa'i rnam thos sras kyi bde byed rtog pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta te sta ba dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong 'phags pa'i shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
rgyal po rnam thos sras kyi gsang ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dga' rab rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rgyal po chen po lus ngan po'i sgrub thabs/ sgrub pa brnyes pa'i slob dpon chen po dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /sgra ba chen po rgyal pa'i snyan la legs par zhus zhing / bstan bcos kyi skad cung zad shes pa'i lo tsA ba shA kyi'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos dpal thar pa gling gi gtsug lag khang du legs par bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon shu ram ga bar mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta te dza de ba dang / lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//



dngos grub brnyes pa'i paN+Di ta a mo g+ha badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so// slad kyi mkhan po dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA na dang lo tsA ba nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po chags pa rdo rje'i dam tshig gi bstod pa paN+Di ta
'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po chags pa rdo rje'i dam tshig gi bstod pa paN+Di ta dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta dI paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA na dang lo tsA ba nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
u tsush+ma sgrub pa'i thabs thun mong yin pa/ slob dpon sgeg pa rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po da na shi las bsgyur ba'o//
paN+Di ta a b+ha ka ra gup+tas mdzad pa'i u tsash+ma dza b+ha la sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta a lang ka de ba dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong tshul khrims 'byung gnas sbas pas/ chos 'khor shongs ma'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o/ slad kyis paN+Di ta ma hA bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra dang / chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing dag par bgyis so//
rgyal po Ar+ya ma tis mdzad pa rdzogs so// dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dpal rmugs 'dzin 'tshol pa nag po'i sgrub thabs/ gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba sbas pa'i bum pa zhes bya ba slob dpon nor sbyin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal chos kyi rje sa'i ster na 'gran zla dang bral ba'i paN+Di ta chen po shAkya b+ha dra dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bod yul dbus kyi bsam yas kyi gtsug lag khang du bsgyar ba'o//
dzam+b+ha la nag po'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa paN chen shAkya shrI'i zhal nas gsung pa/ bsnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi bsgyur ba'o//sa brgyad dbang phyug lha yi lha/ mgon po 'gro kun phong pa sel/ mi'u thung gzugs can nag po che/ utsuSh+ma la phyag 'tshal lo//zhes pa'i bstod pas bstod par bya'o//
'phags pa rmugs 'dzin chu'i dbang po la phrin las nyi shu'i sgo nas khyad par gyis bstod pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po nor 'dzin dpal gyi zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po bud+d+hA shra dz+nyA na dang lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis/ mang yul gyi grong du 'phags pa wa rti'i pho brang du bsgyur ba'o//
bcom ldan 'das rmugs 'dzin la bstod pa slob dpon chen po btsun pa zla bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po mu ti ta shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis legs par bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa rmugs 'dzin la bstod pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mi'i dbang po nyi ma rnam par gnon pas dzaM b+ha la la bstod pa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ka l+ya Na mi tra gzhon nu shes rab kyis bskul nas/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA d+ha ra dang / yar lungs pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis dpal ldan sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
rmugs 'dzin 'chol ba'i man ngag gi bstod pa/ bla ma d+ha byang chub sems dpas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha cig slob dpan nyi ma sbas pas mdzad zhes kyang zer ro//
paN+Di ta dza mA ris lha mo nor rgyun ma la bstod pa rdzogs so/ /dza mA ris 'gyur ro//
chos kyi rnam grangs 'di lha dang bcas pa'i lha dang bcas pa'i skye dgy'i yon gnas dam pa/ rje btsun gnas brtan chen po dpal zhwa dmar cod paN 'dzin pa bzhi pa'i bka ' bzhin zhwa lu lo tsa ba dge slong d+harma b_ha dras bsgyur ba'o//
gnod sbyin chen po gzhan gyis mi thub pa'i sgrub thabs kyi rgyud rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi ma dza mA ris bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon chen po sti ra ma tis dgongs pa las rdo rje bkod pa'i rgyud bstan pa bsrung ba/ rnal 'byor yongs kyi mgon po legs ldan nag po'i sgrub thabs kyi dkyil 'khor bdun gyi rim pa rnam par phye ba slob dpon snang mdzad myu gus mdzad pa rdzogs so//
pho brang skyid kyi byang mkhar du bla ma zhi ba'i blo gros kyi lung gis/ rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta a b+hi yuk+ta de ba shrI dang bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de d+harma yon tan gyis ji itar ji rnyed par bsgyur ba'o//
tshigs bcad 'di thams cad shi ha la'i dge slong nA ka taM gyis so//
grub thob brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i gsol 'debs/slob dpon rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa rdzogs so// paN+Di ta bai ro tsa na dang lo tsA ba shrI chos kyi grags pas bsgyur cig zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/
rgya gar lho phyogs kyi yul dpal ldan 'bras kyi phung po zhes bya'i mchod rten bzhugs pa'i gnas der/ bla ma man lungs pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi spyod pa rlabs po che/ byung chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar pa dang / cha mthun pa la mos pa'i paN+Di ta bi ma la shrI zhes bya ba mkhas shing btsun pa des tshigs su bcad pa 'dis bstod pa'o/ dpal ldan man lungs kyi gtsug lag khang chen por/ paN+Di ta go ta ma b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba grags pa byang chub gnyis kyis bsgyur ba'o/ bla ma'i bstod pa chos 'byung rab gzigs zhes bya ba lags so/ 'di ni thams cad kyis kha ton du gdon par bya'o//
maN+Dal gyi cho ga dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon mkhas pa chen po kam pa la'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /sngon gyi lo tsA ba chen po rnams kyis bsgyur ba ste 'gyur rnying lags skad do/ gsang sngags kyi theg pa'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga'o/ de ltar bsod nams kyi tshogs bsags pa gtso bor ston pa'i chos kyi sde tshan lags so//
maN+Dal bya ba'i cho ga dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /maN+Dal bya ba'i cho ga 'di ni pha rol tu phyin pa dang gsang sngags gnyis ka'i thun mong ba'o//
bla ma''i maN+Dal gyi cho ga'o//
maN+Dala dbul ba'i cho ga slob dpon chen po byang chub sems dpa' dgra las rgyal gsang ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a du lo pa dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
maN+Dal bya ba'i cho ga dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mtshan yongs su grags pa dge bshes rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa lags so/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa'i maN+Dal gyi go cha ga'o//
slob dpon srid gsum rnam par dag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i las dang po'i tshogs sogs bya ba'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa rdzogs so//
byang chub kyi gzhung lam zhes bgyi pa slob dpon mkhas pa chen po 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ji ltar mthong ba bzhin bsdus pa ste gzhung gi tshad ni sh+lo ka sum brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga'o/ dang po'i las kyi bya ba ma brten par nges par byang chub mchog thob mi nus kyang / rtsod dus skye bo stong pa nyid sma zhing / gzhung lam dang po'i las kyi bya ba rnams/ mi shes mi nus mi byed pa rnams mthong / spyod 'dod mi shes 'gro la phan 'dod nas/ thub pa'i dge slong chag ston lo tsA bas/ byang chub gzhung lam 'di ni 'bang pas bsgyur/ nyes kun bzod gsol dge bas bdag gzhan rnams/ sgrib bral tshogs gnyis rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shog /kha che'i mkhan po chen po chos kyi rje shAkya shrI b+ha dra las mnyan nas/ bod yul dbus kyi sde snod 'dzin pa chag lo tsa ba dge slong dgra bcom gyis bsgyur pa'o//
maN+Dala gyi cho ga kha che paN chen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gnubs byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
de kho na nyid bsdus pa'i man ngag /slob dpon shI la saM b+ha bas las dang po'i dor bsdus te mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rgyud sna tshogs las btus pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon dpal klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po slob dpon karma badz+ra'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
chos skyong thams cad pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon chen po ba ling A tsar+yas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon blo bzang seang+ge'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa gtor ma'i phreng ba 'di rdzogs so// rgya gar shar phyogs kyi dge slong dI bA ka ra dang lo tsA ba d+harma pA la b+ha dras dpal e waM chos 'khor du bsgyur pa'o//
paN+Di ta dI pam ka ra shrI dz+nya na dang / lo tsA ba dge bshes ston pas bsgyur ba'o//
gtor ma chen po'i las kyi rim pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon rdo rje mi bskyod pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po badz+ra kIrti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
cha gsum 'bring po'i cho ga nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje'i gdams ngag la brten nas paN+Di ta shrd+d+ha ka ra warmas nye bar sbyar ba rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon dza ya se nAsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
chu gtor gyi las byang rim par phye ba gsal bar bshad pa slob dpon shAkya mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus pa//
gtor ma'i 'grel pa slob dpon chen po bi dA dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAn+ti gar+b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba A tsaR+Ya rin chen mchog gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bdud rtsi 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad nas bsgyur ba ste lo tsA ba khu dngos grub kyis gtan la phab pa'o//
rkyen dang bar chad thams cad bzlog par byed pa yon tan thams cad nye bar sdud par byes pa chu gtor dri ma med pa'i gzhung / slob dpon dpal ma me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon de nyid la zhu ba po kan ston legs pa'i shes rab kyis tshogs bsogs pa'i yan lag tu zhus nas mang yul gya kyi grong du gzhung bris so/ paN+Di ta de nyed dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/
klu'i gtor chen sgrol ma'i zhabs kyi rdul la reg pa'i mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
bkra shis de yis khyed rnams la ni dbang mchog bskul zhes bya na slob dpon snang byed zla bas mdzad pa sangs rgyas sku gsum chos dang dge 'dun dang bcas pa'i bkra shis tshigs su bcad pa'o//
de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i bkra shis tshigs su bcad pa rdzogs so//
dpal rnal 'byor rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor gyi lha de bzhin gshesga ps rigs lnga 'khor dang bcas pa lha sum cu rtsa bcun gyi bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa rdzags so//
rje btsun 'phags ma sgrol mas gsungs pa'i bkra shis brgyad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi ma ya shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba 'dan ma tshul khrims seng+ges bsgyur ba'o//
bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa rdzogs so//

rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i bka' 'grel slob dpon nor bzangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kA ya s+tha pA ga ya d+ha ra'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya ye shes kyil bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i bka' 'grel de kho na nyid bstan par byed pa zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po nor bzangs kyis zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI 'ga' ya d+ha ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba gyi co zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba//
sangs rgyas rje btsun la rgyun chags kyi tshigs su bcad pas bstod pa/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kyogs kyi btsun pa rin chen bkra shis kyi bris//
mi pham mgon po la bstod pa 'chi slu ma zhes bya ba/ dpal 'jigs med grags pas sbyar ba'o//
de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la bstod pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon klu'i blo'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'o/ /paN+Di ta chen po mchog grub pa'i dbang phyug shrI ba na rat+na'i zhal snga nas dang / 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu'i zhabs kyi bka' drin las dge slong chos smra ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sdes bsgyur ba'o//
paN+Di ta chen po shrI ba na rat+na'i zhal snga nas kyi thugs kyi thugs dam ras bris la/ bla ma 'di dag gi sku brnyan bkod pa'i yi ge so so las/ dge slong rgyal mtsho'i sdes bsgyur ba'o//
dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi snying po'i rgya cher 'grel/ dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /sam pa la'i yul byon zhing / mngon par shes pa mnga' mnga' brnyes pa/ dus kyi 'khor lo pa zhes pa/ de'i rim ni brgyad pa dang / u rgyan yul skyes bram ze'i rigs/ na ro pa zhes bya ba ni/ nus pa skyes shing lhas gnang ba/ de'i rigs rgyud thos pa'i/ bla ma lha yi lhas bstan pa/ de mnyan rgya 'grel 'bad bsgyur pas/ mi 'dzags bde ba'i gnas thob shog /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI b+ha dra bo d+hi'i zhal snga nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de zla ba'i 'od zer gyis yon bdag zhing btsun dge slong gi phyir bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
dbang gi rab tu byed pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po zla ba mgon po dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyis bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o/ /'di bris dge ba yod pa des ni 'gro ba ma lus pa/ mi 'gyur bde ba thob par shog /dang po gnyis ni kun tu 'gro/ brgyad dang bcu gsum sku yin no/ gsum drug bdun dang bcu bzhi pa gsungs/ bzhi dgu bcu pa thugs su shes/ lnga bcu gcig ye shes so/ sprul pa la gnyis ste/ rang rgyud pa ni rgyal po grags pa ltar bu ste/ 'jam dpal dngos kyi sprul pa'o/ byin gyi rlabs kyi sprul pa ni/ nyi ma'i shing rta lta bu ste/ 'jam dpal gyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i sprul pa'o/ dus kyi 'khor lo 'dir ni/ 'di skad bdag gis thos pa zhes ma smos la/ dgyes rdor la sogs par ni 'di skad la sogs pa smos pa ni 'gal bar mi 'gyur te/ 'di dbang po rtul ba rnams la yab rgyab po zas gtsang ma dang / yum lha mo sgyur 'phrul ma'i sras su skye ba bzhes pa la bstan pa yin pa dang / dka' thub la sogs pa'i spyod pa bstan pa dang / saMsa kri ta'i skad kyis gsungs pa dang / 'di skad bdag gis zhes pa'i 'dul bar rka ba rnams la gsungs pa yin pa dang / yul sham b+ha la na gnas pa'i gang zag dbang po yang rab tu gyur pa'i gang zag de la theg pa chen po'i sned du rung ba'i rnams la/ zhu ba po phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa rgyal po zla ba bzang po dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dngos su byon nas chos gsungs pa'o/ de la kun mkhyen ye shes sku zhes pa ye shes nas sku bzhi'i bdag nyid can ltar yin no zhes gsungs so//
rang gi lta ba'i 'dod pa mdor bstan pa yongs su brtag pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs mi'i dbang po grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gzhung gi tshad ni shaulka brgyad cu rtsa brgyad lhag pa'i drug brgya'i grangs so/ 'di ni sgra dang mngon brdzod la sogs pa tha snyad kyi gtsug lag rnams la blo'i snang ba cher rgyas pa bal po'i paN+Di ta many+dzu shrI dang / mkhas pa'i dbang po dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa'i bka' drin la brten nas/ lo tsA ba gtogs pa shAkya'i dge slong chos grags dpal bzang pos dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang chen por/ gangs ri'i khrod du sngon chad ma byung ba 'di legs par bsgyur ba'o/ /'gran phyir ma yin grags pa 'dod phyir min/ ston dang bstan bcos dag la gus phyir dang / dam pa 'ga' yi bka' yis bskul ba'i phyir/ gangs can khrod na sngon chad med 'di bsgyur/ 'di las bskrun pa'i dge ba ci mchis pa/ de yang 'gro ba'i byang chub don du bsngo/ bdag kyang gang la gang 'dul skad rnams kyis/ mtha' yas 'gro la dam chos ston pa shog /bod la bka' drin che ba 'jig rten mig /kun gyi phyi mo 'thon mi sma b+ho Tasa/ mdzad pa'i yi ge'i gzugs dang brda mkhas pa'i/ ye ge pa dag gi kyang 'di rtogs shog / rnam par shes pas dpyod pa la/ rnam par g.yeng bas g.yengs pa'i phyir/ rnam par ma dag mchis srid na/ rnam par byang ba rnams la bshags/ /slar yang bzang ldan dben pa'i gnas su rgya dpe dang gtugs pa'i zhus dag kyang grub par bgyis so//
rgyud man ngag thams cad kyi don phyogs cig tu sdebs pa thabs lam man ngag rdo rje tshig gi rnam par dbye ba ces bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta don yod rdo rjes mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi sgrub chen ti phu gsang sngags kya sdong po'i drung du/ bod kyi rnal 'byor pa ras chung rdo rje grags pas zhus shing spyan drangs pa las/ slad kyi paN+Di ta d+ha na shi la'i drung du bal po mcho kha ras pas zhus te spyan drangs pa'o//
gnyis su med pa'i rnal 'byor ces bya/ dang po'i sangs rgyas kyis bsgrub pa/ slob dpon chen po shrI ka la tsakra ra ti pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dus kyi 'khor lo zhabs chung ngu dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba tsa mi sangs rgyas grags pas bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ grub pa'i skyes mchog bla ma rin po che sangs rgyas yar byon gyi zhabs kyi pad mo rnyog pa med pa la/ bdag dbon dpal gyi gus par btu de zhus pa'o//
ces tshigs bcad bcu pa zhes bya ba lam gyi rim pa'o/ /slob dpon bud+d+ha gup+tasa nye bar sbyar ba'o/ bla ma de nyid la legs par brten cing nyan nas/ slar yang de nyid kyi slob ma pur+Na badz+ra la zhus te tA ra nA thas bsgyur ba'o//
zhal nas snyan du rgyud pa'i gdam ngag yab dang 'grel pa'i dal rgyas par sgom pa'i lam thun mongs ma yin pa/ mkha' 'gro'i gsung bzhin bla ma'i bka' lung ma nyams par kha che'i paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po 'jigs med grags pas mdzad pa'i yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba/ de'i rgyas pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po na ro pa de nyid kyi zhal mnga' nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyis/ pu la ha ri'i dgon pa ru zhus zhing gtan la phab pa'o/ slad nas bsod nams snyoms pa mi bskyod pas kyang legs par bcos pa'o//
bcom ldan 'das dpal bde mchog nam mkha'i lding gi bsgrub thabs/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po pradz+nyA rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal pa'i mkhan po mu ti ta shrI dz+nya'i zhal mnga' nas/ a tsaR+Ya mar pa chos kyi dbang phyag gis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon 'gar pa ri pas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
dpa' bo cig pa'i sbyin bsreg rdzogs so//
dpa' bo cig pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon gar pa ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so
slob dpon mdzes dgas mdzad pa'i rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ti ta chen po/ su ma ti kIrti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong pradz+nyA kIrtisa bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon pun+d+ha ri a nan das mdzad pa/ sbyin bsreg gi cho ga le'u rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sa bi ta chen po su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong seng rgyal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
'khor lo bde mchog lhan cig skyes pa'i bsgrub thabs/ bla ma brgyad pa'i man ngag gis brgyan pa yan lag bcu pa zhes bya ba 'di ni/ chos smra ba'i btsun pa 'phags pa zhes bya ba la/ yu gur gyi yul du skyes pa'i ban d+he/ mngon pa'i sde snod 'dzin pa saM g+ha mi Ta zhes bya bas gsol ba btab pa'i ngor sbyar ba'o//
dpa' bo cig pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po Doma b+hi he ru kas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal bde mchog 'khor lo'i bsgrub thabs/ snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa'i rim pa/ dpal na ro pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta shrI na ro pa chen po dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi blo gros bdag gi zhus te bsgyur ba'o//
zhes pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rim pa lnga pa u rgyan nas byung ba rdzogs so/ /slob dpon mkhas pa rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'o/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po kriSh+Na paN+Di ta dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba las/ phyis bla ma chen po sum ti kIrti dang/ dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bcos pa'o/ slar yang shar phyogs san+ta ga ra'i mkhas pa chen po dpal nags kyi rin po che'i zhal sngar pan chen sangs rgyas dbyangs kyi man ngag dang sbyar nas gus par mnyan te/ rgya dpe gnyis dang bstun nas bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba dbang po'i sde zhes bgyi bas g.yar khral tsam du zhus chen bgyis so//
dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bcu gsum ma'i bdag nyid kyi dbang bskur ba'i cho ga slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po A tsaR+Ya dz+nyA na badz+ra'i zhabs pa/ bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po zhang zhung gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab po//
rdo rje theg pa'i rtsa ba dang yan lag gi ltung ba'i bshags pa/ slob dpon in+d+ra bo d+his mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bcom ldan 'das bde mchog la mchog thun mong gi dngos grub brnyes pa/ shrI dzA lan+d+ha ra pas bstod pa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i rgyu mtshan bstan pa/ na ro paN chen gyis zhal mnga' nas gsungs pa/ mar pas bsgyur ba'o//
spra khrid lung bstan te lo dus gsum mkhyen pa'i gsungs rdzogs so//
tor mas mchod pa'i cho ga'o/ rgya gar gyi mkhas pa chen po/ dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
chos drug rdo rje'i tshig rkang zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma'i zhal nas lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o/ bdag khyung po rnal 'byor pas gser srang lnga brgya phul nas zhus te nyams su myong bar byas pa'i/ phyis tho ling du lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos gtan la phab pa'o//
rang shar phyag rgya chen po'i rdo rje'i tshig rkang rdzogs so/ /mkha' 'gro ma de nyid mnyes par byas te/ gser srang lnga brgya phul nas zhu/ lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
chos spyod mi dge rang grol zhes bya ba/ sgrub chen ra hU las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi grub thob ra hU la badz+ra'i zhal snga nas/ lo tsA ba chos kyi blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'di ni gsang sngags mthar thug mchog /bcom ldan 'das bde mchog sku gsung thugs kyi sgrub thabs/ ye shes mkha' 'gro ni gu mas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bdag khyung po rnal 'byor pas seng ldan 'thug po'i nags gseb tu mkha' 'gro ma'i zhal gdams rnams/ ta la'i lo ma la rdzed dor bris nas ga'ur bcangs te lus dang ma bral par byas so//
bde mchog lha lnga'i ting nge 'dzin dbang bskur ba'i cho ga /ye shes kyi Da ki ma ni gu mas sdom pa rgya mtsho'i rgyud las phyung ba'o/ /rdzogs so/ bdag khyung po rnal 'byor pas mkha' 'gro ma de nyid mnyas par byas nas zhus pa'o/ lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyi bsgyur ba'o//
rang shar phyag rgya chen po'i rdo rje'i tshig rkang rdzogs so/ /ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma de nyid mnyes par byas te/ gser srang lnga brgya phul nas zhus so/ lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
rang shar phyag rgya chen po'i rdo rje'i tshig rkang rdzogs so/ /ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma de nyid mnyes par byas te/ gser srang lnga brgya phul nas zhus so/ lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
rang grol phyag rgya chen po zhes bya ba ye shes mkha' 'gro ma ni gu mas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
khyad 'phags lam khyer gyi chos gsum zhes bya ba/ yes shes kyi DA ki mas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba glan dar ma bla gros kyis bsgyur ba'o/ DA ki de nyid la gser srang lnga brgya phul nas zhus te/ bdag khung po rnal 'byor pas nyams su myong bar byas pa'o//
rgyu ma lam gyi rim pa dri med snying po zhes bya ba/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma ni gu mas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma de nyid dang / lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o/ slad nas khyung po rnal 'byor pas zhus te nyams su myong bar bgyis pa'o//
sgyu ma lam gyi rim pa'i don 'grel/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma ni gu mas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma de nyid dang / lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o/ slad nas bdag khyung po rnal 'byor pas zhus te nyams su myong bar byas pa'o//
ni gu ma'i zhal gdams so//
ni gu ma'i zhal gdams so//
rdo rje gar gyi gdams ngag 'di/ ye shes mkha' 'gro'i gdam ngag go/
mkha' 'gro ma'i zhal gdams rdzogs so//
de yan gmkha' 'gro ma'i zhal gdmas so//
'phags pa smon lam gyi rgyal po ye shes kyi Da ki ni/ ni gu mas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
zhes pa bcu gsum gyi bdag nyid can gyi dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga 'di ni dpal ba na rat+na'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /'di ni phyogs thams cad la rnam par rgyal ba'i blo gros can bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sdes kun sum+b+ha'i ka pa ra'i me tog dang bcas te bskul ba las/ rje grub pa'i dbang phyug de nyid kyi 'bangs su gyur pa gzhon nu dpal zhes bya bas ljang phu bkra shis dgon pa'i dben gnas su sgyur pa'o/ slar yang lo tsA ba chen po de nyid kyis paN+Di ta nyid kyi zhal sngar gtugs la dag par byos shig ces bkas bskul ba las/ rje btsun dam pa yab sras kyi bka' drin gyis 'tsho ba'i rgyal khams pa bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde zhes bya bas/ bal yul ye rang gi grong khyer gyi 'dab dpal go bi tsan+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang chen por/ rje grub pa'i dbang phyug nyid kyis spyan sngar zhib tu mnyan zhing gtan la phab ste/ shin tu dag par bgyis la shu b+ha ma stu sarba dza ga taM//
bi muk+ta many+dza ri zhes bya ba don dom pa'i glu dbyangs bde ba mnyam pa nges par byed pa rgyud thams cad kyi yi ge mchog dang ldan pa mchog gi dngos grub thob pa'i slob dpon chen po dang po'i mgon po dzA lan d+ha ra'i zhabs kyi'o/ aM ka yang bshad pa/ lho phyogs kyi rgyud du 'khrungs pa rje btsun bud+d+ha gup+ta dang / shar phyogs kyi slob dpon chen po sa rgya nA tha dang / bla ma chen po kam+ba la narbI Na shrI rnams kyi zhal snga dang bod kyi dge slong rmongs pa kun dga' snying pos g.yar khral du 'tshal ba'o//
de nyid bdun gyi 'grel pa 'bad de byas/ ces pa ni de kho na nyid bdun gyi 'grel pa shar phyogs kam+ba la ba dang gnyis su ma mchis pa/ sangs rgyas sbas pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'o/ rdo rje slob dpon chen po gu ru lho phyogs pa de nyid dang / kun dga' snying pos g.yar khral du 'tshal ba'o//
dpal ldan rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dril bu zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i dpal sdom pa'i man ngag 'di ni rdzogs so/ /lugs gnyis kyi dbang phyug dam pa dpal ldan rnam rgyal grags pa'i gsung gis mkhas pa gnas brtan chen po/ dpal gyis nags kyi rin chen gyi spyan sngar/ 'gos lo tsA ba gzhin nu dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
bcu gsum gyi bdag nyid can dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i cho ga dril bu zhabs kyis mdzad pa 'di ni rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po dpal nags kyi rin chen gyi spyan sngar/ 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal gyi gtsang rong ra lnga'i dge gnas su bsgyur ba'o//
dpal 'khor lo sdom pa la bstod pa 'di/ grub pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor pa mi bskyod rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang gi bya ba 'di ni slon dpon chen po mi bskyod rdo rjes mdzad pa'o/ /sems can gyi don du yes shes kyi mkha' 'gro mas sgra rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
bcom ldan 'das bde mchog 'khor lo'i bstod pa/ dan da ka zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bir+ya b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
dz+nyA na shrI'i mngon par rtogs pa'i snying po/ bla ma kha che dgon pa bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dz+nyA na shrI mi tra ho'i/ mngon par rtogs pa'i 'grel pa rnam par bshad pa'i snying po zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta kha che rnam gnyis kyis gsung/ lo tsA ba chen po dge slong 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug rnams kyis gtsug go nor bu lta bu dpal lU yis pas mdzad pa'i 'khor lo sdom pa'i mngon par rtogs pa'i 'grel pa grub pa brnyes pa'i slob dpon la ba'i na bza' can gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta slob dpon chen po nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje'i dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon b+hu su kus mdzad pa'i bde mchog 'khor lo'i Ti ka rdzogs so//
bde mchog 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon b+hu su kus mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'chi ba bslu ba'i cho ga /slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dge slong shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba'o//
sangs rgyas 'byung ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ dpal lU i pa yis zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dpal De ki pa'i zhabs kyis zhu chen bgyis pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs grong khyer dom pa'i paN+Di ta chen po shrI ba na rat+ni zhal nas mnga' dang / lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes zhes bya bas sgyur ba'o//
dbang bzhi pa'i rnam par bzhag pa/ paN+Di ta chen po shrI ba na rat+na'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'o/ /dam pa de nyid kyis drung du nye bar btugs te zhus pa las/ chos 'khor lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes zhes bya bas bsgyur ba'o//
slon dpon nag po'i zhal snga nas kyi mdzad pa'i ba san ta ti la la zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta g+ha ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lha btsas kyis bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal rdo rje rnal 'byor ma lhan cig skyes kyi gsang ba'i sgrub thabs/ shin tu sba ba'i gnas gyur pas/ rdo rje 'chang dang mkha' 'gro ma'i/ zhal las rab tu rnyed nas ni/ bla ma te lo pa'i thugs la byon pa/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug mkhas pa na ro pa chen pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i skyed rdzogs/ mchi med kyi man ngag dang bcas pa/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta sha ri pu tras zhal nas gsungs pa bzhin/ blo gros bstan pa bzhi pas bsgyur nas bris pa'o//
shes rab snang ba'i sgrub pa'i thabs/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje phag mos rjes su bzung ba'i slob dpon chen po ko kas sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen mo nor bu dpal ye shes dang / lo tsA ba chag dge slong chos rje dpal gyis sgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa rdzogs so//
mkha' spyod dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta di paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
dpal rdo rje phag mo shes rab gsal byed ces bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ dngos grub rnyes pa'i slob dpon ko taM dad tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi ma hA paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ti'i zhal snga nas/ lo tsA ba dge slong grub pa dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
dpal ldan na ro pa'i zhabs kyi mdzad pa/ mar pa chos kyi bla gros kyis bsgyur ba rdzogs so/ /gzhung don gsal byed chan bu 'di/ phyogs mes lo tsAsa gsal bar bkod//
dpal rdo rje DA ki ma'i gsang ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon sing g+ha la pa'i gdams pa/ a tsaR+Ya dmar po zhabs kyis gnang pa/ mkhas pa brgya'i thugs dam/ zhig po bde 'bar la brgyud pa/ sa ma ya tha mi ti//
rnal 'byor ma drug gi sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrtis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon chen po ra tri tas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs dpal gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa lha bcu gsum pa rdzogs so//
rig pa 'dzin ma rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza ya zhabs dang / btsun pa dar ma yon tan gyi bsgyur ba'o//
zhes bya ba ni mang ngag gyi rdo rje phag mo rig ba 'dzin ma rtsen ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bA rA hI mchod pa'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba gnyis su mde pa'i ye shes rdo rje'i zhal sngas mdzad pa'o//
rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rim pa lnga pa zhes bya ba rngon pa'i gdams ngag rdzogs so/ /rje btsun bud+d+ha gup+ta'i zhal snga nas dang kun dga' snying pos g.yar khral du 'tshal ba'o//
slob dpon chen po gup+ta na tha dang / rgyal khams pas sgyur ba'o//
slob dpon chos skyong gi zhal lnga'i rim pas snyan ngag mkhan chen rtse ba can gyis mdzad pa rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta pur+Na n+ta dang ta ra nA this bsgyur ro//
dpal dgyes rdora'i bka' 'grel lha sgom pa rin po che sbyor ba'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po dam tshig rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta chen po nag po'i zhal snga nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba 'gos lha tshas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gsang ba'i mdzod ces bya ba/ 'gu ru mtsho'i skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta gnya' na shrI dang / dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dpal dgyes pa'i rdo rje'i gtor ma'i cho ga /slob dpon chen po shrI a nan+da badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
phyag rgya bzhi yi sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI ga ya d+ha ra dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba gyi co zla ba'i zer gyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sang ba ming gi dbang du byas pa yang dag pa'i man ngag bgrad par dkar ba'i slob dpon phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub can 'bir ba ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ga ya d+ha ra dang / dge slong shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba'o/ /yang slad kyi rgyal bu sprin shugs can gyis zhal snga nas dang bod kyi lo tsA ba 'gos lha btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon 'gar pa ri bas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
pal mchog tu gyur pa'i ngo bo nyid bde ba chen po'i go 'phang rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin rdzogs so/ /slob dpon rta mchog zhabs kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa//
slob dpon dam tshig rdo rjes mdzad pa lhan cig skyis pa grub pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po krish+Na paN+Di ta dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas sgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o// (gzhung 'di rje btsun grags pa'i kyai rdor gyi dkar chag na nag po'i skor la rdzogs rim gyi gzhung gcig yod gsung ba de ka yin/ sngar bstan 'gyur du ma chung ngor chen sogs sa skya pa phyi ma rnams kyi ma rnyed gsungs pa yin/ 'di'i dpe rnying bdag kun dga'i snying po'i lag du byon/ gdam ngag sa lugs ni da lta med bzhan yong / lan tshwa mchog gyur tu grags pa de yin/ bdag gi thob bo)
zhes pa rgyud kyi rgyal po dgyes pa rdo rje'i lus kyi don rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po rigs pa'i brtul zhugs spyod pa shan+ti gup+tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mkhas pa chen po gang ba'i rdo rje las zhus te/ phyis rgya dpe'i steng nas/ rmongs pa tA ra nA thas g.yar khral du bsgyur ba'o//

cung zad dran pa zhes bya ba/ bsdus pa'i don gyi yan lag rdzogs so/ /zhes slob dpon chen po shan+ti gup+tas gsungs pa'i nges pa tshig tu sbyar ba'o/ rgya gar gyi mkhas pa pur+Na badz+ra las dus dang por ring du sbyangs shing mnyan te rgyal khams pa tA ra nA thas dus phyis dpe las g.yar khral du bsgyur ba'o//
ces pa slob dpon chen po dpal ldan bde ba chen po'i rdo rjes nye bar sbyar ba/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i snying po rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i sgrub thabs sbyor ba mdor bsdus zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /yul gu dzi ra ta'i mkhas pa chen po pur+Na badz+ra las zhus te/ rgyal khams pa tA ra na thas bsgyur ba'o//
sgron me gcig pa slob dpon bya da la pa das mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ces pa ni dgyes pa rdo rje'i man ngag dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon ku sA las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gya gar gyi slob dpon bud+d+ha gup+ta'i zhal snga nas dang / dge tshul kun dga' snying pos bsgyur ba'o//
dgyes pa'i rdo rje'i man ngag gsal ba a sig+hana zhes bya ba dang po log pa'i lam la zhugs pa'i spyod pa pa byad la'i gdams pa'i dngos grub brnyes pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'o/ /yul lho phyogs kyi rgyud du 'khrungs pa/ pan grub kyi bla ma dam pa mang po'i zhal lung gis thugs sim pa las rdo rje 'chang gi sa gnas brnyes pa/ rje btsun bud+d+ha gup+ta nA tha'i zhal las byung pa ltar/ dgyes pa'i rda rje'i man ngag ku sA las mdzad pa dang / sgron me gcig pa dang / rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa rnams kyang kun dga' snying pos g.yar khral du bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon rA hU la badz+ra'i zhal snga nas zla ba'i snying po la gdams pa rdzogs so//
de kho na nyid bzhi pa Dom+bisa pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi slob dpon bud+d+ha gup+ta'i zhal sngar man ngag tsam mnos shing / slad kyi paN+Di ta nirba na shrI'i spyan sngar/ mar me mdzad dpal gyi 'grel pa dang stun te sgyur ba'o/ sngon 'di la rdo rje'i tshig bsdus pa chung ba zer/ na ro pa'i slob dpon rgyun rnams nyan bshad byed pa dang / badz+ra pA Ni'i phyag rgya bzhi pa la/ rdo rje tshig bsdus che ba zer/ mai tri pa'i slob ma rnams 'chad nyan byed pa byung ba yin lags//
lag tu bslang ba'i rim pa slob dpon zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bdag med lha mo bco lnga la bstod pa slob dpon chen po bsod snyoms pa 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ces pa slob dpon bde ba chen po'i zhal gyi man ngag stobs kyi 'khor lo bsgom pa'i thabs rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta pur+Na badz+ra dang / tA ra nA thas bsgyur ba'o//
rje btsun ma ku ru ku l+le'i sgrub thabs mang du thos pa'i slob dpon ku ma ra bo des mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rje btsun sgrol ma khams gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i bsgrub thabs yon tan gzungs can/ slob dpon po dge slong klu grub kyis mdzad pa las/ dus phyis shAkya'i dge bsnyen brtul zhugs spyod pa'i bai ro tsa na badz+ra'i zhal snga nas/ ra bsgyur du bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
ku ru ku l+le'i las sbyor gyi man ngag paN+Di ta don yod rdo rjes bla ma ba ri lo tsA ba la gnang ngo / 'di la shin tu dam par mdzad nas mang po la spel ba'i srol med do/ gsang ngo sbas so//
ku ru ku l+le'i bsgrub thabs/ ma tang ki pas mdzad pa rdzogs so
bla ma'i man ngag rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba rin chen rdo rjes bsgyur ba'o//
rje btsun ku ru ku l+le la bstod pa phrin las nye bar bskul ba zhes bya ba mkhas pa chen po dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rnal 'byor ma mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba rtsod pa'i dus su byung ba grub pa'i slob dpon zhi ba sbas pas mdzad pa'o/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta nir bA Na shra dang / rmongs pa tA ra na tha 'am/ ming gzhan kun dga' snying pos bsgyur ba'o//

bdud rtsi thigs pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mtsho kyes rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma'i thod phreng gi zhal snga nas/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dz+nyA na ku ma ras bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa thabs kyi zhags pa pad+mo'i phreng gi 'grel pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa dpal gsang ba'i snying po zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa rin po che'i spar khab ces bya ba rdzogs so/ /thugs dam 'di/ dbus pa gnyan chung pas lus sems btud de bris pa'o//
dpal gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ slob dpon nyi ma'i seng ge'i 'od kyis mdzad pa'i rgya cher bshad pa'i 'grel pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po pra swa ta la/ sgyur byed kyi lo tsA ba pad+ma ru tshes gsang ba'i dbang mnos nas bsgyur te/ dge bar shog//
sgyu 'phrul dra ba rdo rje las kyi rim pa zhes bya ba/ dngos po gnyis pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje sems dpa'i rgyu 'phrul dra ba'i dbang gis rgyal po rdzogs so//
dbang gi don nges par 'byed pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa'o//
sgyu 'phrul thugs kyi thigs pa rdzogs so//
gsang ba'i thigs pa'i man ngag slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i shes pa'i mtshan nyid bshad pa/ shes rab spyan 'byed ces bya ba/ bi ma las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
man ngag gyi rgyal po lta ba'i phreng ba rdzogs so//
las shan lta ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ bzhad pa rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
lta ba'i rim pa yi man ngag /dka' ba dpal brtsegs kyis mdzad pa/ snang ba bcu bdun rdzogs so//
g.yu'i thang ma kras dgu rdzogs so/ /bi ma las phan yul du gnya' la gtad do//
sgyur 'phrul dra ba me long lta bu'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po dz+nyA na dza yas mdzad pa'o//
gyu 'phrul dra ba'i skyed pa'i rim pa ting nge 'dzin/ dkyil 'khor lnga'i dbang du sbyar ba/ 'od kyi rim pa zhes bya ba'i man ngag /slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa'i man ngag rdzogs so//
slob dpon bi ma las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rin chen dra ba mngon rdzogs zhes bya ba mthar phyin pa'o//
dra ba chung ngu rdzogs so//
de kho na nyid snang ba dam pa rgyan rdzogs so//
mang yul khri babs su/ dz+nyA na ku ma ras bsgyur ba/ lam rnam par bkod pa/ sangs rgyas gsang ba'i man ngag rdzogs so//
man ngag rnam par bkod pa rdzogs so//
thugs kyi thigs pa las/ bde gshegs kyi snang ba'i le'u ste/ bzhi pa'o/ rgyu phrul spyi gcod rdzogs so/ /sangs rgyas gsang bas dang bi ma la mi tras dang sgeg pa rdo rjes mdzad pa'o/ rma rin chen mchog gi bsgyur ba'o//
sgyu 'phrul man ngag gsal ba'i sgron me rdzogs so//
sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i lam bshad pa/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rim pa drug pa/ slob dpon sgeg pa rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i man ngag gi rim pa gsum pa rdzogs so
sems bskyed pa'i cho ga mdor bshad pa rdzogs so//
dam tshig gsal bkra zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po sgeg pa rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dam tshig phra rgyas bstan pa rdzogs so//
sgyu 'phrul sbyin sreg gi rim pa mdor bsdus pa slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sgyu 'phrul dra ba ro sreg las kyi phreng ba rdzogs so/ slob dpon bi ma mi tras mdzad pa'o//
sgyu 'phrul dpe chung rang gnas kyi rim pa'o/ sgeg pa rdo rje mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sku gdung las kyi phreng ba rdzogs so//
za tshogs gtor ma'i lung rdzogs so
gsang ba'i mdo don bsdus pa/ slob dpon d+harma bo d+his mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon sti ra ma ti sbyar ba'i/ skabs 'grel bye brag rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
byang chub sems kyi ljon shing / sti ra ma tis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po sti ra ma tis/ ye ge'i gzhung rgyud phyi nang las/ nges don mdo bsdus te mdzad pa/rgyan dam pa'i le'u/ bam po gcig du byas pa rdzogs so/ /cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ skad phyi mo dang thug pa'o//

'phags pa rtogs pa'i rgyal po rdo rje sems dpa' sgru 'phrul dra ba le'u stong phrag brgya pa las/ mtshan nyid dang brgyud thams cad kyi lung gi spyi/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ thams cad ma lus par 'phros te 'khor lo bskor ba de dag gis 'bras bu'i mchog gi rgyud kyi don sdus 'grel pa piN+Dir tha zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi slob dpon chen po bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa'o/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba chen po a tsaR+Ya rma rin chen mchog dang / gnyags dz+nyA na ku mA ras dpal bsam yas dbu rtse'i bar khang du bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges par las/ bro gar dang rtse 'jo'i li'u ste zhes pa/ le'u mtshan 'grel pa'o/ le'u sum cu gsum pa'i spyan rnam par 'grel pa'o//

slob dpon chen po shrI sid+ha yis thugs kyi sgo lcags dbye ba'i don bkrol ba'o/ rdzogs so//
bsre ba'i cho ga'i tho byang yin/ slob dpon bi ma la las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mtshan nyid sgron ma rdzags so//
sgyur 'phrul dra ba khro ba'i dkyil 'khor dbang rab gnas kyi bsgrub thabs/ khro bo rdo rje las rim/ bud+ha g+hu h+yas mdzad pa 'di yongs su rdzogs so//
dbang gi gal po'i don 'grel rdzogs so/ /khri dang 'bum la gcig 'ga' 'byung pa la/ man ngag rdzogs pa'i dbang bskur bya phyir bkrol/ gsum las mangs na rdo rje dmyal bar byed/ 'das na rdo rje sems dpa' nyid kyang 'tshig /gter du bcang ngo / rtsa 'grel gnyis ka sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa gnyags dz+nyA na'i 'gyur ro//
sgyu phrul dra ba lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes snang ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /sgeg pa rdo rje mdzad pa/ ban d+he dz+nyA na ku ma ras bsgyur ba'o//
sgyu 'phrul 'jam pa'i thigs pa/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gsang ba'i thigs pa man ngag rdzogs so/ /slob dpon chen po bi ma las mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba gnya' dz+nyA na ku ma ras bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
dbang cig car 'jug pa'i man ngag rdzogs so//
bde chen phyag rgya'i man ngag /gzhan lus shes rab kyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba rdzogs so//
sgeg rdo rje mdzad pa rgyun bshags so
tshigs rkang bcu dgu ni bi ma la yis lung du bstan / rdzogs so//
sgyu 'phrul dra ba rab tu gnas kyi cho ga rnam par bsres pa gsum dang sbyar ba/ slob dpon rgyal ba bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal gsang ba'i snying po'i rim pa gnyis kyi don/ rgyal po in tra b+hu d+hisa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon bi ma la mi tras/ zhang dz+nyA na la gnang / rgyud thams cad kyi 'grel pa/ lung dam pa'i bcud/ man ngag mtha' dag gi snying po/ rnal 'byor gyi lam dam pa/ log pa'i rtog pa zhi bar byed pa/ zhi ba rtog pa'i lha rgyud do//
sgyu 'phrul tshogs kyi 'khor lo/ thugs kyi sgrub pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon bi ma la'i slob ma/ rgyal ba bzang po dpal sbas pas/ yul me ga d+hara gshegs pa'i dus su mdzad pa/ 'od kyi phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i sgyu 'phrul rdzogs so/ /'phan yul gyi brag khung du bi ma la mi tras/ dz+nyA na ku ma ra la bka' stsal te/ bsdus pa la mos pa'i don du bsgyur ba'o//
khro bo las kyi 'phreng ba bsdus pa yis/ kun kyang tshogs chen sa thob shog/
khro bo yang dag sgron ma/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon bi ma las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
phyag rgya bzhi pa'i bsam gtan rdzogs so
dpal chen kun bzang sku gsung thugs/ bsgrub thabs rnal 'byor phreng ba'i don/ bdag dang gzhan phyir bris pa yi/ mtha' yas 'khor lo'i sa thob shog/
spyod yul sbyong ba'i bsam gtan/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/
bcom ldan 'das bde bar gshegs pa thams cad 'dus pa'i thugs rdze dbang thob/ :mdzad pa lha'i tshe 'dra la: phrin las mthar phyin sgrub pa: gsang sngags nges pa'i don gsal bar byed pa'i sgron ma: lung thams cad kyi rgyal po rdzogs so: rgya gar gyi mkhan gyi slob dpon chen po pad+ma 'byung gnas dang:bod kyi lo tsA ba bai ro tsa na bdag gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i gtor ma'i cho ga / rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug ku ku ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
byA da le'i mang ngag go//
slob dpon byA la'i zhabs dngos grub brnyes pas mdzad pa d+harma'i zhal snga nas kyi rim pa dpal sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i man ngag rdzogs so/ ma hA ma ya'i man ngag dang po 'di rgyal ba kun gyi ngo bo bud+ha nA tha'i gsung las tA ra nA thas bsgyur ba'o/ phyi ma'i gu ru'i rdo rje'i spun ni wANa shrI las glegs baM steng nas zhus pa'o//
slob dpon byA la'i zhabs dngos grub brnyes pas mdzad pa d+harma'i zhal snga nas kyi rim pa dpal sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i man ngag rdzogs so/ ma hA ma ya'i man ngag dang po 'di rgyal ba kun gyi ngo bo bud+ha nA tha'i gsung las tA ra nA thas bsgyur ba'o/ phyi ma'i gu ru'i rdo rje'i spun ni wANa shrI las glegs baM steng nas zhus pa'o//
rgya gar gyi shar phyogs kyi slob dpon ga go na shrI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rdo rje dril thabs kyi skabs su/ bcwa' ba'i dus su mi gsor/ gcu ba'i dus su mi bsdams/ bgyid pa'i dus su mi 'tshom/ bsdu ba'i dus su mi baspro/ steng tshangs pa lha'i zhal mi lta/ 'og klu'i greng khyer mi gzhom/ phyogs bzhi'i rgyal chen gyi rgyal sa mi 'phrog/ phyag rgya dngos kyi skabs su slob dpon ga go la shrI las mdzad pa'i bstan bcos 'di tsam/ slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen gyis/ ko sa la la sogs bar bstan pa ltar/ byang chub mchog dang /sa la rag pa la sogs pa'o/ 'jam dbyangs dge'o/ man lungs dus 'khor ba rad na (rat+na)shrI la'i phyag dpe las gtugs shing dag par byas so/



gyud kyi rgyal po chen po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ mkhas pa chen po rdo rje slob dpon 'phags pa kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa/ le'u bcu bdun pa rdzogs so/ /yul yo ti bsod nams lhun grub rin chen brtsegs pa'i gzhal yas khang du/ paN+Di ta chen po 'phra ras kyis/ 'bral byams pa'i shes rab dang / gnyan byang chub tshul khrims gnyis kyi don du bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//


bsdus pa'i rim pa'i bsgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po dpal klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsar+ya shad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ slad kyi rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po re ben+ta'i zhal snga nas/ chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis ma g+ha d+ha'i dpe ltar legs par bcos shing gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i man ngag kha che'i paN+Di ta na ro pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po rig pa brtul zhugs kyi spyod pa mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor pa/ dpal no ro chen po dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyis/ dpal pu la ha ri me tog brtsegs pa'i dgon par gus shing legs par bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o/ /gsang ba 'dus pa'i man ngag phyin ci ma log pa 'di ni AR+Ya pra ba pen+d+ha bas dpal dge sding gi gtsug lag khang du bris so//
rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po 'phags pa klu sgrubs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /'di ni thams cad mkhyen pa rang ston chos rje'i bka' bskul ba las/ rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po shrI ba na rat+na'i zhabs dang / stag tshang lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyis bsgyur ba'o//
de kho na nyid rin po che snang ba'i rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
go 'phang snang ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gshin rje gshed nag po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a du la da sa dang /lo tsA ba dge slong 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
