dpon mkhas pa dngal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta shan ti b+hang tra dang /lo tsha ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la pab pa// mchan : bstan 'gyur skabs la lar paN+Di ta shan ti b+had tra dang skabs la lar shan ti b+hang hra sogs 'khor par snang yang don dngos thog rgya gar gyi mkhan po shan+ti b+ha dra 'am mtshan gzhan zhi ba bzan gpo'am nag po zhi ba bzang po yin snang bas dpyad par 'tshal/
'khor lo'i tshogs gsal bar byed pa'i/ de kho na nyid bsdus pa/ bsod snyoms pa bud d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta di paM kA ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur bas las/ dus phyis dge slong rdo rje grags kyis bcos pa'o//
dpal ldan gshin rje gshed nag po'i 'khrul 'khor bri ba'i cho ga rgyas pa'i rtogs pa rdzogs so//
'jam dpal gyi rtog pa las dam rdzas bdud rtsi sman du rtogs pa rdzogs so//
dpal ldan gshin rje gshed nag po'i 'khrul 'khor bskor ba'i cho ga las/ las kyi rgyud dang grogs bstan pa'i rtogs pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon chen po la li ta badz+ra rgyad 'bum pa nas phyung ba/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta mkhan po di paM kA ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur ba'o//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po las kyi rdo rje dang / dge slong ku ma ra shi las bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon ka ma la rak+Shi tas sbyar ba badz+ra b+hai ra ba'i sgrub thabs pad+ma rgyas pa rdzogs so//
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon chen po a rA ya la li ta badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta a du ya badz+ra dang glog skya shes rab brtsegs kyis bsgyar cing gtan la phab pa//
slob dpon ngag gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa'i 'chi ba blu ba'i bsdus don rdzogs so//

'chi ba blu ba bstan pa slob dpon mkhas pa chen po lha mo sgrol mas byin gyis brlabs pa/ ngag gi dbang phyugs grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
chos thams cad 'phags pa 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed por bsgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon chen po 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon chen po dpal seng ge'i 'od can dang / dge slong bai ro tsa nas yul d+ha he na'i 'dul khang du bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i mngon par rtogs pa dngos grub kyi snye ma zhes bya ba/ rdo rje theg pa'i slob dpon gsang bas byin gyi zhal mnga' nas mdzad pa dge'o/
gshin rje gshed dmar po'i 'khrul 'khor gyi de nyid nges par bshad pa zhes bya ba'i bsgrub thabs/ gnas brtan mkhas pa chen po/ byang chub snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar mkhan po bla ma rje btsun/ nyi ma'i snying po'i 'od zer zhal sngon nas/ chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gshin po rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis rjes su bzung ba'i paN+Di ta/ grub thob chen po Doma b+hi he ru ka pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta dik+Shu mang+ga la dang / lo tsA ba zla ba 'od zer gyis rgyang ro rgyang po'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
gshin rje mthar byed kyi 'khrul 'khor gyi cho ga rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po rje btsun nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer gyi zhal snga nas/ chag lo tsA ba dge slong chos rje dpal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon 'phags pa klu grub kyis/ sha za rig pa rdzin pa'i rgyud nas phyung nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gnod sbyin ma kun nas 'khyil pa'i gwa sgrub thabs/ slob dpon klu grub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gnod sbyin yid 'phrog gi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po in dra bo d+hisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kha che paNa chen dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba tshul khrims gzhon nus bsgyur ba'o//

rje btsun dam pa rgya gar gyi gdams pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje rnal byor mas gsungs pa'i 'jam dpal ngag gi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so//
'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i spyan dbye ba'i cho ga zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen smri ti dz+nyA na kIrtis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'jam pa'i dbyangs dpa' bo gcig grub pa'i bstod pa gser gyi phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon gi dbang phyug grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so
a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po mi pham bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lhag pa'i lha 'di nyid kyis mngon su du byin gyis brlabs pa'i paN+Di ta chen po shrI ba na rat+na'i zhal snga nas kyi bka' drin las/ legs par sbyar ba'i skang kyi cha shas rig pa dge slong rgya mtsho'i sdes 'grub snying las cung zad bcos shing / rgya dpe'i rkang pa dang mthun par dpal gnod gnas kyi gtsug lag khang chen por bsgyur ba'o//
yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /jo bo rje lha gcig gis dpal gyi yer par mdzad do//
'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i sgrub thabs/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po sa'i steng na 'gran zla dang bral ba/ shAkya shrI b+ha tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs na dza ka ta ta li'i paN+Di ta dpal b+hi bu ta tsan+d+ra dang / glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ sa steng na 'gran zla dang bral ba'i paN+Di ta chen po kha che'i shAkyi shrI b+ha tra ces pa de/ rdo rje gdan na bzhugs pa'i tshe sku khams bag tsam ma bde nas dpyid zla 'bring po'i tshes brgyad la gso sbyong la gnas pa dang / nam gyi brgyad cha tsam lu pa na gzims nas bzhugs pa'i tshe/ 'phags pa don yod zhags pa 'khor dang bcas pa gzims nas bzhugs pa zhal mngon sum du gzigs nas/ bzhengs pa dang de bzhengs par zhal bstan te/ sku khams kyang dngas nas sgrub thabs 'di mdzad do//
'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i sgrub thabs/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal b+hi bu ti tsan+d+ra'i zhal snga nas gsungs pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i byin gyis brlabs pa dpal b+hi bu ti tsan+d+ra'i zhal snga nas/ glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyis bal yul thang gi b+hi har gyi gtsug lag khang du zhus te legs par gnang ngo//
don yod zhags pa'i mdo las bsdus pa/ slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po don yod rdo rje dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong ba ris bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dpal 'jig rten mgon po kha sar+pa Na'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba grub chen pad+ma 'byung gnas zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po shrI ba na rat+na'i zhal snga nas dang / chos 'khor lo tsA bas bsgyur ba las/ slad kyi btsun pa rgya mtshos dag par bcos shing gtan la phab pa'o//
bstod pa rin po che'i phreng ba 'di rdzogs so/ rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta chen po nags kya rin po che'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'o/ /mkhas pa chen po de nyid kyis spyan sngar/ dge slong rgya mtsho'i sde zhes bya bas bal yul ye rang gi grong khyer chen po'i 'dabs dpal go bi tsan+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang chen po bsgyur ba'o//
sems dpa'i phyag rgya zhes bya ba rim pa gnyis rgya cher gsal ba/ slob dpon chen po grub pa'i sa la 'gro ba 'god pa'i thugs rje can/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi zhabs kyi ze'u 'bru spyi bos reg pa/ bsod snyoms pas bshad pa rdzogs so/ rje btsun shar phyogs pa nirba Na shrI'i zhabs dang / rmongs pa kun dga' snying po tA ra nA thas bsgyur ba'o/ sngon chad gangs ri'i khrod du ma byon pa'i/ gzhung bzang 'di ni bla ma'i zhal las thob/ shar phyogs mkhas pa'i gsung bzhin 'di bsgyur te/ rmongs pa bdag gis cha tsam 'tshal bas so//
slob dpon dwa kin+ta chen po/ sems kyi phyag rgya gsung bar mdzad/ khaD+ga ba yi man ngag go /sngon chad gangs ri'i khrod du ma byon pa'i/ gzhung bzang 'di yang bla ma'i dran las thob/ sangs rgyas sbas pa'i gsung bzhin 'di bsgyur te/ rmongs pa kun dga' snying pos g.yar khral du'o//
dpal phyag na rdo rja'i sgrub thabs yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gnod sbyin sde dpon chen po phyag na rdo rje bsgrub pa'i thabs/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+hi paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
dpal phyag na rdo rje'i las bsgrub pa'i thabs/ rnal 'byor pa b+hira ya shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus pa'o/ dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa'i las rim 'di/ rdo rje'i mtshan ldan bla ma'i zhal snga nas/ rdzogs don grub zhes bya bdag gis ni/ gzhan la phan 'dod sems kyis zhus pa'o/ de la shes rab bsod nams bdag gis zhus//
rdo rje gtum po'i sgo nas rbod gtong phyir bzlog pa'i 'khor lo/ slob dpon las kya rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar mu stegs pa'i mthu bzlog pa'i don du mdzad pa'i gsung / bla ma wa la tsan dras/ rje ras chung pa la gnang ba'o/ mgo dang / gshen dab/ ras pa dang / su ga badz+ra bdag las brgyud gsung ngo/ 'di lga len cig yong sem mo//
U Sh+Ni Sha ri rab ma'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon shrI sing ngas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba be ro tsa nas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga /rgya gar gyi mkhan po rdo rje go chas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
sgrol ma nor sbyin ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta chen po sa ha dza shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mkhyen rab thugs rjes rab kyi phul du byung pa dpag tu med pas spras pa chos rje bla ma dam pa spyan snga rin po che grags pa byang chub rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bka' lung dang / dpon po grags pa rin chen gyi gsung bzhin du/ sne gdong nang so nas yo byad phun sum tshogs pa stsal te gnas de nyed du/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po ku mA ra shrI b+ha dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba nam mkha' bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
sgrol ma u gra'i mchod pa'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /rdo rje gdan gyi mkhan po shrI sha ri pu tra ma hA swa mi'i zhal mnga' nas mdzad de/ rang 'gyur du bsgyur ba'o//
sgrol ma dmar mos 'gro ba dbang du bsdu pa'i 'khor lo dag dang bcas pa rdo rje gdan pa bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sngags gi don 'jug pa/ slob dpon di paM ka ra shrI dz+nya nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
di paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa'i dbang gi man ngag rdzogs so//
dam tshig sbas pa/ di paM ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
maN+Dal 'bul ba rdzogs so//
chu gtor gyi cho ga rdzogs so//
sbyin sreg gi cho ga rdzogs so//
lha mchod pa'i rim pa rdzogs so//
rdo rje tshe bsgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so//
'chi ba slu ba rdzogs so//
'chi ka ma'i bsten bcos so/ byung chub kyi sems sbyang ba'i man ngag rdzogs so//
ro bsreg pa'i cho ga rdzogs so//
bdun tshigs kyi cho ga rdzogs so/
tsha tsha'i cho ga / slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gsang ngo/ dge bshes spyang nga bya yul ba'i/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis sgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa sgrol ma la rig pa'i gnas rnam pa lnga la ma rmongs pa snyan ngag mkhan po rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu lta du/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mi'i 'chi med zla ba zhes bya bas bstod pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shri dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas/ bod kyi ban+de sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas ka ma la shrI la'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
lha mo sgrol ma'i bstod pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon gyis sgrol mi'i shing sku de la bstod pas phyag 'dzub ke re mdzad skad/ de ltar mdzad pa ci lags zhus pa/ khyod kyi bstod pa de snyan gsungs te sgrol ma 'dzub ker du grags so//
rje btsun ma sgrol ma la bstod pa smon lam thams cad rab tu grub pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa'o//
ye shes kyi lha mo sgyu 'phrul chen po la/ shAkya'i dge slong dad byed go cha rin chen zhes bya bas bstod pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba rig pa'i khu byug gis bsgyur zhing legs par gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa sgrol ma 'jigs pa chen po brgyad las sgrol ba'i bstod pa/ slob dpon dpal btsun zla ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags ma sgrol ma la bstod pa slob dpon mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i mkhan po bud+d+ha ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi ye shes kyis bsgyur zhing zhus pa'o//
slob dpon ak+Sho b+h+ya badz+ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
yum chen lha mo dam tshig sgrol ma la bstod pa ko sa la'i yul rin chen ri zhes bya ba'i gnas na bzhugs pa'i slob dpon ngag gi dbng phyug tshe la dbang ba'i rin 'dzin thob pa des 'chi bdag bzlog pa'i phyir mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po mar me mdzad grags pa dang / lo tsA ba tshur pra pa ka ras bsgyur ba'o//
di mtshan yongs su grags pa rin po ches gsungs pa rdzogs so/ /bod kyi sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba gnyan dge slong d+harma kirtis rang 'gyur du gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon klu sgrub kyis bstod pa'o//
rje btsun ma 'phags ma sgrol ma la mtshan sum cu gnyis kyi bstod pa don thams cad grub par byed pa/ rin chen brgyan 'dra zhes bya ba/ kha che nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/
'phags ma sgrol ma'i bkra shis brdzod pa rdzogs so/ paN+Di ta suR+Ya shrI dang / lo tsA ba longs sa dge slong tshul khrims brtsegs kyis bsgyur//
gzhon nu kha ti ta re ma la bstod pa tshigs su bcad pa bcu drug pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu grub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags ma sgrol ma'i mtshan nges pa zhes bya ba stong phrag bcu gnyis pa las phyung ba rdzogs so//
bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag tu med pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma grub pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bcom ldan 'das mgon po tshe dpag tu med pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bzang po yongs su bzung ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta bzang po dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba glan dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur cing zhus te dag par byas so//
bcom ldan 'das tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i dbang bzhi bskur ba'i cho ga'i las khrigs/ 'chi med ye shes kyi bdud rtsi'i bum pa zhes bya ba/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma grub pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rta mgrin gyi bsgrub thabs rdzogs so/ bla ma ba la tsan+d+ra dang lo tsA ba glan dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur ba'o//
khro bo'i rgyal po mi g.yo ba bsgrubs pa'i thabs/ slob dpon dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gtum po'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpa' bo cig du bsgrub pa'i rgyud las/ paN+Di ta chen po rat+na shrI dz+nyA nas phyung ba rdzogs so//
gtum po khro bo chen po'i sgrub pa don dam pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po b+hang+ga la'i mkhas pa/ dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta nirbA Na shrI'i zhal snga dang / rmongs pa ta ra nA thas g.yar khral du bsgyur ba'o//
dpal nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /a tsar+ya ra hU la dmar po dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba gyi ljang gyi bsgyur//
dpal mgon po nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs kyi rim pa/ slob dpon klu grub kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta 'bum phrag gsum dang / lo tsA ba dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dpal nag po chen po'i bsgrub thabs zhes bya ba slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba ga rod kyis bsgyur ba'o/ rgyal tsha lung mang po dang / chos rjes bsod nams kyi phyag dpe las/ yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis klu'i dgon par zhus dag bgyis pa las bshus so//
zhal gyi u pa de sha 'di/ rak+Shi ta yis mdzad pa las/ gnyan lo dar ma grags kyis bsgyur//
dpal nag po chen po'i srog gi spu gri'i bsgrub thabs/ bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma mal kyi khyad chos lags so//
sbyin sreg cho ga sha thag pa/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /la li ta badz+ra dang / gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
dpal nag po chen po'i gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon bram ze mchog sred kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal sgeg pa'i rdo rje dang / gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
bram ze blo ldan mchog sred kyi dpal nag po chen po la rtags kyi sgo nas bstod pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta shrI ta ka ra varma dang / gu ru yon tan shi las gu ge tho ling du bsgyur ba'o//
nag po chen po khyod la bstod pa/ bstod pa'i phreng ba bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta la li ta badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o/ bram ze mchog sred zhes mthong dus dga' nas bstod pas/ mgon po mnyes nas zhal 'dzum mdzad do/ de nas phrin las bcos pa'i bstod pa mdzad do/ zhal gzigs kyi bstod pa'o//
nag po chen po gtor ma'i dus bskul ba/ slob dpon b+ha wi lhas mdzad pa//gyi ljang dbya dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
bla ma mai tri pas mgon po zhal gzigs du ston pa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /la li ta badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar kyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon a b+ha yas zhal gzigs dus bstod pa/ paN+Di ta shra ta ka ra warma dang / gu ru yon tan shi las gu ge tho ling du bsgyur ba'o//
dpal nag po chen po la bstod pa 'di ni bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa'o//
paN+Di ta spyan chen pos dur khrod bsil ba'i tshal du bstod pa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa'o//
dpal lha mo la bram ze mchog sred kyi rtags kyi sgo nas bstod pa'o/ la li ta badz+ra dang gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
ces lha mo srin gyis bstod pa/ la li ta badz+ra dang gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
ces drang srong ke'u tri las bstod pa/ la li ta badz+ra dang gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
ces bla ma mai tri pas lha mo zhal gzigs dus su bstod pa/ la li ta badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
dpal ldan lha mo la a b+ha yas zhal gzigs dus bstod pa/ paN+Di ta shra ta ka ra warma dang / gu ru yon tan shi las gu ge tho ling du bsgyur ba'o//
dpal ldan lha mo la nam mkha' lding gi rgyal po gser mig can gyis yan lag bdun du bstod pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta snying phreng can dang / lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbya dkar gyis bsgyur ba'o//
ces pa 'khor gyi bstod pa/ slob dpon chen po bram ze mchog sred kyis bstod pa mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shra ta ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon mchog sred kyis mdzad pa'o//
dpal ldan lha mo'i rjes gnang / slob dpon chen po zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dmag dpon chen po zhal bzhi pa'i bstod pa sho lo ka nyi shu pa zhes bya ba bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so//
byin gyis brlabs pa nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dpal ldan dzA pa ra pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi bla ma a ta ya badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims mgon gyis bsgyur ba'o//
byin gyis brlabs pa'i nag po chen po'i gsang ba'i sgrub thabs 'phags pa klu byang kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mi bskyod pa la brten nas mgon po'i bgegs sel bla ma gnad sgyur/ dpal ldan sha ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mgon po'i bka' gang byed kyang gser gyi maN+Dala shin tu gal che'o//
mgon po'i bkra shis yon tan rgya mtsho zhes bya ba dpal ldan sha ba ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dpal shA ba ri pa'i tshe sgrub rig 'dzin//
lha mo'i srog sgrub mai tre pas mdzad pa'o//
dpal ldan lha mo'i gsang sgrub rgya gar gyis mkhan po chen po dpal na ro pas mdzad cing / bod kyi lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyis blo gros kyis bsgyur zhing zhus pa'o//
ho phyogs bla ma ra hu las mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs thugs kyi gtso bo rdzogs so//
dpal nag po chen po phur par sgrub pa slob dpon bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mgon po'i nang sgrub rje mai tri pa la bdag 'khyung po rnal 'byor gyi zhus pa'o
slob dpon 'jam dpal gshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
nag po chen po phyag drug pa'i sgrub thabs/ dpal sha ba ri dbang phyug gis zhal mngon sum gzigs nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mgon po chen po'i byin gyis brlabs pa'i sgrub thabs/ sa ra has mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi bla ma a ta ya badz+ra dang/ lo tsA ba shangs pa tshul khrims mgon gyis bsgyur ba'o//
dpal nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs/ dpal sha ba ri pa chen pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta a ta ya badz+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba phur bu 'od kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gsang sgrub rim pa dam pa'o/ sha ba ris mdzad pa rdzogs so
nag po chen po'i bstod pa rngam pa sgra sgrogs zhes bya ba bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
mgon po'i gzhung bstod bla ma rA hu las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bram ze sa ra has zhal gzigs dus su rtags kyis sgo nas bstod pa'o//
dpal sha ba ri pas mgon po'i zhal gzigs pa'i dus su don gyi sgo nas bstod pa'o//
zhes bya ba nag po chen po phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon klu sgrub zhabs kyis mdzad pa 'di rdzogs so/ /dngos grub brnyes pa'i paN+Di ta chen po nags kyi rin chen gyi spyan sngar bsgyur ba'o//
'di yang jo bo rjes mdzad pa'o//
dpal sa skya lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rig sngags 'chang 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ me mkha' rgya mtsho lo dag pa'i gzhir bzhags nas lo drug cu bskor brgyad dang nyag ma nyi shu bsre ba kun 'dul ces bya ba me mo phag gi lo nag pa zla ba'i tshes gcig gi nyin/ mkhan chen chos kyi rje bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bka' gnang ba bzhin/ dpal sa skya bzhi thog tu dag par bsgyur ro/ rgya skad ma dag pas da dung cung zad dpyad par bya rgyu yod do//
srog bdud nag po'i dbang bsdus pa rin po che rgyas pa zhes bya ba slob dpon b+ha li na a tsaR+Yasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i rgyas pa gcig dang bzhugs skad//
rdo rje nag po chen po'i las bsad pa'i man ngag rdzogs so//
tsaN+Di ka'i sgrub thabs ces bya ba rdzogs so/ /rong glings lo tsA ba rdo rje dbang phyug gis bsgyur ba'o//
dbang bskur gyi cho ga rin chen 'phreng 'dra zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa//
dpal mgon po nag po'i sgrub thabs gsang ba mdzod kyi las byang rdzogs so/ /bla ma bram ze bde bas rang 'gyur du mdzed pa rdzogs so/ tshul khrims shes rab kyi man ngag ltar sgyur ro//
dpal nag po chen po'i gsang ba'i man ngag /slob dpon ro langs bde bas gdams pa rdzogs so/ /bram ze chen po la rim par brgyud nas/ tshul shes sgyur ba'i man ngag gi rgyud do/ mgon po 'di man ngag gi dbang du byas pa yin pas/ sgrub thag nye'o rdzogs so/ bla ma rin chen 'od pa'i phyag dpe la/ bla ma sang 'od pa'i zhal zhus so/ de'i dpe la dag par byas te/ rim par ban chung gis kyang zhal zhus so//
mgon po 'dus pa yi ge bcu ces bya ba rdzogs so/ bla ma bram zes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /tshul shes bsgyur ro
dpal mgon po bya rog ma'i bskang so kyi cho ga'i rim pa/ bla ma a b+ha ya kA ras /dpal nA len+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang du/ rdo sku rang byung gi rtsar mdzad pa'o/ /phyis bla ma chen po dpal rga los rang 'gyur mdzad pa'o//
slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ dpal rga los/ phag mo grub pa la gsungs pa 'di ni shin tu gnyan pas dam tshig med pa la mi bstan/ gang rung rung du mi bya//
mgon po bya rog gdong gyi gtor mdos/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu grub nag pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gnod sbyin nag po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po las kyi rdo rjes kong kha na'i 'od ma'i tshal du/ rang gi slob ma rje btsun chen po thang lo pas gsol ba btab nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta wa la tsan+d+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyis gus par bsgyur ba'o//
dpal nag po chen po yon tan gyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po wa la tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyis legs par bsgyur ba'o//
gnod sbyin nag po chen po la rin po che zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ka na ri pas bstod pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma wa la tsan+d+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur ba'o//
zhes pa 'jig rten dbang phyug ma hA ka la'i sgrub thabs rang gnas pa zhes bya ba de bA a ka ras mdzad pa'o/ 'di'i 'gyur rnying grub chen tshul mgon nyid kyis mdzad pa las/ sngags rnams phal cher zhal bzhes kyi dbang du mdzad pa 'dra bas dkyus na med/ mdzad byad bram ze rat+na pha las mdzad ces 'byung ba la bar skabs su mchan bu dkyus su shor ba sogs lhag chad nor skyon shin tu mang po snang ba/ rgya gar shar phyogs kya paN+Di ta pur+Na badz+ra ba'i zhabs kyi rgya dpe dang bstun nas/ rgyal khams pa tA ra nA thas 'gyur chad mang du bsabs shing / g.yar khral du zhus thug byas pa'o//
rje btsun dpal nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs man ngag mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba grub pa'i slob dpon shAn+ti'i gup+ta'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /shar phyogs gau ra'i paN+Di ta nirba Na shrI dang / slob dpon pUr+Na badz+ra'i zhabs dang / rmongs pa kun dga' snying pos bsgyur nas slar yang rgya dpe dang gtug te 'bru zhus yang yang byas pa'o//
ces pa nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs dpal ldan klu'i zhal gyi rim pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhas pa nirba Na shrI'i zhal snga nas dang / rmongs pa kun dga' snying pos g.yar khral du bsgyur ba'o//
'jigs byed nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs dpa' bo rgyal po'i zhal snga'i rim pas grub pa'i slob dpon pa ga la'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta pur+Na nan+da dang /dge slong tA ra nA thas g.yar khral du 'tshal ba'o//
rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyis rjes su 'brang ba'i gtor ma'i cho ga zhe bya ba/ 'gro bzang snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa klu grub kyis mdzad pa'o//
tshogs kyi bdag po'i sgrub thabs 'khor lo chen po zhes bya ba/ slob dpon a ba d+hu ti ba'i zhal snga nas gsungs pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/ rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas la gtad pa'o
dpal bgegs kyi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ grub pa'i brtul zhugs brnyes pa/ slob dpon nag po spyod pa bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang lo tsA ba gyi jo bla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba'o//
sna tshogs nor bu bde mchog 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba'o//
grub pa brnyes pa'i rnal 'byor pa nag po spyod pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
bgegs kyi rgyal po bsgrub pa'i thabs/ grub pa brnyes pa'i slob dpon chen po pas/ rgyud kyi rgyal po rdo rje mkha' 'gro nas phyung ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po la bstod pa/ slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bgegs bdag chen po'i sku bri ba'i man ngag /yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po nag po pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba'o//

grub pa'i dbang phyug ak+Sho b+h+ya badz+rasa kyi zhal snga nas slob bshad du bstsal ba'i man ngag gi dbang po'i lung skabs ji lta ba'i rtsa tshig tu'ang sbyar nas gsung pa rnams bskyud pas 'jigs pa las/ rje nyid kyi bzhed pa ji lta bar bal yul ye rang gi 'dab dpal go bo tsan+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten gom sa'i drung shAn+ta stu ri gsang pa mchog gi gnas la sogs par bsgyur te/ phyis mtshan ma khyad par can dang sbyar nas mtshams sbyor dang ming tho'i sa bon tsam dang spro'i dben gnas lhun grub snang zhes bya bar ri khrod pa rgya mtshos ye ger bgyis pa'o//
'dzam bu'i gling gi mkhas pa mtha' dag gi thig le mtshan brdzod par dka' ba'i grub pa'i dbang phyug shrI ba na rat+na'i zhal snga nas/ mdo sngags kyi bstan pa'i snying po las do gal du yi dam du bya ba'i gnad che long la gdams pa'i gzhung zhal las 'byung ba'i shas 'ga' zhig zin pa rnams/ paN+Di ta chen po de nyid kyi bka' drin gyis 'tsho ba'i dge slong rnal 'byor spyod pa rgya mtsho'i sde zhes bya bas brgyud par phangs pa kho na'i lhag pa'i bsams pas bzhed pa ji ltar bar bsgyur zhing / rin po che'i snying po dam pa'i phreng ba lta bu bsgrigs te ye ger spel pa re shig go//
'dzam bu'i gling gi mkhas pa mtha' dag gi thig le mtshan brdzod par dka' ba'i grub pa'i dbang phyug shrI ba na rat+na'i zhal snga nas/ mdo sngags kyi bstan pa'i snying po las do gal du yi dam du bya ba'i gnad che long la gdams pa'i gzhung zhal las 'byung ba'i shas 'ga' zhig zin pa rnams/ paN+Di ta chen po de nyid kyi bka' drin gyis 'tsho ba'i dge slong rnal 'byor spyod pa rgya mtsho'i sde zhes bya bas brgyud par phangs pa kho na'i lhag pa'i bsams pas bzhed pa ji ltar bar bsgyur zhing / rin po che'i snying po dam pa'i phreng ba lta bu bsgrigs te ye ger spel pa re shig go//
dpal ldan bla ma nags kyi rin po che'i bstod pa rin po che bdun pa rdzogs so/ /'di ni ma ga d+ha'i yul du byung ba'i dge bsnyen nyi ma zhes bya bas mdzad pa'o/ bstod pa'i yul dam pa paN+Di ta chen po de nyid kyi spyan sngar dA ri drangs rgya mtsho'i sde zhes bya bas bal yul ye rang gi grong khyer chen po'i 'dab dpal go bo tsan+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba las phyis cung zad kyang bcos so//
'di ni dpal sha ba ra'i zhabs kyi bstod pa rin po che zhes bya ba/ dpal nags kyi rin po chen zhabs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po de nyid dang / 'gos lo tsA ba dge slong gzhon nu dpal gyis bsgyur ba las/ slad du rje btsun gyi zhal snga nyid la lags par mnyan zhing don khong du chud par bgyis nas/ dge slong bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde zhes bya bas cung zad bcos te gtan la phab pa'o//
ces pa dpal rak+sha bdag nyid chen po'i bstan bcos dge ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar wA ra Na sa'i dzo ki paN+Di ta shrI gau sA lA nA tha dang / btsun pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis bsgyur ba'o//
dam tshig gsum bkod pa'i rgyal po yi ge brgya pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po ke la d+ha ra nan+desa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o/ 'gyur rnying la rgya dpe dang bsdur pa'i zhus dag can no//
'phags pa 'jig rten mgon po zhal bcu gcig pa'i sgrubs thabs rdzogs so/ /'di gsar 'gyur kho na yin no//
'jig rten mgon po ri khrod pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur kho na yin no//
gso sbyong rang gi blang ba'i cho ga 'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i mdo las phyung ba rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grags pas bsgyar ba'o/ rgya dpe ma rnyed 'gyur rnying zangs ma'o//
bcom ldan 'das 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba ba ris bsgyur ba'o//
o rgyan las 'byung ba'i 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur kho na yin no//
'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i snying po rdzogs so/ /'di yang gsar 'gyur yin no//
gtum po khro bo chen po'i sgrub thabs nyung ngu rdzogs so/ /'gyur gsar 'ba' zhig pa'o//
seng ldeng nags kyi sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /'di yang 'gyur gsar yin
bcom ldan 'das ma o rgyan gyi rnal 'byor ma'i mngon par rtogs pa'i rim pa rdzogs so/ /'di 'gyur rnying la rgya dpe dang zhu dag grub pa lags//
byang phyogs nas 'byung ba/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /'gyur rnying la zhu dag byas pa'o//
ral pa gcig ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /'gyur rnying la zhu dag go//

dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur ro//
dpal rnam par snang mdzad kyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur ro//
dpal rdo rje snang byed gser zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur ro//
bdud rtsi 'od kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon 'phrog byed seng ges mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur ro//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag rdo rje lta bu zhes bya ba/ dpal kam+ba la pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rngog 'gyur gtsang ma yin no//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag rdzogs so/ /rgya dpe ma rnyed rngog 'gyur gtsang ma yin//
sna tshogs yum gyi sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur yin no//
bskul byed ma'i sgrub thabs bud+d+ha kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so//gsar 'gyur ro//
bcom ldan 'das ma nor rgyun ma'i rtog pa rdzogs so/ /'gyur rnying dngos yin no//
ji ltar snyed pa'i bcom ldan 'das ma nor rgyun ma'i gzungs kyi rtog pa rdzogs so/ /de ltar chos mtshan gnyis nor rgyun ma'i cho ga ste rgya dpe ma rnyed/ 'gyur rnying kho na'o//
dpal u rgyan gyi rdo rje'i gnas nas nges par byung ba'i rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /pa tshab dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
'di ni mdor bsdus pa'i rdo rje phags mo'i sgrub thabs rdzogs pa yin no/ /slob dpon a b+ha ya'i zhal snga nas dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
do rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /pa tshab tshul rgyal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro mas bstan pa mdor bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /kha che rdo rje 'chang chen po shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba mchog dpal bzang gis bsgyur ba'o/ 'gyur rnying kho na'o//

gtor ma'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so//'gyur rnying la 'bru zhus byas pa'o//
synopsis: rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /sgrub thabs kyi rgya dpe la 'dir sngags ma gtogs sam pu Ti'i rgyud tshig tu snang bas rgyud mgos 'gyur bzhin bris nas rgya dpe dang zhu dag tsam byas pa'o//

bya ba'i sbyor ba rdzogs so//'di ni phal cher sdom pa 'byung ba'i rgyud tshig yin pas shong 'gyur dag las/ zhu dag cung zad byas shing tshig zur cung zad sgyur 'dug pa rnams rgya dpe ltar bcos pa'o//
khro mo'i dbang phyug ma gzhan gyi mi thub pa'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur yin no//

yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon rgyal dka' zla bas btus pa rdzogs so/ /'gyur rnying kho na ste rgya dpe rnyed na zhus dag dgos pa yod do//
khodpal bde mchog 'khor lo dpa' bo gnyis su med pa'i sgom thabs/ dngos grub brnyes pa slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po rab 'byor zhi ba dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba ting 'dzin bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ 'gyur rnying na'o//
mdor bsdus pa'i he ru ka'i sgrub thabs rdzogs so/ /ba ri ba'i 'gyur kho na lags so//
dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgrub thabs man ngag gi gnas zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po ka la haM pa ku mA ras mdzad pa'o//'gyur rnying la brgya dpe'i steng nas cung zad zhus dag byas pa'o//

dpal phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon bud+d+ha kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so//lo chen gyis bsgyur ba'i 'gyur rnying la zhus dag tsam bgyis pa'o//

je btsun phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub pa'i thabs gzung kyi rjes su 'brangs pa rdzogs so/ /'di stong pa nyid ting nge 'dzin rdo rjes mdzad pa yin te/ rgya skad lhug pa yin yang bod skad tshig bcad du sdebs par snang / tshig phal cher sgrub thabs rgyas pa ba ri'i 'gyur dang tshig gcig tu 'dug pa rnams ba ri'i 'gyur ltar bris nas 'bru zhus rgya dpe dang gtugs pa'o//
