dpal tshogs kyi dbang ldan chen po sgrub pa'i thabs rdzogs so/ /gsar 'gyur nyid do//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po bud+d+ha gup+ta'i zhal snga nas dang / nirbA Na shrI'i zhabs la rmongs pa tA ra nA thas zhus te gus pa chen pos 'bad pas bskur ba'o/ rim lnga dang kyai rdo rje'i lung drangs pa sogs pa ni 'gyur rnying ji lta ba bzhin du bris pa'o/ slob dpon chen zhi ba sbas pas nang gi khyabs pa zhes bya ba tshig bcad nyis brgya pa dang / rtsa ba'i mdo la phyed dang nyis brgya/ rlung gi mdo la phyed dang nyis brgya/ mkhams kyi mod brgya phrag gcig /lam lnga bstan pa la lung 'dren mi the ba tshig /nyis brgya/ rgyu bstan pa la brgya/ gnas bstan pa la nyis brgya/ phyag rgya chen po lam rdzogs pa dang / gtum mo'i gzhung la brgya nyi shu des lam rdzogs pa dang / lhan skyes gsal ba zhes pa la brgya bdun cu phyag rgyas lam rdzogs pa dang / ye shes nges bstan la sum brgya rgyu lus dang 'od gsal rnam par bzhag pa dang / man ngag thor bu la lnga brgya/ gsang 'dus pa dang / kyai rdo rje dang / bde mchog rnams la bsdus pa'i don gyi tshigs su bcad pa dang / rdo rje'i glu dang sgrub thabs chung ngu yang mang du mdzad par gda' ba/ rgyas pa la dga' ba'i dbang byas pa dang / 'bring du dga' pa la/ de dag las bsdus ta/ rdo rje lam che ba tshigs bcad stong tsam yod pa/ slob ma mchog mang po spyan sngar bsdus so// bsdus pa la dga' ba la lam bar pa tshigs bcad sum brgya pa/ slob dpon su ma tis bsdus so/ shin tu bsdus pa la dga' ba'i don du gzhung chung ba 'di la/ rgya gar skad du tshig bcad brgya dang lnga yod pa yin te/ bod skad du'ang rags rtsis la tshig bcad de tsam ste/ rnal 'byor ma chen mo/ dI na ka ras zhus nas bsdus pa/ 'di ni shin tu dar ba yin par gda' 'o/ ces pa'ang twa nas thas gzig go//
ces pa'ang tA ra nA tha'i reg cig go/
zhes pa rnal 'byor gyi glu/ slob dpon chen po bde ba chen po'i rdo rje'i zhabs kyi'o/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta gang ba'i rdo rje'i zhal snga nas las 'grel pa dang bcas pa mnyan nas/ g.yar khral du bsgyur ba po ni tA ra nA tha'o//
rang byin gyi brlab pa'i man ngag zhes bya ba/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon bar-tula bzhugs kyi rim pas slob dpon chen po ku pA las mdzad pa'o/ /slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas sbas pa'i zhal snga nas dang / rmongs pa kun dga' snying po tA ra nA thas g.yar khral du bsgyur ba'o//
yon srong ba'i man ngag nag po'i zhabs ma ga d+hara grags pa mchog thob pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /'di kah+ni pa chung bas yin ces paN+Di ta rnams zer gsung /grub mchog bud+ha gup+ta nA tha'i zhal snga nas gzhung 'di/ b+ha ba nA tha'i glu dbyangs dang 'grel ba sbyar pa'i bshad pa man ngag bcas gnang ba'i skabs su/ tA ra na thas rje nyid la zhu tig byas kyin bsgyur ba lags//
las sna tshogs spyod pa'i man ngag slob dpon seng ge go chas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta dza ya nan+ta dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rmongs pa'i gnyan po dgos 'dod thams cad 'byung bas bsgyur cing btan la phab pa'o/ 'di'i nang gi rdzas kha yar dang lag len la yig chung phran bu zur na yod lags so//
zhes pa nag mo'i 'bangs kyis bkod pa'i bkra shis brgyad pa rdzogs so/ /ces pa 'di ni rgya gar gyi snyan dang mkhan chen po nag mo'i 'bangs kyis mdzad pa'i bkris brgyad pa zhes bya ba 'di'i rgya dpe rgya gar nub phyogs kyi rnal 'byor pa chen po tsang ga yi zhes pa/ bod skad lha mo'i dpal zhes pas bsnams byon pa/ dpal ldan bla ma'i bka' drin gyis bsgyur nas sum bi ta 'bri ba po ni dge slong dpal ldan grags pas bgyis nas phul ba'o/ bkra shis//phyi mo ltar gcig zhus/

shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta go mi 'chi med dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa legs par spyad pa'i las can/ theg pa chen po la yang dag par gnas pa/ 'phags pa mang pos bkur ba ku ru ku la'i sde pa gtsug lag khang rgya chen po du ma'i bdag po/ slob dpon sangs rgyas 'bangs kyi tsha bo/ shAkya'i dge slong 'phags pa rnam par grol ba'i sdes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gang du dngos po dmigs pas dkrugs pa mang po bkur pa bzhin du 'khrul gyur pas/ shes rab pha rol phyin tshul gang zhig theg chen lam pa gzhan gyis ma gtogs pa/ des na 'phags pa gsal ba'i blo mnga' de yis rgyal la mngon sum 'di zhus nas/ grang don go rim ming dang dbye ba 'bras bu'i sgo nas 'di bshad ngo mtshar che/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po shar phyogs kyi dge bsnyen chen po dpal go mi 'chi med dang / lo tsA ba chen po shAkya'i dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur cing legs par gtan la phab pa'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa mkhas pa chen po mos pas spyod pa'i sa brnyes pa/ slob dpon rnam par grol ba'i sdes mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rje btsun byang chub 'od kyis bka' lung gis/ bal yul kyi paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po shAn+ti b+ha dra'i zhal mnga' nas dang / 'bro seng dkar dge slong shAkya'i 'od kyis bsgyur/ 'di la sho lo ka stong bzhi brgya yod//



slob dpon seng ge bzang pos mdzad pa'i nyi khri le'u brgyad ma'i bar dum rdzogs so//


dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag bod kyi lha btsan po khri bkra shis lde btsan gyis bkas/_rgya gar gyi mkhan po su b+ha Shi ta dang /_sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur nas/ slad kyi rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba chen po dge slong rin chen bzang pos yul dbus kyi dpe dang yang gtugs nas bcos shing zhus te gtan la phab pa las/ de nas dus phyis paN+Di ta chen pos 'bum phrag gnyis kyis mgrin pa brgyan pa d+hi ra pA la zhes bya ba dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyi legs par bsgyur zhing bcos pa'o//

yon tan rin po che sdud pa'i tshigs su bcad pa'i dka' 'grel rtogs par sla ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po seng ge bzang po'i zhal nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal yul gyi paN+Di ta dze ta ha du shan+ti b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba 'bro seng dkar shAkya'i 'od kyis bsgyur/ blo ngan tshong pa nor bu 'ching bu la/ rin chen rin thang med snyam 'chang ba ltar/ dam pa brgyud pa'i gdams ngag dang bral ba/ ngan rtog rgyud la rgyal yum don yin par/ log rtog bsal phyir sa bdag mam kyi mchog /bzhon nu rab gshegs thos pa'i shes rab byang / de don gtan phab sems pa'i shes rab chung / bsgom pa'i rgyun bsten tshul khrims gtong ba'i 'od/ rin chen dang bcas rje btsun bkas bskul nas/ bzhin gyis skyon yon gsal byed me long ltar/ seng ge bzang po'o man ngag rtogs sla ba/ 'bad pas bal yul bgrod nas bdag gi bsgyur/ gal te kha cig 'di la'ang phrag dog gos spong na/ gzhan la gnod med bdag nyid kho na phung byed yin/ ji ltar rus skam dung pa khyi rgan gyis 'chos pas/ rkan phug rang khrag 'jib cing rus pa'i ro snyam sems/ rang rtags ngan rtog gzhung la chags pa'ang de bzhin no/ dus gsum kun tu mi 'gyur nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa/ chos nyid skyon med pha rol phyin pa 'di nyid lags/ de thos de la ma dad log bltas bdag tu 'dzin/ na so chod dang ldan yang byis par 'dren pas gsungs/ 'dis kyang bstan pa rin po che rgyas par byed nas par gyur cig/
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan ces bya ba'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon seng ge bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+ya ka ra pra b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ slad kyi paN+Di ta dpal go mi 'chi med la sogs pa dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis legs par gtan la phab pa'o//
gser gling gi dpal rnam par rgyal ba'i grong du lha dpal gtsug gi nor bu'i go cha'i rgyal po'i rang lo chigs bcu pa las dpyid zla ra ba'i tshes bcu gcig la mdzad pa/_rtogs par dka' ba'i snang ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/_/rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang /_sgra bsgyur gi lo tsA ba chen po dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
nub kyi sgo glegs pa dpal mkhas pa chen po shes rab 'byung gnas blo gros kyis mdzad pa mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyis bshad pa bsdus don rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po su ma kIrti dang /lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi bsgyur ba'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa'i 'grel bshad tshig rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba/ yul chen po pai da lar skyes pa'i slob dpon mkhas pa chen po pa/ grub pa'i mtha' rab 'byam la mkhyen pa'i snang bas khyab pa/ theg pa chen po dbu ma'i slob dpon dpal chos kyi bshas gnyen zhes bya ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a b+hi yug ta kad ta ra shrI mi tra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi dad pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i don bsdus pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mA ra shrI b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba bkra shis rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
sdud pa tshigs su bcad pa'i dka' 'grel slob dpon bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra sing+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur nas zhus te gten la phab pa'o//
mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa grags pa'i cha zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta rat+na kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta chen po rat+na kIrti dang / lo tsA ba chings yon tan 'bar gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//

dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum bcom ldan 'das ma/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag gi bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa shes rab sgron ma'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ dpal chos kyi rje byang chub sems dpa' dam pa mkhas pa/ thams cad kyi bla mar gyur pa kha che'i rigs kyi paN+Di ta chen po bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po de nyid dang / gnubs lo tsA ba dge slong byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi 'grel pa dag ldan zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag lha btsan po khri bkra shis 'od lnga btsan gyi bkas rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI su b+hu ti shAn+ti'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya blo gros dang / dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyar cing / bcos te gtan la phab pa/ slad kyis paN+Di ta chen po shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lha btsas kyis gtan la phab ste bcos pa'o//
stong phrag brgya pa'i rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /'di ni kha che'i paN+Di ta d+harma shrIsa mdzad do zhes grags so//
'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brgyad stong pa'i bka' 'grel snying po mchog ces bya ba rgyal po'i slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta shrI su b+hu ti shan+ti dang / lo tsA ba shAkyi blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i don bsdus sgron ma zhes bya ba dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba mkhas pa chen po'i chen po tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur/ slad kyi dpal bsam yas lhun gyi sgrub pa'i rig pa 'byung ba'i gnas su/ dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas nyi khri bshad pa'i dus su 'dir bshad pa nas bton/ phyis lo paNa gnyis kyis bi bar ta yis gsungs pa dag pa'i dpar tshud pa'o/ 'di dpe phyi ma dang pe bar ta dang rgya dpe gsum mchims phun/ bai ro tsa nas bsgyur ba'i 'bum sha sgro can gyis nang na yod skad//

'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brgyad stong pa'i 'grel pa paN+Di ta chen po 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa'i gnad kyi zla ba'i 'od ces bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid kyi zhal snga nas dang / mkhas pa ban+de shes rab dpal gyis dpal nA lan+d+rara bsgyur ba'o //
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mdzod kyi lde mig ces bya ba kha che'i mkhan po bla ma d+harma shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ 'phags pa sdud pa'i gdams ngag 'di/ myang chu sa'i snying po dpal 'bum ste stengs kyi gtsug lag khang gsar du bzhengs pa'i dus su/ slob dpon chen po byang chub sems dpa' 'dzom nas/ shes rab kyi pha rol phyin pa 'di 'sgyur cing bka' stsal te/ ston sgom sbag ma gsum gyis zhu ba phul/ dge slong dri ma med pas yon bdag mdzad nas/ mkhas pa chen po ba reg lo tsA bas sems can gyi don du bsgyur ba'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'bum pa rgya cher bshad pa las le'u nyi shu gsum pa'o//

skye bo kun la brtse phyir mdo gzhung bkrol// gnas brtan che la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo//
'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'bum pa dang / nyi khri lnga stong pa dang / khri brgyad stong pa rgya cher bshad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma bsdus pa'i tshig le'u'r byas pa/ slob dpon phyogs kyi glang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta ti la ka ka la sha dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon phyogs kyi glang po'i zhal snga nas nye bar sbyar pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsdus pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa'i rnam par 'grel pa slob dpon bla ma dkon mchog gsum gyi 'bangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che paN+Di ta thig le bum pa dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//

bcom ldan 'das ma'i 'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brgyad stong pa'i rnam par bshad pa man ngag gi rjes su 'brang pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /'di'i gzhung tshad ni sho lo ka stong phrag brgyad do/ dpal ldan nga rgyal skyong gis rgyal srid mdzad pa'i lo bdun pa la dgun zla 'bring po'i tshes bzhi la dpal byang chub chen po'i lha khang du bris pa'o/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po a la ka de ba dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims 'byung gnas kyis dpal sgye'u ri'i drung du chos skor dben sa'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
tshigs su bcad pa dgu pa zhes bya ba/ dpal la ba pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsAr+ya shrd+d+hA ka ra war ma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la pa pa'o//
bcom ldan 'das ma shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i don bsdus pa/ tshigs su bcad pa dgu pa'i rgya cher bshad pa / slob dpon chen po kam+pa la'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gup+ta dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bdun brgya pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ mgon po ngag gi dbang pos spobs pa bskyed pa'i slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bdun brgya pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon ka ma la shrI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi ma la mi tra dang / li'i mkhan po su ran trA ka ra pra b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong nam mkha' skyong gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
zhes pa 'di ni thams cad mkhyen pa gzhon nu'i dpal gyis zhal snga nas gsar 'gyur mdzad pa'i 'phro cung zad lus pa/_rje dam pa de'i dgongs pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i slad du 'gyur bar gyis shig ces/ zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa bzhi pa/ chos grags ye shes dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas bka' stsal pa spyi bos mnos te/ zhwa lu lo tsA ba 'gos chos skyong bzang pos / lugs gnyis kyi mdun sa chen po pho brang sne'u gdong rtser/ chos kyi rje rgyal ba chen po dpal ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba'i mnga' thang chen po la brten nas legs par bsgyur ba'o// slar yang rgya dpe la gtugs shing slob dpon kA ma la shI las mdzad pa'i 'grel par brjod bya ris mthun pa rnams dang sbyar te tshig phrad dang 'khrugs sdeb sogs cung zad legs char 'gyur ba rnams 'bad cing dag par bgyis so//
'phags pa rdo rje gcod pa dbu ma'i tshul du rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po many+dzu shrI dang / dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
phags pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po'i brgya cher bshad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dri ma med pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyis mkhan po bi ma la mi tra nyid dang / bod kyi zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de nam mkha' dang ye shes snying po la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bcom ldan 'das ma shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po'i 'grel pa slob dpon dz+nyA na mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so
bcom ldan 'das ma shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po'i 'grel pa don gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ bal yul ye rang gi grong khyer du rje btsun bla ma dam pa phyag na rdo rje'i spyan sngar bod kyi dge ba'i gshes gnyen rnams kyis chos zhus pa'i dus su/ bla ma dam pas chos ston pham babs gnang ba'i nyen bar bod kyi dge ba'i bshes rnams kyis mdo bton pa la/ bla ma dam pas lo tsA ba la khong 'don pa de ci yin gsungs pas/ lo tsA bas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po lags zhus pas/ 'o na bod du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po dar na sangs rgyas kyis lung bstan pa de bden pa yin no/ snying po'i don gyi gdams ngag shes sam gsungs pa la/ skye mang bde chen bud ba smyon pa'o/ ba la su zhag mnyan du yang / gal te smyan pa'i chag la bden pa yang srad thugs la dgongs nas su/ mthun pa'i grags pa rnams kyis ma bden na yang don 'di dgongs par zhu/ gal te stod pa thabs yin na/ de tsho lo tsA bas ma 'tshal zhes lan btab pa la/ 'o na ngas khyed rnams la gdams ngag bstan gyis gsungs nas/ snying po'i don gyis gdams ngag gnang ba zin ris bris nas nan tan bya pa yin no/ bla ma dam pa'i zhabs kyi pad ma'i sbrang rtsi smyo chu 'thungs nas su/ skye med bde chen bung ba smyon pa'i kha la su zhig mnyan du yod/ gal te smyon pa'i tshig la bden pa yod srid thugs la dgongs nas su/ mthun pa'i grogs po rnams kyi mi bden na yang don 'di dgongs par zhu/ gal te stong pa thabs yin na/ de tshe sangs rgyas nyid mi 'gyur/ rgyu las 'bras bu gzhan med phyir/ thabs ni stong pa nyid ma yin/ lta ba rnams las legs rnams dang / bdag tu lta ba tshol rnams kyi/ bdag tu 'dzin pa bzlog pa'i phyir/ rgyal ba rnams kyi stong pa bstan/ srid zhi mnyam nyid dus gsum rgyal ba'i yum/ 'gro ba'i bde sgrub thabs mkhas ston par byed/ gzhung gi bdag nyid rin chen lta bu la/ dad dang gus pas yang yang phyag 'tshal lo/ phan sems spro dgas bris pa'i 'grel pa 'di/ gang zag dam pa rnams kyi phyag tu brgyud pa dang / bstan pa'i bya ba mdzod pa bdag gi smon lam yin/ chos nyid bden pas de ltar grub gyur cig/
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po rgya cher 'grel pa pra shA s+t+ra se nas mdzad pa rdzogs so
shes rab kyi pho rol tu phyin pa'i snying po yongs su shes pa/ paN+Di ta shrI ma hA dza nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba ge slong seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shri dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//

dbu ma rtsa ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa shes rab ces bya ba theg pa chen po'i chos rnam par bzhag pa/ don dam pa'i de kho na yang dag par ston pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul gsal bar byed pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams dang ba'i 'od ces bya bar/ slob dpon bdag nyid chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub mi 'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rjer ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i theg pa bla na med pa'i tshul gsal bar byed pa/ rab tu dga' ba'i sa bsgrubs nas/ bde ba can gyi zhing du gshegs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams dang ba'i 'od ces bya bar/ ye shes 'byung gnas 'od ces bya bar 'gyur bas mdzad pa rdzogs so// dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag rgyal po chen po dpal ldan lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po theg pa chen po dbu ma pa/ dz+nyA na gar b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la rab tu byed pa nyi shu rtsa bdun/ sh+lo ka bzhi brgya bzhi bcu rtsa dgu yod/ bam po ni phyed dang gnyis su byas so/ slad kyis kha phye'i grong khyer dpe med kyi dpung / gtsug lag khang rin chen sbas pa'i dbus su/ kha che'i mkhan po ha su ma ti dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis mi'i bdag po 'phags pa lha'i sku ring la 'grel pa tshig gsal ba dang bstun nas bcos pa'o//
rigs pa drug cu pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa zhes bya ba slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po mu ti ta shrI'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyi bcos te gtan la phab pa'o//
zhib mo rnam par 'thag pa zhes bya ba'i mdo/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta a nan+ta dang / lo tsA ba dge slong grags 'byor shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
stong nyid bdun cu pa tshig le'ur byas bya ba/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu grub kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba gzhon nu mchog dang/ gnyan d+harma grags dang / khu'i 'gyur dag las/ don dang tshig bzang du bris pa'o//
rtsod pa bzlog pa'i tshig le'u byas pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur pa las/ slad kyi kha che'i paN+Di ta dza ya a nan+ta dang / lo tsA ba khu mdo sde dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o//
dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag rgyal po chen po dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po theg pa chen po dbu ma pa dz+nyA na garba dang/ bod kyi zhu chen gyis lo tsA ba/ dge slong klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa/ theg pa che po'i nges don/ dbu ma'i bstan rtsa ba shes rab ces bya ba'i 'grel pa mdzad pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub dang / gnas brtan bud d+ha pA li ta dang / tsan d+ra kIrti dang / de ba sharma dang / gi Na ma gi ti dang /s+thi ra ma ti dang / legs ldan 'byed dang brgyad ces gna' mchan cig las 'byung / 'di la rab tu byed pa ni nyi shu rtsa bdun/ shu log nyis stong chig brgya yod/ bamapo ni bdun du byas so//
shad ma la sogs pa tshig gi don bcu drug sel bar byed pa zhib mo rnam par 'thag pa zhes rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /yongs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po/ yon tan grags pa'i bkas/ kha che'i paN+Di ta dza ya a nan+ta dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po shAkya'i dge slong khu mdo sde 'bar gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
stong pa nyid bdun cu pa'i bshad pa/ brda' sprod pa chen po bstan bcos thams cad 'chad par bzhed pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rtsod pa bzlog pa'i rab tu byed pa'i 'grel pa sa dang por rab tu dga' ba la bzhugs pa slob dpon nA gA rdzu nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nya na gar+b+ha dang lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
theg pa chen po nyi shu pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po tsan+d+ra ku ma ra dang / dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur//
ye ge brgya pa rdzogs so//
yi ge brgya pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal kha che'i grong khyer dpe med du ban+de gzhon nu shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/ slad kyi paN+Di ta/ a nan+ta dang / lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyis zhu chen legs par byas so//
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i snying po'i tshigs le'u'a byas pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i snying po'i rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ma rtogs pa rtogs par byed pa/ gnyi ga bdag med par rab tu gsal bar byed pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta a nan+ta dang / lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
skye med rin po che'i mdzod ces bya ba 'phags pa klu sgrub snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka na ga bar ma dang / lo tsA ba sur+ya kIrtis lha sa ra mo cher bsgyur ba'o//
dbu ma srid pa 'pho ba zhes bya ba/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'gro ba rigs drug las srid pa 'pho ba'i thabs sangs rgyas thob par byed pa'i thabs rdzogs so//paN+Di ta byams pa mgon pos mdzad pa'o/ paN+Di ta zla ba gzhon nu la/ sgru ston chung gis zhus nas rang 'gyur du mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dbu ma rtsa ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa shes rab cas bya ba theg pa chen po'i chos mngon pa rnam par bzhag pa don dam pa'i de kho na yang dag par ston pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul gsal bar byed pa/ slob dpon bdag nyid chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub mi 'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rabs dang / thugs rjer ldan pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i theg pa bla na med pa'i tshul rab tu 'byed pa rab tu dga' ba'i sa sgrubs nas bde ba can gyi zhing du gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams dang 'do ces phya bar de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes 'byung gnas 'od cas bya bar 'gyur bas mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa/ bud+d+ha pA li ta/ zhes bya pa theg pa chen po nges pa'i don ston pa/ lta ba ngan pa'i dri ma sel bar byed pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul gtan la 'babs pa/ don dam pa'i bden pa gsal bar byed pa/ slob dpon btsun pa sangs rgyas bskyangs 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi bka' grub pa bstan bcos du ma'i rnam par bshad pa mdzad pa/ theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa/ rig sngags 'chang grub pa'i gnas khyad par can du gshegs pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mtshan nyid gsum la 'jug pa/ slob dpon chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal mnga' nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta dge slong zla ba grags pas bsgyur ba'o//
cha shas kyi yan lag ces bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrad+d+ha ka ra varma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i bsgyur ba'o//
cha shas kyi yan lag ces bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrad+d+ha ka ra varma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i bsgyur ba'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i rnal 'byor spyod pa bstan bcos bzhi brgya pa'i tshig le'u'a byas pa zhes bya ba/ seng+gala'i gling du pad+ma'i sbubs las brdzus te 'khrungs shing / rang rang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa yang dag pa ma yin pa'i lta ba rnam par 'byed pas dbu ma'i lam rab tu gsal bar mdzad pa/ 'phags pa klu'i zhabs kyi sras su gyur ba'i slob dpon 'phags pa lha'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i brong khyer dpe med kyi dbus/ rin chen sbas pa'i kun dga' ra bar/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su sma dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba pa tshang nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
khrul ba bzlog pa'i rigs pa gtan tshigs grub pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nyA na de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rab tu byed pa lag pa'i tshad kyi tshig le'ur byas pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so//

dbu ma 'khrul pa 'joms pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po AR+Ya de bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus pa/ 'dzam bu'i gling gyi rgyal po su kha tsaR+Yasa na lan+da'i gtsug lag khang chen por gsol ba btab nas mdzad do//
ye shes snying po kun las btus pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po 'phags pa lha'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kriSh+Na ra ba dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
ye shes snying po kun la btus zhes bya ba'i bshad sbyar/ slob dpon byang chub bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyis shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag rgyal po chen po dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po theg pa chen po dbu ma pa dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / bod kyi zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la rab tu byed pa ni nyi shu rtsa bdun / sh+lo ka ni drug stong yod/ bam po ni nyi shur byas so
bka' ma lus pa'i snying po bsdus pa/ de kho na nyid gsal por ston pa/ dbu ma rin po che'i sgron ma/ bdag dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha'/ rgya mtsho lta bu mkhyen pa'i pha rol tu byon pa/ sku tshe 'di nyid la/ sku lus de nyid kyis rig 'dzin gyi gnas su gshegs pa'i/ slon dpon mkhas pa chen po/ b+ha byas/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi gsung bzhin du mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bla ma rje btsun zangs gling pa/ dge bsnyen mgon po la/ paN+Di ta chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas/ bka' drin zhus pa las/ phyis so ma phu ra'i gtsug lag khang du/ rgya brtson 'grus seng+ge dang / nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba gnyis kyis/ yang nas yang du zhus nas/ bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//

dbu ma'i snying po'i tshig le'ur byas pa slob dpon chen po b+ha byas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang gi gzhir/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas/ lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrim rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dbu ma'i snying po'i 'grel pa rtog ge 'bar ba/ slob dpon d+ha byas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /ra sa 'phrul snang gtsug lag khang gi gzhir/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dbu ma'i don bsdus pa slob dpon legs ldan 'byed kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o
dbu ma rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa rdzogs so



slob dpon leg ldan 'byed gyis nye bar sbyar ba dbu ma rtsa ba'i 'grel pa shes rab sgron ma las song ba dang / ma song ba dang / bgom pa rtag pa zhes bya ste/ rab tu byed pa gnyis pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon spyan ras gzigs brtul zhugs kyi nye bar sbyar ba rdzogs so//

kha che'i grong khyer dpe med kyi dpung / rin chen sngas pa'o gtsug lag khang gi 'dabs su/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po rtogs ge pa chen po/ ma hA su ma ti'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis kha che'i dpe dang mthun pa ltar bsgyur/ phyis ra sa ra ma che'i gtsug lag khang du kha che'i mkhan po ka na ka warma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba bde nyid kyis nyi 'og shar phyogs kyi dpe dang / gtugs shing legs par bcos te gtan la phab pa'o//
dbu ma la 'jug pa zab pa dang rgya che'i tshul gsal bar byed pa/ slob dpon zla ba grags pa theg pa mchog la thugs gzhol ba/ mi 'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rje mnga' ba/ ri mor bris pa'i ba drus las 'o ma bzhos pas bden par zhen pa bzlog par mdzad pas sbyar ba rdzogs so/ /kha che'i yul gyi grong khyer dpe med kyi dbus/ rin po che sbas pa'i gtsug lag khang du/ kha che'i rgyal po dpal 'phags pa lha'i sku ring la/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ti la ka dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis kha che'i dpe dang mthun par bsgyur/ phyis ras ra mo cher rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka na ki warma dang / lo tsA ba de nyid kyis nyi 'og shar phyogs pa'i dpe dang gtugs shing legs par bcos te gtan la phab pa'o/ 'di 'grel pa'i mdzad byad dang / 'gyur byang gi steng nas thun mong pa rnams bkod pa ni/ rtsa ba logs su bsgyur ba dang 'grel pa'i nang gi rtsa ba gnyis sbyar nas zhus dag byas pa'i dbang du byas pa yin no//
dbu ma 'jug pa bshad pa zab pa dang / rgya che ba'i tshul gsal bar byed pa/ slob dpon zla ba grags pa theg pa mchog la thugs gzhol ba/ mi 'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rabs dang thugs rje mnga' ba/ ri mor bris pa'i ba drus ma las 'o ma bzhos pas bden par zhen pa bzlog par mdzad pas sbyar ba rdzogs so/ khungs rnams phal cher mdo bzhin bris/ phyin chad skad gnyis byung srid na/ rtsa 'grel sgra don bzhin bsgyur la/ gzu bor byos la dpyad par gyis/ kha che'i yul gyi grong khyer dpe med kyi dbus rin chen sbas pa'i gtsug lag khang du/ kha che'i rgyal po dpal 'phags pa lha'i sku ring la/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ti la ka ka la sha dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis/ kha che'i dpe dang mthun pa ltar bsgyur/ phyis ras ra mo cher rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka na ka warma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba de nyid kyis nyi 'og shar phyogs pa'i dpe dang btugs shing legs par bcos te gtan la phab pa'o/ gzhung 'di yi tshad ni bam po bcu gnyis su bam po'i drug cha gcig gis dman pa ste/ sho lo ka sum stong lnga brgya lnga bcu yod pa'o//
dbu ma shes rab la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po zla ba grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba 'gos khug pa lhas btsas kyis bsgyur ba'o//
rigs pa drug cu pa'i 'grel pa 'di ni/ slob dpon zla grags zhes bya ba theg pa chen po dbu ma'i slob dpon yul sa ma ta nas skyes pa/ mu stegs can rtog ge ngan par smra ba'i tshogs thams cad kyi mun pa mang po rnam par 'joms pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dka' mtha' gnyis rnam par spangs pa'i nam mkha'i dkyil thos pa dang bsam pa las byung ba'i ye shes kyis snang bar gyur na/ gnas pa yang dag pa ma yin pa'i phyin ci log rnam pa sna tshogs kyi tshabs gdungs pa'i 'gro ba mtha' dag bsil bar mdzad pa'i zla ba'i zer dri ma med pa dpag tu med pas grags pa yin te/ des mdzad pa'i rigs pa drug cu pa'i 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon 'phags pa lha'i byang chub sems dpa'i rnal 'byor spyod pa bzhi brgya las/ slob dpon dang slob ma rnam par gtan la dbab pa sgom pa bstan pa zhes bya ba ste/ rab tu byed pa bcu drug pa'i 'grel ba'o/ bzhi brgya pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon zla ba grags pa'i zhal snga nas kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal grong khyer dpe med kyi dbus rin chen sbas pa'i kun dga' ra bar/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po suk+Sha ma dzA na zhes bya ba gdung rabs grangs mes par paN+Di ta brgyud ma'i rigs su sku 'khrungs pa bram ze chen po rin chen rdo rje'i dpon po bram ze chen po sad dzA+nya na'i sras gcig tu bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa la gces spras su mdzad pa bdag dang gzhan gyi gzhung lugs rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyis sgra bsgyur gyis lo tsA ba dge slong pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa rdzogs so//
phung po'i lnga zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal lha btsun pa bo d+hi rA dza'i bka' lung dang / dge 'dun kyi bka' stsal gyis tshangs pa'i 'byung gnas gtsug lag khang du rgya gar gyis mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas phag gi lo la bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
stong nyid bdun cu pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /stong nyi bdun cu'i 'grel pa ni/ dge slong d+harma grags kyis bsgyur/ gzhung grang stong phrag gnyis dang ni/ brgya phrag gcig gis lhag pa yin/ dpal nA len+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang du paN+Di ta a b+ha ya ka ra dang / snur lo tsA ba d+harma grags kyis bsgyur pa'o//
kha che'i yul gyis mkhas pa chen po slob dpon so ma shrI'i zhal snga nas kyi zhabs kyi rdul la nye bar bsten par mdzad pa'i slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal gzhan la phan pa'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa stong pa nyid bdun cu pa'i 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /thugs dam sa'i tho ling du/ kha che'i mkhan po pa ra hi ta'i zhal snga nas nyid dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong gzhon nu mchog gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o
rtog ge'i tho ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa nyi shu pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta dza ya A nan+dasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba khu mdo sde 'bar dang / paN+Di ta de nyid kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//

dbu ma la 'jug pa'i 'grel ba bshad pa don gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po dza ya a nan+dasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa lha yi yul dang mtshungs/ chos rgyal gdung mi 'chad par 'byung ba'i mi nyag yul/ chu bo rmo yi dogs dang ri bo rtse lnga'i 'dabs/ rgyal po'i pho brang dpung tshogs gnas pa yi/ khyad par mkhar sku zhes bya'i gtsug lag khang chen du/ kha che'i mkhas pa chen po rtsom mdzad de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de kun dga' grags zhes pas/ dbu ma la 'jug 'grel bshad don gsal zhes bya bsgyur/ 'di bsgyur ba las dge ba gang / thob des 'gro ba ma lus pa/ sgrib pa rnam pa gnyis spangs nas/ bla med byang chub thob par shog /kha che'i mkhas pa chen po dza ya A nan+da dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de kun dga' grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ 'phags pa 'bum gsal brtsegs pa zhes bya ba'i gtsug lag khang chen po'i 'dabs su/ gnas brtan chen po su ra sa ba h+ye na gyon ti shi'i phyag dpe la bris nas/ shakya'i dge slong smon lam rgyal bas gzhan las sbyin par ba bya'i chos su bzhengs nas spyan drangs pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa slob dpon shan+ta de bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyi kha che'i dpe la gtugs te gtan la phab pa las/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po dang / shAkya blo gros kyis yul dbus kyi dpe dang 'grel pa dang mthun par bcos shing bsgyur te gtan la phab pa/ yang slad kyi bal po'i paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis dag par bcos shing zhus te/ legs par gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i 'grel bshad las sher rab le'u'i rgya cher bshad pa/ dge slong mkhas pa shes rab 'byung gnas blo gros kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i grel bshad las le'u dang po gnyis dang brtson 'grus bsam gtan shes rab kyi Ti kA mkhas pa chen po su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyis bsgyur ba'o/ dbu ru byang phyogs lcung ka mkhar grags su mkhas pa chen po blo gros bzang grags pa/ ldong stong macho gnas rgya sgo mched grogs kyis/ gsol btab dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur//
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i rnam par bshad pa'i bka'i 'grel pa rdzogs so//

shu log stong phrag gcig dang ni/ dgu brgya bdun cu rtsa lnga zhes/ grangs nyid kyis ni legs grangs nas/ dge ba'i lha yis bys pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i legs par sbyar ba las/ yongs su bsngo ba bstan pa ste le'u bcu pa'o/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI ku mA ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i rtog par dka' ba'i gnas brten la phab pa'i gzhung / slob dpon mkhas pa chen po kr-iSh+Na ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kr-iSh+Na pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyi sgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
shes rab le'u'i dka' 'grel rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta mi mnyam khol po dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba/ li ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan mos pa'i dbang gis 'grel pa 'di legs bsgyur//
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i rnam par bshad pa rdzogs so//
gser gling gi bla ma chos skyong la/ gus pa dang ldan pa'i slob ma ka ma la rak+Shi ta dang / dI paM ka ras gsol ba btab nas/ spyod pa la 'jug pa'i don bcu gcig pa las phye ba sum cu rtsa drug gi don bsdus pa logs su bkod pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
gser gling gi bla ma chos skyong pas/ gus pa dang ldan pa'i slob ma ka ma la rak+Shi ta dang / dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas gsol ba btab nas/ spyod pa la 'jug pa'i gtso bo'i don bcu gcig bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon 'phags pa dpal zhi ba'i lha'i zhabs kyi mdzad pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa'i dgongs pa 'grel pa khyad par gsal byed ces bya ba rig pa'i 'byung gnas dbus 'gyur gyi shar phyogs pa ren drar rgyal rigs las 'khrungs shing / sa bcu'i dbang phyug rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis rjes su bzung ba/ rigs pa'i gnas rnam pa lnga la mkhas shing tshul khrims dri ma med pa'i brgyan gyis spras pa/ rim pa gnyis kyi don la rgyud legs par spyangs pas lam gyi rtogs pa gong nas gong du cher 'phel ba/ rtsod pa'i dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis par grags pa/ ma 'ongs pa'i sangs rgyas kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po bsod snyoms pa shAkya shrI b+ha dra la sogs pa paNa grub du ma'i legs bshad kyis/ thugs kyi bum pa legs par bltams pas phyogs phyi nang gi theg pa ma lus pa la mnga' brnyas shing / sgra dang tshad ma'i mig gis shes byi'i nyid gzigs pa/ rgya gar shar phyogs dza ga ta la bi ha ra'i paN+Di ta chen po shrI bi b+hU ti tsan dras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po de nyid kyi rus lag gtsang stod 'bring 'tshams kyi sa'i cha dpal rgya rtags kyi gtsug lag khang du rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
bden pa gnyis rnam par gtan la phab pa yang dag par mthong bar brtson pa slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len+dra b+ho d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bden pa gnyis rnam par gtan la dbab pa/ yang dag par mthong bar brtson pa slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so// paN+Di ta shI len+dra b+ho d+Hi dang ban+de ye shes sde'i 'gyur//
bden pa gnyis rnam par 'byed pa'i dka' 'grel/ slob dpon zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
dbu ma rgyan gyi tshig le'u byas pa/ slob dpon zhi ba 'tsho bdag dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa/ 'phags pa ngag gi dbang phyug gi zhabs kyi pad+ma rnyog pa med pa'i ze'u 'bru spyi bos len pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dbu ma rgyan 'di slob dpon zhi ba 'tsho bdag dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' yis rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa/ 'phags pa ngag gi dbang phyug gi zhabs kyi pad+ma rnyog pa med pa'i ze'u 'bru spyi bos len pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ren+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dbu ma'i rgyan gyi dka' 'grel slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la sh+lo ka stong sum brgya brgyad bcu yod//
bstan bcos dbu ma snang ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang /bod kyi lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi basgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
de kho na nyid snang ba zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
chos thams cad rang bzhin med pa nyid du grub pa/ slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//

sku gsum la 'jug pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos slob dpon klu'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA na warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sku gsum 'grel pa/ slob dpon ye shes zla bas bgyis pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA na varma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ 'di la sh+lo ka ni brgya drug cu mchis so//
de kho na la 'jug pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon dpal sbas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dbu ma'i lugs kyi snying po mdor bsdus pa'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon bid+yA ka ra pra b+hasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra pra b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o
rnam pa med pa'i tshig le'u'a byas pa/ bal yul gyi paN+Di ta dga' ba'i dpal gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
snang ba'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ka ma la'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mA ra ka la sha dang / lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
snang ba'i phreng ba zhes bya ba'i dka' 'grel yid dga' ba bskyed pa zhes bya ba/ dge bsnyen btsun pa ngo bo nyid med pa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mA ra ka la sha dang / dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur//
dus byas dang 'dus ma byas rnam par nges pa zhes bya ba/ shAkya'i dge slong paN+Di ta gnas brtan chen po stobs cu dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'o//
lta ba tha dad pa rnam par phye ba mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon dbu ma'i seng+ge'i zhal snga nas bshad pa rdzogs so/ /'di ni paN+Di ta chen po dbu ma'i seng+ge zhes bya bas rtsod pa chen pa'i dus su ji skad bshad pa rnams mkhas pa dag gis gzung ste/ gcig nas gcig tu bshad pa gtam gyi man ngag ces bya bar grags pa la slad kyi gzhung du bkod pa'i/ gcig nas gcig tu byung pa/ mngon par brtson pa'i dge bsnyen pa'i dge bsnyen ta ra shrI mi tras byas/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ta ro shrI mi tra nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis zhus cing bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
bde bar gshegs pa'i gzhung rnam par 'byed pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ b+hang+ga lar 'khrungs pa'i mkhas pa chen po mdzo tA ris mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gcig tu gzhol ba'i slob dpon dgra las rgyal bas mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhas pa chen po ka na ka shri mi tra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de shes rab grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan l aphab pa'o//
dbu ma rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta chen po rtsan+d+ra ha ri pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba cog ro ting 'dzin bzang pos bsgyur pa//
bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng ges bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mkhas pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' rab 'byams la shes pa'i snang ba skyes pa'i mkhas pa chen po de nyid las mnyan nas/ de nyid kyi zhal sngar shAkya'i dge slong spong zho gsal ba grags zhes bya bas/ yul dbus kyi grong khyer chen po mkhas pa'i 'byung gnas dpal nA len drar bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ dus phyis lung dang rigs pa'i dbang phyug stag sde pa chen po seng+ge rgyal mtshan gyis bka' drin dang / de nyid kyi sras kyi thu bo bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i blo gros kyi stobs kyis matha' yas pa'i shes bya'i chos la dbang sgyur ba shong ston lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis legs par bshad pa'i srol la sogs pa las brten nas/ phyi dang nang gi gzhung lugs du ma rnams la bla'i snang ba char rgyas pa/zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dpang dge slong dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas/ dge ba'i bshas gnyen dog shing dbon po dang / bde ba chos kyi bzang po la sogs pas/ mthun rkyen bsgrub pa la brten nas/ legs par bcos nas/ dag par bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ slar yang dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa de nyid kyis gzhungs 'di'i skabs su/ gzhung lugs gzhan gyi skabs mthun pa ji snyed snyed pa rnams sbyar zhing rgya dpe dang gtugs te legs par brtags shing dpyad nas zhu chen bgyisla/ don la'ang legs par dpyad pas shin tu dag par bgyis pa'o//

theg pa chen po'i mtshan nyid kun las btus pa/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta kar+No pa ti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong pradz+nyA sing has dpal nA lan+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang chen por bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sems brtag pa slob dpon tshul khrims 'phags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta ka na ka dang / lo tsA ba chos 'bar gyis zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
theg pa thams cad du snang bar byed pa'i bye brag tu bshad pa zhes bya ba/ bram ze'i btsun pa rab 'byor dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta rab 'byor dbyangs de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong teng nge 'dzin bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//

'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i sgom pa'i rim pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta lo ta dang dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur//
rnal 'byor sgom pa'i lam/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi zhabs kyi pad ma'i ze 'bru spyi bos len pa/ sde snod gsum la mkhas pa/ slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
cig car 'jug pa rnam par mi rtog pa bsgom don/ slob dpon chen po'i bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma tA shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o
kun rdzob byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa'i man ngag yi ge pad+ma spungs pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rta dbyangs kyis zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra warma dang /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
don dam pa byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa'i yi ge rin po che'i sgron ma zhes bya ba brim pa yi ger bris pa/ slob dpon chen po rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra varma dang /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
zha lu lo tsA ba dge slong dh+rma pA la b+ha dra zhes bgyi bas grwa thang du bsgyur ba'o//
tshad med bzhi'i rgya cher 'grel pa slob dpon bud+d+hA gup+tasa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sa'i mnga' bdag dpal lha btsan pos bka' stsal nas/ ka ma la shI las sgom pa'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa 'di bgyis so/ sgom rim dang po rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sgom pa'i rim pa A tsar+ya ka ma la shI las bar du mdzad pa rdzogs sa/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA varma dang / lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sgom pa'i rim pa slob dpon A tsaR+Ya ka ma la shI las tha mar mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA varma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rnal 'byor sgom pa la 'jug pa/ slob dpon chen po ka ma la shI la'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA varma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag ces bya ba dpal kam pa las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
lus yongs su dpyad pa'i bsgom pa'i rim pa slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
mi gcing bsgom pa'i thabs bshad pa/ slob dpon dge ba'i go chas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /'di ni sngon gyi lo tsA ba chen po rnams kyis bsgyur ba te/ 'gyur snying lags skad do//

sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bla na med pa'i mdo'i rjes su 'gro ba zhes bya ba/ dkyil 'khor chen po'i slob dpon ma hA ma ti'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /a tsar+ya bi na ya tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs kyi le'u zhes bya ba/ slob dpon byang chu bzang po mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po biR+Ya tsan+d+ra las zhus te/ bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
ting nge 'dzin tshogs kyi le'u slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kriSh+Na pa de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bsam gtan gyi chos drug rnam par bzhag pa slob dpon chen po a ba d+hu ti pas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bsam gtan gyi chos drug rnam par bzhag pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon d+ha na shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA shrI b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
cig char 'jug pa'i man ngag paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
dbu ma'i man ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas lha sa 'phrul snang du bsgyur cing zhus te/ gtan la phab pa'o/ ra sa 'phrul snang gtsug lag khang chen du/ mar me mdzad dpal zhes bya'i mkhas pa la/ bod kyi rdog btsun legs pa'i shes rab kyis/ gsol ba btab nas bdag gis bsgyur ba yin/ gnas brtan mar me mdzad dpal gyis/ gzhung lugs skyes bu gsum 'dzin pa/ gol ba'i lam du mi 'gro zhes/ nags tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba smra/
theg pa chen po dbu ma'i man ngag rin po che'i za ma tog kha phye ba zhes bya ba/ ma hA paN+Di ta dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge bsnyen chen po rgya brtson 'grus seng ge dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dbu ma'i man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas/ lha sa 'phrul snang du bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dbu ma'i man ngag ces bya ba'i 'grel pa paN+Di ta she rab thar pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shes rab thar pa de nyid dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
ting nge 'dzin gyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs rnam par bzhag pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po hA shang zab mo la sogs pa dang / zhu chen gyis lo tsA ba ban+de rnam par mi rtog pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o
bsgom pa'i rim pa mdo kun las btus pa rdzogs so//
mdo sde sna tshogs las btus pa/ theg pa chen po rin che'i gtam/ A tsar+ya ar+ya nA ga rdzu nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mdo kun las btus pa'i bshad pa rin po che snang ba'i rgyan ces bya ba/ lung gi tshad mas rab tu sbyar ba las/ bsdus pa'i tshigs su bcad pa'o/ mdo kun las btus pa'i bshad pa / slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta nag po'i zhabs dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA ka ra warma dang / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhu te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na la bod kyi dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas gser srang bcu bzhi sbram bu me tog du phul nas bod du 'byon pa'i zhu ba phul pa las sgom spyod pa rnams mthar phyin par bya ba'i don du bla ma zla ba bcu drug tu lam du ma chud do/ de nas bod du 'byon khar slob ma sems sbyong ba rnams kyis zhal chems bzhag par zhus pas mdo'i don man ngag tu byas pa 'di zhal chems su gnang ngo / de'i dus su rgya brtson seng+gesa bsgyur bar zhus pas gnang ste gtan la phab po/ dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas spel bar 'dod pa las bod kyi ston pa rnams ni nga rgyal dang phrag dog che bas nga rgyal gyi sgang bu la yon tan gyi chu mi chags so/ de 'dra lha khang ke ru'i khyams smad kyi ban de bdag gyi zhus te gdams ngag dang bcas te gnang ngo/ jo bo'i bla ma a wa d+hU ti pas rab tu mi gnas pa'i lta ba dang / las mtha' sems bskyed pa'i cho ga dang / mdo kun las btus pa'i don man ngag tu byas pa 'di gsum stabs gcig tu gnang ba lags so//
rim gyis 'jug pa'i sgom don/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bslab pa kun las btus pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa zhes bya ba mkhan po zhi ba lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bslab pa kun las btus pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i 'dul ba mdo sde du ma las btus pa/ slob dpon zhi ba'i lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ slad kyi kha che'i paN+Di ta ti la ka kla shu dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis/sri mda'i dgon par zhusasa tug legs par byas pa'o//
bslab pa kun las btus pa las 'byung ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po yi ge brgya pa'i bsrung pa dang sdig pa bshags pa'i cho ga /slob dpon zhi ba'i lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bslab pa kun las btus pa'i mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /dpal mar me mdzad ye shes dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/ gser gling rgyal po dpal ldan chos skyod gis/ bcom ldan 'jam pa'i rdo rje mnyes byas pas/ bslab pa kun las btus pa'i mngon par rtogs/ ka ma la dang mar me mdzad la gsungs//
bslab pa me tog snye ma zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /bi kra ma la shI la'i paN+Di ta chen po bai ro tsa na rag Shi ta'i zhal snga nas sbyar ba'o/ dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag bod rje lha btsan po khri bkra shis nam mkha' dbang phyug btsan gyi bka' lung gis rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti kIrti dang / bod kyi lo tsA zha ma se dge slong seng rgyal dang / glog skya gzhon nu 'bar gyis bsgyur pa las/ slad nas bod kyi lo tsA ba ban+de mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
pha rol tu phyin pa bsdus pa slob dpon ar+ya shU ras mdzad pa'o// lo tsA ba a tsAr+ya bai ro tsa na rak+ Shi tas bsgyur ba'o//
las dang po pa'i sa sbyang pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mkhas pa chen po byang chub sems dpa' dgra las rgyal gsang ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po kriSh+Na pa dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams ngag tu byas pa/ slob dpon chen po dpal ma me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
byang chub lam gyi sgron ma/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa/ chos 'di ni zhang zhung gi tho ling gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa'o//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po/ bla ma byang chub sems dpa' b+ha ga la pa/ dpal mar me mdzad ye shes zhabs dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus//
snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims 'byung gnas de ba rtses bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//

rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i nor bu'i phreng ba rdzogs so//

theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs shin tu bsdus pa/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rang gyi bya ba'i rim pa bskul ba dang bcas pa yi ger bris pa/slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
mdo sde'i don kun las btus pa'i man ngag /slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po de nyid dang /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa/slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po de nyid dang /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
las rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang /mkhas pa chen zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma slob don mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal pas bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//

dge bsnyen rdo rje g.yung drung dang / bslab gus yid gzhungs gzhon nu shes rab dang / bzod ldan rin chen bzang po yongs la drin/ gdung brgyud sa las 'phags pa pa tshab ldang gi sras/ bslab gsum sgrub pas skyong bar 'jig rten rab grags pa/ da ltar lnga brgya'i dus kyi bstan pa'i srog 'dzin pa'i/ dge slong yon tan grags kyi rab tu bskul gyur pas/ kha che'i bram ze mkhas pa rgyal ba kun dga' dang / sgra bsgyur phul du phyin pa pa tshab khu gsum kyis/ ya rabs spyod pa ma nyams pa tshab rom po'i khul/ gnod sbyin nor spel grags pa zhogs lha phyug po'i 'dabs/ mkhas btsun bzhugs rjes skyod pa ya gad gtsug lag tu/ mdo sde kun las btus pa bsgyur cing legs par zhus/ bod 'bangs yongs la sman pas sa yang rab tu g.yos/ dge legs bsam pa dag pas dgongs pa mthar yang chub//
byang chub sems dpa'i lam gyi rim pa de kho na nyid bsdus pa/ dpal chos kyi rje sa'i steng na 'gran zla bral ba'i paN+Di ta chen po/ ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas gsum par yongs su grags pa'i kha che shAkya shrI bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po de nyid dang lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal ldan gyis rgyang ro sa lu'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas chos rje shAkya shrIs yul 'khor so sor byon pa'i tshe zhu ba po rnams kyi skal pa dang sbyar te zhar byung du brtsams shing gsungs pa'i tshigs su bcad pa kha 'thor ba rnams rdzogs so/ /dpal sa'i steng na 'gran zla dang bral ba'i ma hA paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur pa'o
gyal ba'i lam la 'jug pa zhes bya ba kha che'i rigs kyi paN+Di ta chen po rigs pa'i gnas lnga pa sbyangs shing byang chub kyi sems kyis brgyan pa bud d+ha shrI dz+nyA na zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rtsom pa'i tshad ldan paNa chen gyis mdzad rgyal ba'i lam 'jug 'di/ nyung la gsal rdzogs lung rigs dang 'brel don chen ldan mthong ste/ legs sbyar skad kyis dben pa'i mi rnams la ni phab 'dod nas/ rtsod dus skyes kyang rig gnas lnga sbyangs sdom gsum la gnas pa'i/ bod yul dbus kyi dge slong dgra bcom legs par mnyan te bsgyur/ phrag dog 'gran kheng dreg sems spangs te blangs na don chen 'gyur/ gang dag srid zhen bla zhan 'tsho med long med bsgom 'dod sogs/ thos bral rnams kyang 'di tsam cig nyan nus na thos mang 'gyur/ gzhung 'di'i tshad ni tshigs bcad stong dang gcig brgyas lhag pa ste/ sgra don dpyad nas bsgyur kyang nongs na mkhas rnams bzod par bzhes/ brtsams zhus bsgyur pa'i mkhan po gsum gyis 'bad 'bras 'di dar nas/ dge des bdag sogs 'gro kun rgyal ba'i lam zhugs kun mkhyen shog/ bsgyur pa'i dgos 'brel dang gzhan la gdams pa dang bzod par gsol ba dang bsngo//
spyod yul yongs su dag pa'i mdo'i don mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon dpal sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal chos kyi rje sa'i steng na 'gran zla dang bal ba kha che shAkya shrI bzang po dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur ba'o།།
byang chub tu sems bskyed pa'i cho ga /slob dpon mkhas pa chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ren dra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa'i cho ga /slob dpon mkhas pa chen po byang chub bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bla ma pu n+ya shrI mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa dang yi dam blang ba'i cho ga //slob dpon mkhas pa chen po byang chub sems dpa' dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po su ma ti kIrti dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
byang chub sems bskyed pa dang byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa'i cho ga / slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur ba lags so/ slad kyi paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bcos shing gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon mkhas pa chen po 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pas sdus pa'i sdom pa bzung ba'i cho ga rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / chag lo tsA ba dge slong dgra bcom gyis bsgyur pa'o//
gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba bdun cu pa/ slob dpon zla ba grags pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
skyabs 'gro yan lag drug pa/ slob dpon bi ma las mdzad pa rdzogs so
ltung ba bshags pa'i cho ga thams cad yod par smra ba'i paN+Di ta de ba shAn+tisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
ltung ba bshags pa'i cho ga slob dpon mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
kha ton dang glegs bam bklag pa'i sngon du bya ba'i cho ga slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzadpa rdzogs so//
bla ma'i bya ba'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa /slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sdom pa gsum gyi rim pa/ slob dpon chen po rnyog med rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a tu l+ya dA sa dang /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
chos spyod yan lag bzhi pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po shI dza ga ta mi tra A nan+dasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug de nyid dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur pa'o//
dam pa'i chos spyod la 'jug pa'i yan lag bdun pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po shAkya shrI b+ha dras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur pa'o//
'phags pa dgongs pa nges par 'grel pa'i rnam par bshad pa slob dpon thog med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyis mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len dra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon thog med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
chos rjes su dren pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon thog med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dge 'dun rjes su dran pa'i bshad pa slob dpon thog med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dge slong a dzi ta shrI b+ha drA dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur te gtan la phab pa//
'phags pas lu ljang pa'i mdo tshig le'ur bya pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sA lu ljang rgya cher bshad pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI pra b+ha dang / lo tsA ba ban+de legs pa'i blo gros dang / dz+nyA ku mA ras bsgyur/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis zhus nas gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon dbye gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dA na shI la dang / zhu chen chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
tshigs su bcad pa gcig pa'i bshad pa/ bstan bcos tshigs su bcad pa bsdus pa las byung ba/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa sgo drug pa'i gzungs kyi rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa chos bzhi pa'i rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so
'phags pa chos bzhi pa'i rgya cher bshad pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon ye shes byin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dA na shI la dang/ pradz+nyAwarma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa ga ya mgo'i ri zhes bya ba'i mdo'i rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ren dra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa ga ya go ri'i mdo dang spel mar bshad pa/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gtso bo'i zhabs la brten pa/ mang du thos pa gnas brten shAkya'i blos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa sa bcu las/ sa bcu pa chos kyi sprin zhes bya ba'i rnam par bshad pa rdzogs te/ sa bcu'i rnam par bshad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po many+dzu shrI gar+b+ha dang / pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde dang /ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur te zhus nas gtan la phab pa'o//

'phags pa blo gros mi zad pa'i mdo rim gyis mi zad pa rnams kyi lus rnam par bzhag pa ni rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa las bstan pa te/ der blta bar bya'o/ 'phags pa bla gros mi zad pas bstan pa'i bshad pa rdzogs so//
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba dang po dang rnam par 'byed pa'i mdo sde rnam par 'grel pa slob dpon ba su ban+dusa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /li'i mkhan po su ran+d+ra ka ra pra b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong nam mkhas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba thog ma dang rnam par 'byed pa'i mdo sde'i 'grel pa rgya cher bshad pa rdzogs so/ /'di mdzad pa'i slob dpon ni yon tan blo gros yin te/ theg pa chen po pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yin no/ li'i mkhan po su ren dra ka ra pra b+ha dang / lo tsA ba nam mkhas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon ngang tshul bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//

'phags pa sa bcu'i rnam pa bshad pa'i rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon nyi ma grub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma pa dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa sa bcu'i mdo sde'i gleng gzhibshad pa/ slob dpon shAkya'i blos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa rnam par mi rtog par 'jug pa'i gzungs kyi rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon ka mA la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
phags pa sA lu ljang pa'i mdo sde'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshigs su bcad pa gnyis pa'i bshad pa slob dpon chen po mdzes bkod kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa 'da' ka ye shes kyi mdo'i rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon pradz+nyA sa mu dras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
phags pa 'da' ka ye shes kyi mdo'i don gsal ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon zhi ba lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma rA dza dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o
byang chub kyi ltung ba bshags pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon chen po 'phags pa klu grub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAn+ta rak+Shi ta dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rnyi pa de ba g+ho Shasa bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub kyi ltung ba bshags pa'i 'grel pa byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dzai tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal po paN+Di ta dang / chags lo tsA bas bsgyur ba'o//
las kyi sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i cho ga bshad pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
phung po gsum pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon kr-iSh+Na pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nya na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
'phags pa dkon mchog brtsegs pa chen po chos kyi rnam grangs le'u stong phrag brgya pa las 'od srungs kyi le'u rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon blo brtan gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//

'phags pa kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i smon lam gyi rgyal po chen po'i bshad sbyar slob dpon klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i mkhan po thig li bum pa dang / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po shAkya'i dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
phags pa bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyis rgyal po'i bshad pa/ slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyis rgyal po'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon shAkya'i bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAkya sim ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis zhus nas gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyis rgyal po'i rgya cher 'grel pa/ slob dpon rgyan bzang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / zhu chen chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa bzang po spyod pa'i smon lam gyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta a tsaR+Ya a nan+da dang / lo tsA ba dge slong b+ha dra pA las bsgyur pa'o//




mdo sde dgongs pa zab mo nges par 'grel pa rgya cher 'grel pa/ rgya'i slob dpon wen tshig gis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong 'gos chos grub kyis rgya'i dpe las bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
dam pa'i chos pad+ma dkar po'i 'grel pa yul sing+ga la'i blon po sa'i rtsa lag gis byas pa rdzogs so//
'phags pa lang+ka ra gshegs pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon ye shes dpal bzang pos sbyar ba dge legs su gyur cig/

'phags pa lang+ka ra gshegs pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo'i 'grel pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po'i rgyan zhes bya ba/ rgya'i mkhan po dz+nyA na badz+rasa mdzad pa rdzogs so//
theg pa chen po mdo sde'i rgyan gyi tshig le'ur byas pa/ rje btsun byams pa mgon pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAkya sing ha dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ slad kyi paN+Di ta pa ra hi ta dang / bram ze chen po sad dza na dang /lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis cung zad bcos legs par bshad nas gtan la phab pa'o//
dbu dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa'i bstan bcos/ mgon po byams pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta shAn+ti b+ha dra dang zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa las/ slad kyi kha che'i mkhan po paN+Di ta pa ra he ta dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dga' rdor gyis thugs dam sa tho ling gi gtsug lag kang du bcos shing gtan la phab pa//
chos dang chos nyid rnam par 'byed pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ mgon po byams pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po ma hA dza na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong bsnyen seng+ge rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
theg pa chen po rgyud bla ma'i bstan bcos/ mgon po byams pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal grong khyer dpe med kyi mkhas pa chen po/ bram ze rin chen rdo rje'i dpon po paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po sa dza na dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis/ grong khyer dpe med de nyid du bsgyur pa'o//
'phags pa mgon po byams pas mdzad pa/ theg pa chen po rgyud bla ma'i bstan bcos rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon thogs med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal grong khyer chen po dpe med kyi mkhas pa chen po bram ze rin chen rdo rje'i dpon po/ paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po sa dza na dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis/ grong khyer dpe med de nyid du bsgyur pa'o//
theg pa chen po'i mdo sde'i rgyan gyi bshad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAkya sing ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//

bstan bcos dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa las theg pa bla na med pa zhes bya ba'i tshig le'ur bcad pa lnga pa'i 'grel pa ste/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len dra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
chos dang chos nyid rnam par 'byed pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta ma hA dza na dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
theg pa chen po'i mdo sde'i rgyan gyi rgya cher bshad pa/ slob dpon ngo bo nyid med pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAkya sing ha dang zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
mdo sde rgyan las dang po'i skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa gnyis pa'i bshad pa/ kha che yul gyi mkhas pa chen po dpal btsun pa so ma shrI'i zhal snga nas gyi zhabs kyi pad+ma'i zi'i 'bru'i rdul gyis reg pa/ slob dpon gzhan la phan pa bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /thugs dam sa khwa char gyi dpal yid bzhin lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang du kha che'i mkhan po paN+Di ta sa ra hi ta b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong gzhon nu mchog gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ slar yon tan rgya mtsho mched kyis lan cig zhus so//
theg pa chen po'i mdo sde rgyan gyi don bsdus pa/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dz+nyA na shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi brtson 'grus kyis bsgyur ba'o//
bstan bcos dbus dang mtha' rnam par 'byed pa las/ theg pa bla na med pa'i le'ur bcad pa lnga'i 'grel pa bshad de/ slob dpon blo brtan gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa dgongs pa nges par 'grel pa'i mdo las 'phags pa byams pa'i le'ur bshad pa/ slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so／／


theg pa chen po mdo sde brgyan gyi 'grel pa rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon chen po bla gros bstan pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /mang yul du mkhan po mu ne tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba lce bkra shis kyis TI ka rnam gnyis kyi gzhi bzung ste/ mkhan pos kyang ci mkhyen du TI ka gsar du bsgyur pa rnam pa gnyis dang gtugs na yang/ TI ka gsar pa las mi mngon bdag 'di las zhib tu 'chad pa 'di yang gces par bgyi'o/ mjug cung zad cig ma tshang ba 'di stor bas TI ka gnyis dang gtug cing bgyi lags so//
'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa las/ phung po mdo pa'i sa rdzogs te/ sa mang po rdzogs so/ /'di la sh+lo ka ni brgyad stong dgu brgya brgyad cu rtsa bzhi yod do//

'phags pa thogs med kyi mdzad pa nyan thos kyi sa rdzogs so/ /'di la sh+lo ka drug stong yod do//
byang chub sems dpa'i sa'i go rims rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba / ban+de mkhan po ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ sh+lo ka drug stong bdun brgya lnga bcu yod do//


rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa rnam par gtan la dbab pa bsdu pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / su ren dra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa las mdo sde'i gzhi bsdu pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ rnal 'byor spyod pa gzhi bsdu pa sh+lo ka drug stong brgya dgu rtsa gsum mchis so/ lan cig zhus//

'dul ba 'du ba rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa las rnam grangs bsdu pa rdzogs so/ /'di la sh+lo ka bdun brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga yod do//
rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa 'di ni 'phags pa thogs med bdag dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu byon pa chos kyi rgyun gyi ting nge 'dzin byang bar brnyes pa/ 'phags pa mi pham pa'i zhabs kyi pad+ma rnyog med pa'i ze'u'i 'bru spyod pas len par mdzad pa ste/ rnal 'byor pa bdag dang gzhan gyi don sgrub par byed pa bla na med pa'i byang chub kyi phyir go cha chen po bgos pa rnams kyis dang du blang bar bya'o/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / su ren+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes zhus te gtan la phab pa// 'di la sh+lo ka lnga brgya bdun cu rtsa lnga yod do/ spyir sh+lo ka bzhi khri lnga stong yod do/ bam po ni brgya dang lnga bcu yod do//
