sbyin pa rim par phye ba ste dgu pa rdzogs so/ tshul khrims rim par phye ba ni gong du phyung ba yin/ slob dpon yon tan 'do kyis mdzad pa byang chub sems dpa'i sa'i 'grel pa las ji snyed 'gyur ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ rgya gar gyi dpe bying nas yi ge ma mthong bas 'phro lus te da dung bam po bdun tsam yod do//
byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims kyi le'u bshad pa slob dpon yon tan 'od kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims kyi le'u rgya cher 'grel pa slob dpon rgyal ba'i sras kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sa'i dngos gzhi las/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa'i rgya cher 'grel pa slob dpon rgya mtsho sprin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lha btsun pa byang chub 'od kyi bka' lung gis bal yul gyi paN+Di ta chen po shAn+ti b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur pa'o//

heg pa chen po bsdus pa/ slob dpon thogs med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang ban+de ye shes sde'i 'gyur//
chos mngon pa kun las btus pa slob dpon thogs med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
theg pa chen po bsdus pa'i 'grel pa/ theg pa chen po la rab tu gnas pa bstan bcos phul du byung ba du ma mdzad pa'i slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas/ yul brag dmar lha sdings/ ri has po ri'i rtse/ chu bo lo hi ti'i 'gram/ dpal bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gnas/ dbyig 'du dpe dkar gling du bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la sh+lo ka nyis stong chig brgya brgyad cu yod do/ bam po brgyad du byas so//
theg pa chen po bsdus pa'i bshad sbyar/ slob dpon dge bsnyen btsun pa ngo bo nyid med pa chos rnams sgyu ma lta bu'i ngo bo nyid du thugs su chud pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la sh+lo ka ni nyis stong bdun brgya bdun cu rtsa bzhi yod do//
don gsang ba rnam par phye ba bsdus te bshad pa rdzogs//
chos mngon pa kun las btus pa'i bshad pa/ slob dpon rgyal ba'i sras kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI lan+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ bam po ni bcu yod do//
chos mngon pa kun btus pa'i rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rgyal pa'i sras kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ rtsa 'grel 'di gnyis sngon gyi chos skyong ba'i mi dbang phyug rnams kyi bka' drin las/ lo paNa ches cher mkhas pa rnams kyis legs par bsgyur te gtan la phab mod kyi/ 'on kyang rgya gar gyi dpe la 'grel pa'i nang na rtsa ba'i tshig yongs su rdzogs par yod pa dang / skabs la lar 'grel pa chad pa dang / de ltar dris lan dang mtshams sbyor gyi tshig chad pa dang / 'grel pa'i tshig gong 'og tu ha cang bsgyur ches par bsgyur pa dang / 'grel pa'i tshig ji lta ba ma yin par don rtsam bsdus te bsgyur ba dang / mdor bstan dang / rgyas bshad mi mtshungs par bsgyur ba dang / rang bzor bsdu pa'i tshigs bcad byas la sogs pa'i skyon 'ga' zhig mthong ste/ slar yang rgya gar gyi dpe dang mthun par mang du thos pa'i lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ gtsug lag khang chen po dpal thar pa gling du cung zad dag par bcos pa'o//

sum cu ba'i tshig le'ur byas pa slob dpon chen po dbyig gnyen mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur zhing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
nyi shu pa'i tshig le'u byas pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan pa dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon dbyin gnyen gyi mdzad pa'i nyi shu pa'i 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes zhus te gtan la phab pa//
slob dpon dbyin gnyen gyi mdzad pa'i rang bzhin gsum nges par bstan pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lha btsas kyis gtan la phab ste legs par bsgyur ba'o//
phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan pa dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rnam par bshad pa'i rigs pa'i mdo sde'i dum bu brgya rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bu shud+ha sid+ha dang / sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / lo tsA ba ban+de rtsangs de ben+t+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de many+dzu shrI warmas zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rnam par bshad pa'i rigs pa las le'u bcad pa lnga pa ste/ rnam par bshad pa'i rigs pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi shud+d+ha sid+ha dang / shAkya sid+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de rtsangs de ben+d+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
las grub pa'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi shud+d+ha sid+ha dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rtsangs ban+de de ben+d+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing / zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis zhus te gtan la phab pa//
theg chen chos brgya gsal ba'i sgo'i bstan bcos yongs su rdzogs so/ /rgya'i dpe la slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyi mdzad pa snang /ding sang bod rnams dpal ldan chos skyong gis mdzad ces grags so/ dpal ldan dbang phyug rgya'i lo tsA ba thang sam tsang zhes bya bas rgya gar las rgya'i yul du bsgyur zhing / phyis ston pa dge slong chos kyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya bas bsgyur par zhus pa'i don du gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i sde pa las rab tu byung ba rgya nag chen po'i lha btsun chos kyi rin chen gyis dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur zhing legs par gtan la phab pa'o//
sum cu pa'i bshad pa slob dpon blo brtan gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rab tu byed pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel bshad/ slob dpon dul ba'i lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa bye brag tu bshad pa/ slob dpon blo gros brtan pa s+thi ra ma tis mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len dra bo d+hi dang / dA na shi la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
phung po lnga'i rnam par 'grel pa/slob dpon yon tan 'od kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
phung po lnga'i bshad pa slob dpon sa'i rtsa lag gis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rnam par bshad pa rigs pa'i bshad pa slob dpon yon tan bla gros kyi dzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi shud+d+ha sing ha dang / shAkya sing ha dang / lo tsA ba ban+de de wen+d+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la tshigs su bcad pa ni bzhi stong cig brgya yod do//

slob dpon dul ba'i lhas sum cu pa'i 'grel bshad byas pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / dA na shI la dang zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
las grub pa'i rab tu byed pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon dpal na len+d+ra'i gtsug lag khang chen po na gnas pa'i dge slong blo bzang ngang tshul gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi shud+d+ha sid+ha dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rtsangs de ben+d+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o//
bsam gtan gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba'i man ngag gi snying po slob dpon 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rnal 'byor la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon phyogs kyi glang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i man ngag slob dpon chos kyi dbang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza rat+na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa'i man ngag slob dpon mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lha btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
rnal 'byor spyod pa'i bsgom pa'i don mdor bsdus te bsten pa/ slob dpon ye shes zla bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ lo tsA ba slob dpon klu yi bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa lags so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mang ngag paN+Di ta chen po rat+na ka ra shAn+tisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po dpal rab 'byor zhi ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA badge slong ting nge 'dzin bzang pos sgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mang ngag paN+Di ta chen po rat+na ka ra shAn+tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po zhi ba bzang po dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bi kra ma shI la'i paN+Di ta rat+na kIrtisa mdzad pa dge ba'i sdong po zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta bi d+yA ka ra sing+ha dang / lo tsA ba many+dzu shrI warmasa bsgyur ba'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa nyi shu pa/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
sdom pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon shAn+ta rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra sing+ha dang zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba many+dzu shra warmas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa nyi shu pa'i dka' 'grel/ slob dpon byang chub bzang po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta k+She la ka ga na dang / lo tsA ba mang 'or dge slong byang chub shes rab kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
paN+Di ta chen po rat+na kIrtisa mdzad pa'i chos rnam par nges pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po rat+na kIrti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chings yon tan 'bar gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba/ g.yo sgyus spyod pa tshar gcod bsnyon 'debs gnad la 'bebs/ rtog ge'i srog shing kun mkhyen ye shes rgyal mtshan can/ theg chen rnam rig dbu ma'i rgyan kyi man ngag bcas/ legs mdzad gang de zla grags 'joms pa'i rtog ge yin/ slad nas a che a mo ka dang 'o ru lo tsA bas zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa maung+gal gyi bus mdzad pa'i 'jig rten bzhag pa rdzogs so// 'di la 'gyur byang las bam po bdun 'byung yang dongs su dgu snang ngo//
rgyu gdags pa rdzogs te gnyis pa'o/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
las gdag pa bshad pa ste gsum pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//

chos mngon pa'i mdzod kyi tshig le'u byas pa/ slob dpon shAkya'i dge slong dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
chos mngon pa'i mdzod kyi bshad pa las/ phra rgyas bstan pa zhes bya ba mdzod kyis gnas lnga pa'o//
chos mngon pa'i mdzod kyi bshad pa slob dpon shAkya'i dge slong dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o //
chos mngon pa'i mdzod kyi bstan bcos kyi 'grel pa mdo dang mthun pa zhes bya ba slob dpon 'dus bzang gis mdzad pa rdzogs so//

chos mngon pa'i mdzod kyi 'grel bshad don gsal zhes bya ba slob dpon rgyal po'i sras grags pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa las/ 'jig rten bstan pa zhes bya ba ste mdzod kyis gnas gsum pa'o//
chos mngon pa'i mdzod kyi 'grel bshad don gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rgyal po'i sras grags pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi shud+ha sing+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la sh+lau ka ni khri brgyad stong yod do/ bam po ni drug cur byas so//

slob dpon gang ba spel pas mdzad pa chos mngon pa'i mdzod kyi 'grel bshad mtshan nyid kyi rjes su 'brang ba zhes bya ba las/ 'jig rten bstan pa zhes bya ba mdzod kyi gnas gsum pa'i 'grel bshad do//
slob dpon gang ba spel ba zhes bya ba/ chos mngon pa'i gzhung gang chen mtsho'i pha rol tu son pas mdzad pa/ chos mngon pa mdzad kyi 'grel bshad/ mtshan nyid kyis rjes su 'brang ba zhes bya ba 'di ni/ gangs ri chen po te se dang / yid bzhin gyi mtsho'i lho ngos ri bo chen po spos kyi ngad ldan pa'i 'dab yul pu rangs su/ dge 'dun gtse gyur pa brgya phrag gcig dang / dge 'dun spyir gyis g.yu phag sgur la sogs pa phul ta/ bkas gnyar nas/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka na ka warma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur ba zhig go

chos mngon pa mdzod kyi rnam par bshad pa nye bar mkho las/ gnas bzhi pa phal cher mdo dang sbyar ba rdzogs so/ /slob dpon bal po zhi gnas lhas mdzad
chos mngon pa mdzod kyi TI ka nye bar mkho ba zhes bya ba dge slong zhi gnas lhas yang dag par sbyar ba rdzogs so/ /gsung rab mdo sde stong gyi mdo khungs kyis/ chos mngon mdzod kyi bstan bcos brgyad pa 'di/ khams pa ston pas dad pas rab bsgyur las/ 'gro kun mngon pa'i chos kyi don rtogs shog /kha che'i grong khyer chen po dpe med kyi dbus dza ra me'i gtsug lag khang gi byang phyogs kyi bsil khang du/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzA ya shrI dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba khams pa dge slong shes rab 'od zer gyis yang dag par bsgyur pa//
tshig le'ur byas pa'i 'grel pa gnad kyi sgron ma zhes bya ba 'jam dbyangs phyogs kyi glang pos sbyar/ de nyid 'dzam gling nyi ma shAkya'i mtshan can chos rje de sras thub bor gyur pa yi/ paN chen rnal 'byor zla ba ltar grags mkhas mchog gang yin de dang 'jam dpal gzhon nus bsgyur//
slob dpon gang ba spel ba zhes bya ba chos mngon pa'i gzhung lugs rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pas mdzod pa chos mngon pa'i 'grel bshad mtshan nyid kyi rjes su 'brang ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /'di gangs chen po ti si dang yid bzhin gyi mtsho'i lho ngos ri bo chen po spos kyi ngad ldang pa'i 'dab/ yul pu rangs su dge 'dun gtso bor gyur pa brgya phrag gcig dang / dge 'dun spyir gyis g.yu phag skur la sogs pa phul te bkas gnyer nas rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka na warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis bsgyur pa zhig go/
chos mngon pa la 'jug pa rgya cher 'grel pa snying po kun las btus pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rab tu byed pa chos mngon pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so//

ched du brjod pa'i tshoms/ dgra bcom pa chos skyob kyis bsdus pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra pra b+hA dang / lo tsA ba ban+de rin chen mchog gis bsgyur/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis zhus nas gtan la phab pa/ 'di la sh+lau ka stong lnga brgya dang bzhi bcu bzhugs so//
ched du brjod pa'i tshoms kyi rnam par 'grel pa slob dpon shes rab go chas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ched du brjod pa'i tshoms kyi rnam par 'grel pa/ yul ka pa d+h+yar skyes pa thos pa mang pa'i slob dpon bo d+hi warma'i slob ma yul b+ha ga lar skye ba bzhes pa thams cad yod par sma ba'i slob dpon pradz+nyA warmas mdzad pa rdzogs so// 'grel pa 'di la sh+lau ka stong phrag bcu gnyis dang lnga brgya yod do/ zhes rgya gar gyi yi ge las smos/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po sgra'i gtsug lag 'byams par mkhas pa/ paN+Di ta dza na d+ha na dang zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de shAkya blo gros kyis bsgyur pa//
'phags pa chos kyi dbyings kyi snying po'i rnam par 'grel pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ye shes snying po dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bstan bcos tshigs su bcad pa bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA ka ra dang /lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes snying pos bsgyur te/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis zhus//
bstan bcos tshigs su bcad pa'i don bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA ka ra dang / lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes snying pos bsgyur te/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis zhus//

ltung byed dag gdon pa bshad zin to/
so sor thar pa'i mdo'i gzhung 'grel/ 'dul ba'i gzhung nyid las 'byung ba nyi tshe'i skabs bsgyur ba rdzogs so/ /dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag rgyal po chen po dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis/ 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la sh+lau ka ni dgu stong yod/ bam po nyi shu rtsa bdun du byas so//
'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba bsdus pa rdzogs so/ slob dpon khyad par bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'o/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAkya pra b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba bai ro tsa na rak+Shi tas bsgyur ba'o/ slad kyis kha che'i mkhan po dz+nyA na shrI b+ha drA dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rgyal ba shes rab dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong shAkya bshes gnyen gyis bcos shing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ snyan pa'i 'brug sgras 'dzam gling khyab gyur cig /rig pa'i gnas lnga zla ba'i 'od kyis blo'i ku mud rgyas/ rgyal bas lung bstan kha che'i grong khyer dpe med kyis/ dz+nyA na shrI la bod kyi rgyal po bkra shis rtse lde bkas/ rgyud bskul bod kyi spyi thun bsod nams dag gis ni/ tho ling gtsug lag khang du sku bskyod chos kyi sbrang rtsi yi/ 'gro ba tshim mdzad de la shAkya'i dge slong ni/ rgyal ba'i shes rab cis bya tshul khrims g.yag rnga dang / mig gi 'bras bu bzhin du srung zhing lung dang rtogs pa'i bdag nyid can/ snyan pa nam mkha' thugs rjes sprin can 'dul ba'i bdud rtsi yi/ char gyis rab byung tha ba'i rgyud spangs tshul khrims lo tog skyed mdzad pa/ skyes chen de yis 'gro la phan phyir dz+nyA shrI la zhus te/ 'dul 'dzin chen po de dang shAkya'i bshes gnyen gyis/ sngar 'gyur gyur ni mi zad ma dag pa yis phan pa chung dgongs nas/ legs par bcos nas zhu chen byas yin 'di la 'jug par rigs//

'thag pa bskyed pa'i spang ba ste nyi shu bzhi pa bshad zin to
bslab pa la nye bar 'jog pa spong ba'i ltung byed de bdun cu lng apa bshad zin to//

dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag rgyal po chen po dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis/ 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang /sarba dz+nya de ba dang bod kyi zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o// 'di la sh+lau ka ni khri lnga stong yod/ bam po ni lnga bcur byas so//
so sor thar pa'i mdo rgya cher 'grel pa rdzogs so//
so sor thar pa'i 'grel pa mi brjed pa'i dran byed tsam du bris pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza ran d+ha ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
so sor thar pa'i tshig gi brjed bya rdzogs so/ dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal/ lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yong par smra par 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mdo sde 'dzin pa ka l+yA na mi tras nye bar sbyar ba/ so sor thar pa'i tshig gi bshad pa dga' ba bskyed pa las/ gtsug lag khang ltung byed kyi rnam par nges pa'o//


'phags pa thams cad yod par smra ba'i rtsa ba'i dge slong ma'i so sor thar pa'i mdo'i 'grel pa rdzogs so//
'dul ba gzhi rgya cher 'grel pa slob dpon dge legs bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'dul ba rnam par 'byed pa'i tshig rnam par bshad pa slob dpon 'dul ba'i lhas nye bar sbyar ba rdzogs so/ dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gi 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa byed brag du smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'di la sh+lau ka ni lnga stong tshig rgya yod bam po ni bcu bdun du byas so//

lung phran tshegs kyi rnam par bshad pa/ slob dpon tshul khrims bskyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI bud+d+ha shAn+ti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
'dul ba lung bla ma'i bye brag lung zhu ba'i 'grel pa dge ba'i bshes gnyen rdzogs so//
'dul ba'i mdo rdzogs so/ 'dul ba'i mdo zhes bya ba nges par 'byung ba'i tshul khrims kyi dbang du byas pa/ 'dul ba rgya mtsho'i snying po mdor bsdus pa lhag pa'i tshul khrims kyi bslab pa mtha' dag gi mdzod du gyur pa/ 'dul ba'i sde snod thams cad kyi ma lta bu 'di ni 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po bram ze'i slob dpon btsun pa yon tan 'od bdag dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa/ bde bar gshegs pa'i chos 'dul ba bdud rtsi'i nying khus shes rab kyi dbang po rgyas ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' dam pa nan tan snying por bsgrubs pas sde pa thams cad kyi 'dul ba'i sde snod mtha' dag gi gtso bor gyur pa 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba kun las btus pa yin no/ dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ 'di la sh+lau ka nyis stong bdun brgya yod/ bam po dgur byas so//
las brgya rtsa gcig pa/ 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po bram ze'i btsun pa slob dpon yon tan 'od bdag dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa/ bde bar gshegs pa'i chos 'dul ba bdud rtsi'i nying khus shes rab kyi dbang po rgyas pa/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' dam pa nan tan snying por bsgrubs pas/ sde pa thams cad kyi 'dul ba'i sde snod mtha' dag gi gtso bor gyur pa/ 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba kun las btus pa rdzogs so/ dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ 'di la sh+lau ka sum stong bdun brgya yod/ bam po dgur byas so//

khri'i rkang pa 'chos pa'i ltung byed do//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta a lang+ka de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong tshul khrims 'byung gnas sbas pa gnyis kyis dpal sgye'u ri'i rtsa chos skor dben tsha'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur/ 'di la sh+lau la stong phrag bcu bzhi yod do//

gyal po'i pho brang du nub mo 'gro ba'i ltung byed do zhes bshad zin to//

'dul ba mdo rtsa ba'i rgya cher 'grel pa rdzogs so/ 'dul ba'i mdo zhes bya ba/ nges par 'byung ba'i tshul khrims kyi dbang du byas pa/ 'dul ba rgya mtsho'i snying po mdor bsdus pa/ lhag pa'i tshul khrims kyi bslab pa mtha' dag gi mdzod du gyur ba/ 'dul ba'i sde snod thams cad kyi ma lta bu/ 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po bram ze'i slob dpon btsun pa yon tan 'od/ bdag dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa/ bde ba gshegs pa'i chos 'dul ba bdud rtsi'i snying khus/ shes rab kyi dbang po rgyas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' dam pa nan tan snying por bsgrubs pas/ sde pa thams cad kyi 'dul ba'i sde snod mtha' dag gi gtso bor gyur ba/ 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod pa smra ba'i 'dul ba kun las btus pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa 'di ni 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul pa 'dzin pa chen po/ tho gar gyi bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon d+harma mi tra byas so/ rdzogs so/ dbang phyugs dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal ldan lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis/ 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ kha che'i bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de klu'i rgyal mtshan gyi bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa / 'di la sh+lau ka ni nyi khri tshig stong yod/ bam po ni bdun bcur byas so//

slob dpon yon tan 'od kyis mdzad pa'i 'dul ba mdo'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon pradz+nyA ka ras mdzad pa rdzogs so//
'dul ba'i mdo'i rtsa ba'i 'grel pa chud pa slob dpon mang du thos shing yon tan dang ldan pa yon tan gyi 'od thams cad yod par smra ba pas byas pa'o//

'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba tshig le'ur byes pa me tog phreng rgyud ces bya ba/ 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po 'phags pa dge 'dun 'bangs kyi slob ma/ dpal 'phags pa sa ga'i lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ bal po'i paN+Di ta dza yA ka ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong pradz+nyA na kIrtisa bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ rgya gar shar phyogs sad na ga ri'i paN+Di ta bA na rat+na ma hA thi bI ri la gtugs te/ sgra'i don la mkhas pa/ rong ston shes bya ba kun rig gis/ 'gyur cung zad bcos te gtan la phab pa'o//
gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i dge tshul gyi tshig le'ur byas pa/ mang du thos pa'i slob dpon shAkya 'od kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ nyan thos bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong de ben+d+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus pa'o//
'phags pa thams cad yod par smra ba'i dge tshul gyi tshig le'ur byas pa'i 'grel pa 'od ldan zhes bya ba mang du thos pa'i/ slob dpon chen po shAkya 'od kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de rtsangs de ben+d+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dge tshul gyi tshig le'ur byas pa sum brgya pa'i rnam par bshad pa slob ma la phan pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dul ba lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po bud+d+ha shan+ti dang / lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
thams cad yod par smra pa'i dge tshul gyi le'u byas pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po mu ne warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba sna nam ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dge sbyong gi kA ri kA lnga bcu pa mdo bshad tsam bshad pa/slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so//
thams cad yod par smra pa'i dge tshul gyi bya ba rdzogs so//
mdo sde 'dzin pa'i slob dpon ka l+yA na mi tra mdzad pa/ dge tshul gyis bslab pa'i gzhi'i mdo rdzogs so/ kha che'i mkhan po grong khyer dpe med kyi paN+Di ta ma hA dza na dang / shAkya'i dge slong gzhon nu mchog gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa las/ slad kyi kha che'i paN+Di ta pa ra he ta dang / lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong gzhin nu mchog gis bcos cing zhus pa'o//
byang phyogs kyi kha che'i yul nas byung ba'i paN+Di ta 'dul 'dzin pa shAkya'i dge slong ba la shrI b+ha tras mdzad pa gleng gzhi dang gang zag bsdus pa'i tshig le'u byas pa rdzogs so/ tho ling gis gtsug lag khang du rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong gzhon nu mchog gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dge tshul gyi dang po'i lo rdzogs so/ kha che'i mkhan po na ra sa de ba dang / lo tsA ba shA kya'i dge slong rgyal ba'i shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dge slong gi dang po'i lo dri ba rdzogs so/ dpal ra sa'i gtsug lag khang gi 'od mchog dngos grub gtsug lag khang du/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
'dul ba dri ba'i tshig le'u byas pa slob dpon mdo sde 'dzin pa ka l+yA pA mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA ka ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'dul ba dri ba'i tshig le'u byas pa'i gtan la dbab pa/ slob dpon mdo sde 'dzin pa ka l+yA pA mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ gal te bdag ni rmongs pa yis/ lan zhig legs par ma theb na/ 'di ni phyogs tsam bstan par byas/ mkhas pas bde legs gdab du gsol/ sdug cing gdung ba sel byas pa/ ji ltar 'dod pa'i 'bras bu ster/ sgrib ma sdug po'i shing mchog ltar/ gzhan don dga' ba'i phyir 'khrungs ba/ kun dga' go chas bdag la ni/ shin tu bcol te de yi phyir/ ci dran pa zhig 'bad de byas/ nga rgyal gyi ni phyir ma yin/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harmA ka ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la dbab pa/ sh+lau ka stong drug brgya drug cu rtsa bzhi yod do//
'dul ba la bstod pa btsun pa chos kyi tshong dpon gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'dul ba la bstod pa btsun pa chos kyi tshong dpon gyis mdzad pa slob dpon dul ba'i lhas bshad pa rdzogs so/ dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag btsan po'i bka' lung gis 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gzhung lugs kyi bye brag bkod pa'i 'khor lo btsun pa dbyin gi bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma ka ra dang / lo tsA ba ban+de bzang skyong gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sde pa tha dad pa bsdu pa dang rnam par bshad pa slob dpon b+a byas mdzad pa rdzogs so// ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang du dge slong legs pa'i shes rab kyis gsol ba btab nas rgya gar shar phyogs baM ga la'i mkhas pa chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nya na zhes bya ba'i paN+Di ta'i zhal sang nas dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
sde pa tha dad pa bstan pa bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon 'dul ba lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
ge bsnyen gyi sdom pa brgyad pa/ slob dpon chen po su na ya shrIs mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang lo tsA ba dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur pa'o//
dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa brgyad pa'i bshad pa/ slob dpon chen po su na ya shrIsa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po su na ya shrIsa dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong dar ma grags kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rnam par grol ba'i lam las sbyangs pa'i yon tan bstan pa zhes bya ba ste/ kun nas btus pa gsum pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+ya ka ra pra b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gser mdog gi rtogs pa brdzod pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
ku na la'i rtogs pa brjod pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+ma ka ra warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o
'phags pa dga' ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rtogs pa brjod pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur།།
gzhon nu ma bdun gyi rtogs pa brjod pa/ slob dpon gsang ba byin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
bslab pa bcua'i cho ga klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas gsungs pa rtse thang lo tsA ba gzhon nu'i zhabs kyi 'gyur//
'di ni slob rtag pa'i rdo rje'i gsung pa gzhon nus bsgyur ba'o//

skyes pa'i rabs kyi rgyud slob dpon 'phags pa dpa' bos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra sing+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de many+dzu shri warmas bsgyur te zhus nas gtan la phab pa'o//
skyes pa'i rabs kyi rgya cher bshad pa/ slob dpon d+harma kIrtis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta dzanAra d+ha na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba i bu dge slong shAkya blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
rgyal po'i sras slob dpon seng ge zhabs 'bring pas mdzad pa'i skyes pa'i rabs kyi phreng ba rdzogs so/ /dge slong dpal ldan blo gros 'byung gnas zhes bya mkhas pa ni/ sems can rnams la chos dang zang zing kun nas 'god mdzad cing / tshad ma dang ni lung rgyud rnams du ma la 'dris pas/ 'gro ba'i mnga' bdag ni spyod pa 'di la gnyis po dag /gzhal du med cing dri ma med pa kun nas bsags te de las 'di/ nyon mongs shes bya'i sgrib ba'i dri mchog bzhin du myur spangs sngon du 'gro ba ni/ de dang de'i skyes rabs yongs bzung 'gro ba sdug bsngal rgya mtsho las ni gdon byas te/ mthar yang thub dbang rnams bzhin mtha' dag bya byas sangs rgyas khams gsum du ni khyed 'byung shog /lcang lo can gyi bum pa zhes bya mkhas dang lhan cig 'di nyid du/ gang zhig tshul khrims 'byung gnas skad gnyis pas ni 'di ltar cho ga bzhin/ bdud las rnam par rgyal ba'i spyod pa shin tu rnam dag yangs pa ni/ skye ba ma lus pa la phan pa'i don du yis yang dag bsgyur/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta la ka de ba'i zhabs dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong tshul khrims 'byung gnas sbas dpa' gyi sgye'u ri'i rtsa chos skor dben sa'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur//
gzhon nu gtsug na nor bu'i skyes pa'i rabs zlos gar gyis bstan bcos 'jig rten kun tu dga' ba'i zlos gar zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mis rab tu sbyar ba'o/ dam pa rnams kyi tshul la brten nas paN+Di ta chen po kIrti tsan+d+ra dang / yar lungs pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bal yul grong khyer du legs par bsgyur ba'o//
klu kun tu dga' ba zhes bya ba'i zlos gar dpal dga' ba'i lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /yon tan 'phul du byed pa dpag tu med pas smras pa'i bla ma dam pa chos kyi rgyal po dang / dpon chen shAkya bzang po'i bka' lung gis/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po lak+ShI ka ra dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shong ston gyi dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur pa'o//

ces pa dge ba'i dbang pos byas pa'i rtogs brjod dpag bsam 'khri shing las glang po can gyi rtogs pa brjod pa'i yal 'dab ste bzhi bcu rtsa dgu pa'o//
byang chub sems dpa'i rtogs pa brjod pa dpag bsam gyi 'khri shing snyan dngags mkhan po dge ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /yon tan phul byud ba dpag tu med pas spras pa'i bla ma dam pa chos kyi rgyal po dang / mi'i dbang po dpon chen shAkya bzang po'i bka' lung gis/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po snyan dngags mkhan chen po lak+Shi mi ka ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shong ston gyi mang yul 'phags pa'i drung dge 'dun bzhi sde'i gtsug lag khang du zhus te gtan la phab pa'o// dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du rgya dpe dang gtugs nas zhus dag tshar bar byas so/ rgyal ba'i rtogs brjod snyan ngag chen po dpag bsan 'khri shing zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos skad gnyis zung du sbyar ba'dir/ yi ge pa dang dag byed pa'yi skyon las yig 'bru lhag chad brda nor 'khrul pa ji snyed mchis pa rnams 'di yi skad gnyis zung sbyar thog mar byed po 'jig rten mig 'gyur chos skyong bzang po zhes bya'i dge slong gis/ legs sbyar gzhung dang sdeb sbyor bstan bcos bod skad brda yi bstan bcos dang bstun blo gros zhib mos dag par bgyis//

yul shA ke ta ka'i gser mig ma'i bu dge slong slob dpon snyan dngags mkhan chen po/ smra ba dang ldan pa phyogs su rnam par grags pa/ btsun pa rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa'i/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba'i snyan dngags chen po las sku gdung rnam par bgo ba'i le'u ste/ nyi shu rtsa brgyad pa yongs su rdzogs so/ /sa steng rgya mtsho'i mthar thugs bstan pa'i bdag po'i mchog /yon tan mtshungs med phul byung du ma'i gter chen po/ mkhas pa rnams kyi bla ma skye dgu rnams kyi dpal/ bla ma dam pa chos kyi rgyal po'i bka' lung gis/ 'jig rten kun na zla bral skyes mchog de nyid kyi/ phrin las sgrub pa brnyes pa'i thugs dgongs rnam dag dang / mi rje lha sras gung thang rgyal mo yum sras dang / chos la gcig tu dkar ba'i lha cig kun dga' 'bum/ mang yul skyid rong bzo mo yon tan skyid la sogs/ chos ldan dam pa rnams kyis sbyin bdag bgyid pa'i ngor/ 'phags pa rta dbyangs kyis mdzad thub pa'i mdzad pa 'di/ sa dbang bzang po dang ni blo gros rgyal pos bsgyur//
byang chub sems dpa'i skyes pa'i rabs kyi chos kyi gaN+Di'i sgra bsgrags pa snyan dngags mkhan chen po slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal chos kyi rje sa'i steng na 'gran zla dang bral ba'i paN+Di ta chen po kha che shAkya bzang po dang / lo tsA ba dge slong byams pa'i dpal gyis bsgyur//
rgyal po la gtam bya ba rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na gar b+ha dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ slad kyi rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka na ka warma dang / lo tsA ba pa tshab nyi ma grags kyis rgya dpe gsum la gtugs nas legs bcos pa'o//
rin po che'i phreng ba'i rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon mi pham bshes gnyen gyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra pra b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal rtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rmi lam yid bzhin nor bu'i gtam slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta shrI ra tha dang / lo tsA ba dge slong grags 'byor shes rab kyis bsgyur//
slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa sbyin pa'i gtam rdzogs so//
srid pa las 'das pa'i gtam/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta shrI ra tha dang / lo tsA ba dge slong grags 'byor shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
yon tan bdun yongs su brdzod pa'i gtam slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta gang+gA d+ha ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
tshul khrims kyi gtam slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza ran d+ha na dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
tshul khrims kyi gtam gyi 'grel pa slob dpon gsal grags kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshogs kyi gtam slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po gang+gA d+ha ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mi khom pa brgyad kyi gtam/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI a dzi ta b+ha dra dang zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur//
legs par bshad pa rin po che'i za ma tog lta bu'i gtam snyan dngags chen po slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ru dra dang dge slong shAkya 'od kyi bsgyur//
phyin ci log bzhi spong ba'i gtam slob dpon mA ti tsi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bud+d+ha b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rtsod ba'i dus kyi gtam slob dpon mA ti tsi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur pa'o//
dben pa'i gtam slob dpon chen po sa 'tsho sbyin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM kA ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
chos smra ba dang dam pa'i chos nyan pa la gus par bya ba'i gtam slob dpon sa 'tsho sbyin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po gnas brtan a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o//
ched du brjod pa'i gtam drang srong chen po zla bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o//
mi rtag pa'i don gyi gtam zhes bya ba snyan dngags mkhan chen po dga' ba'i dbang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
legs pa'i lam bstan pa'i gtam las ti nge 'dzin gyi yan lag rnam par dag pa zhes bya ba phun sum tshogs pa gsum pa'o/ slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa legs pa'i lam bstan pa'i gtam rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba chen po dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ bam po phyed dang gsum mo//
dge ba bcu'i lam bstan pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon bram ze btsun pa chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bud+d+ha ka ra warma dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mya ngan bsal ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o//
dam pa'i chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pa'i 'gro drug gi tshig li'u byas pa/ slob dpon btsun pa chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma ka ra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rtsangs de ban+d+ra rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//
'dod pa'i yon tan lnga'i nyes dmigs bshad pa/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis dge slong rab gsal gzhon nu la springs pa'i phrin yig rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / lo tsA ba ban+de dpal rtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bshes pa'i phrin yig slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis/ mdza' bo rgyal po bde spyod la bkur ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal rtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob ma la springs pa'i 'phrin yig slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal rtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon mA tri tsi tras rgyal po chen po ka ni ka la springs pa'i 'phrin yig rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra pra b+hA dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de rin chen mchog gis bsgyur / a tsaR+Ya dpal rtsegs kyis zhus te gtan la phab pa//
sems rin po che rnam par sbyang ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i spring yig slob dpon byang chub sems dpa' chen po dgra las rgyal gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a tsar+ya du lo ba dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bla ma la springs pa dge slong dgon pa bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po a tsar+ya bi na ya tsan dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bu la springs pa paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po sad dza nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i mkhan po ma hA dza na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
dri ma med pa rin po che'i phrin yig ces bya ba/ gnas brtan mkhas pa chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas/ rgyal po nir pha la la brdzangs pa rdzogs so/ /dus de nyid du bla ma de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba/ sh+lau ka bzhi bcu pa'o//
gyal po zla ba la springs pa'i phrin yig /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug shrI dzA ga ta mi tra a nan+dasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug de nyid dang / bod kyi lo chung gnubs tshul khrims shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
bshes pa'i spring yig rgya cher bshad pa tshig gsal ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon blo gros chen pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal rtsigs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan lo phab pa'o//
slob ma la springs pa'i dka' 'grel slob dpon bai ro tsa na rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta chen po su ga ta shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob ma la springs pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon mkhas pa chen po shes rab 'byung gnas blo gros kyis rang gi slob ma rnams la phan pa'i don du mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi nA ya tsan+d+ra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon ka ma la shI las lho za mo tshangs dbyangs la sdug bsngal gyi bye brag bstan pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas gsang pas bod kyi rgyal po khri srong lde btsan rje 'bangs dang khong btsun rnams la brdzangs pa'i spring yig go//
slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa dad skyed sgron ma rdzogs so//
sangs rgyas mchog gi dpe de dang po rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba ban+de tshul khrims yon tan gyis bsgyur cing / dge slong rin chen bzang pos bcos nas zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
mya ngan med pa'i sgo nas klu btul pa'i le'u rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po gnas brtan a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba//
zhes bya 'di dpal 'byor rab brtan gyi rgya dpe las zh lu lo tsA bas bsgyur cing zhus so//
gnas brtan spyan drangs slob dpon b+ha ba kan+da s+ya zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /a tsar+ya dzi na mi tra dang / ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'di rgya dpe shog gcig ma ma cig lag tu byung ba/ bstan pa'i gtad rabs su 'dug pas mgo 'jug ma tshang na yang / tshong 'dus kyi pho brang du 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal gyis bsgyur ba yin no//
dgra bcom pa dge 'dun 'phel bar gyis lung bstan pa rdzogs so//
li yul lung bstan pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so///

slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su d+ha rak+Shi ta dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge bsnyen seng rgyal gyis bsgyur cing zhus pa'o/ 'jam pa'i mgon pos bkas bskul phyogs kyi glang po'i bstan bcos rgya mtsho ltar zab 'di/ rigs ldan rgyal po'i bka' bskul bor bzangs srung mdzad ces bya sde bdun bshad mkhan dang / gzus chung ston pa'i bkas bskul dge bsnyen sengrgyal zhes bya zha ma lo ts+tshas bsgyur/ dge gang bsod nams bkas skul 'gro kun rigs lam la gnas byang chub myur thob shog/
tshad ma kun las btus pa rtsod pa chen po shin du phra ba'i thugs mnga' ba/ slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /phyogs rnams kun gyi phas kyi rgol ba rnams/ 'joms par byed la glang po'i stobs ldan pa/ phyogs kyi glang po'i gzhung kun las btus pa/ bdag nyid kyi ni 'byor pa la brten nas/ shis pa'i dge gnas gtsug lag khang gnas su/ rgya gar mkhan po gser gyi go cha dang / sgra bsgyur lo tsA dad pa'i shes rab kyis/ bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa yin//
rgya gar gyi mkhan po rigs pa smra ba'i gtsug gi nor bur grags pa ba su d+ha ra rak+Shi ta dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba zha ma dge bsnyen seng rgyal gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
tshad ma kun las btus pa'i 'grel pa rtsed pa chen po shin tu phra ba'i thugs mnga' ba slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /phyogs rnams kun gyi phas kyi rgol ba rnams/ 'joms par byed la glang po'i stobs ldan pa/ phyogs kyi glang po'i gzhung kun las btus pa/ bdag nyid kyi ni 'byor pa la brten nas/ shi pa'i dge gnas gtsug lag khang gnas su/ rgya gar mkhan po gser gyi go cha dang / sgra bsgyur lo tsA dad pa shes rab kyis/ bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa yin//
dmigs pa brtags pa'i tshig gi le'ur byas pa slob dpon phyogs kyi gling pos mdzad pa rdzogs so
dmigs pa brtags pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dus gsum brtag pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /paN+Di ta chen po shAn+ta ka ra gup+ta'i zhal snga nas/ lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba'o//
tshad ma rigs par 'jug pa'i sgo slob dpon chen po phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po thams cad mkhyen dpal bsrung ba las/ shAkya'i dge slong grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang chen por bsgyar ba'o//
tshad ma'i bstan bcos rig pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar las rgya'i lo tsA ba thang sam tsang gis bsgyur cing / slad kyis rgya'i dge shes sing gyang jus dang / bod kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen ston gzhon gyis bod skad du bsgyur cing / phyis gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i sde pa las rab tu byung ba rgya nag chen po'i lha'i btsun pa chos kyi rin chen gyis/ dpal sa skya'i gtsug lag khang du rgya'i dpe dang / bod kyi dpe gnyis po legs par btugs shing bcos te dag par bsgyur ba'o/ rgya'i dpe la rigs pa la 'jug pa zhes snang /eing sang bod rnams rigs pa'i sgo zhes grags so//
phyogs chos dgu'i 'khor lo ni/ slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /za hor mkhas pa bo d+hi sa twa dang / dge slong d+harma a sho kas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
tshad ma rnam 'grel las gzhan gyi don gyi tshig le'u byas pa/ yul lho phyogs kyi rgyud du byung ba/ gzhung lug ngan pa thams cad ches shin tu 'khrul par 'jug pa/ snyan pa'i grags pas sa'i steng ma lus pa khyab pa 'gran zla med pa'i mkhas pa chen pa dpal chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su b+hU ti shrAn+ti dang bod kyi lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur/ yang paN+Di ta skal ldan rgyal po dang / dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis cing zad bcos/ dpal ldan dam pa'i las la mngon dgyis pa/ smad med che ba'i bdag can rgyal po mchog /dge ba'i thugs mnga' nges pas sa skyong pa/ mi yi bdag po dbang lde'i bkas bskul nas/ brtson ldan lhag par dpyod ldan 'chad po dang / nyan po rgol dang phyir rgol don nges dang / 'bel gtam dga' ston rgya chen myong bya'i phyir/ 'dzam gling mkhas pa'i rgyan gyur rgyan 'di bsgyur/ lta ngan kun sel gnyis su med pa yi/ don dam rnam dpyod lhur lan bstan bcos 'di/ gzhung mang don dka' sgrub par dka' na yang / 'bras bu che phyir 'bad par rigs pa yin/ log pa'i rgyun phyogs rjes su gzhol gyur ba/ lta ba'i chu bo bzlog par dka' mod kyi/ yang dag rigs pas legs par brda sprad na/ 'ga' yi yid la ci ste 'bab mi 'gyur/ sgra don gnyis ka nyams su bder lon te/ mun sbrul gyi ni ma bslad legs bsgyur pa/ sngon gyi sgyur byed dam pa deg dag gi /dri tsam bro ba da lta kho bo zad/ dpal ldan kha che'i rigs pa pa'i/ gtsug gi nor bu skal ldan ni/ rgyal po zhes bya la thos nas/ blo ldan blo ldan bzang pos 'di bsgyur ro/ grong khyer chen po dpe med kyi shar phyogs na/ yul 'khor lo 'dzin zhes bya ba/ grub pa'i gnas su grags pa'i 'dabs/ rnam par rgyal ba'i zhing zhes bya bar/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po skal ldan rgyal po dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/ dus phyis sa'i steng na 'gren zla thams cad dang bral ba'i mkhas pa bsod snyoms pa chen po/ shAkya shrI b+ha dra la sogs pa rnams dang / shAkya'i dge slong kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
tshad ma rnam par nges pa rnam par nges pa zhes bya ba/ yul lho phyogs kyi rgyud du byung ba/ gzhung lugs ngan pa thams cad ches shin tu du 'khrul par 'jug pa/ snyan pa'i grags pas sa'i steng ma lus par khyab pa/ 'gran zla med pa'i mkhas pa chen po/ dpal chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi kha che'i paN+Di ta gzhan la phan bzang po la sogs pa dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis/ kha che'i grong khyer dpe med du bsgyur ba'o//
rigs pa'i thigs pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa rdzogs so// paN+di ta gzhan la phan pa bzang po la sogs pa dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gta la phab pa'o//
gtan tshigs kyi thigs pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nya war ma dang zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phan pa'o//
'brel ba brtag pa'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa rdzogs so// rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nya na gar+b+ha dang lo tsA ba ban+de nam mkhas bsgyur/ slad kyi pan+Di ta rab 'byor zhi ba dang / lo tsa ba ting nge 'dzin bzang pos bcos shing gtan la phab ba'o//
'brel ba brtag pa zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa/ smra ba'i seng ge slob dpon chos kyi grags mdzad pa rdzogs so//
rigs pa chen po sa'i steng ma lus pa na/ smra ba'i glang po che'i spyi bo gnon par mdzad pa'i seng ge /phyogs ma lus par snyan grags pa can/ dpal slob dpon chos kyi grags pas sbyar pa las/ tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi li'u dang po'i 'grel pa rdzogs so//

smra ba chen po slob dpon lha dbang blos mdzad pa tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi dga' 'grel rdzogs so// bde skyid dpal lha btsun byang chub 'od kyi bka' lung gis so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po paN+Di ta su b+hU ti shrI dang / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur ba'o//
rtsod pa'i rigs pa 'di ni dam pa gzhan la phan par dgyes pa dag gis gsungs/ gang phyir 'gro ba mi shes yis de nyid mthong ba dag la sgrib byed pa'i/ de phyir de la yang dag gsal bar bya phyir bdag gis 'bad pas 'di byas so/ /slob dpon chen po d+harma kIrti'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rtsod pa'i rig pa zhes pa'i rab tu byed pa rdzogs so/ /dpal lha btsun pa zhi ba 'od kyi zhal snga nas dang / dpal lha btsan po khri bkra shis mnga' bdag rtse lde btsan gyi zhal snga nas kyis bkas/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po dz+nyA na shrI ba d+ha'i zhal snga nas dang / dge slong dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ slad kyis kyang paN+Di ta chen po dI paM ka ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong dar ma grags kyi zhus shing gtan la phab pa'o//
rgyud gzhan grub pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon d+harma kIrtisa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi shud+d+ha sing ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//


bcom ldan 'das 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs sgom pa/ slob dpon shAkya'i blos sbyar pa tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi 'grel bshad rdzogs so/ /'di ni lo tsA ba rma dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur pa'o//


tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi rgyan zhes bya ba slob dpon shes rab 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa rdzogs so// kha che'i paN+Di ta skal ldan rgyal po dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bgyur/ slad kyi kha chen paN+Di ta ku mA ra shrI dang zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong 'phags pa shes rab kyis zhus shing bcos te gtan la phab pa//


tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi rgyan gyi 'grel bshad slob dpon rgyal ba can gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bcom ldan 'das rigs gsum mgon po'i sprul pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i gdung rgyud mi rje lhas mdzad pa bod kyi lha btsan po shAkya'i dge slong lha bla ma zhi ba 'od kyi zhal snga nas dang /bod kyi lha btsan po dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag chen po khri bkra shis rtse lde btsan gyi zhal snga nas/ rgyal po'i yang rgyal po chen po 'phrul gyi lha btsan po khu dbon gyi bkas/ thugs dam sa'i snying po tho ling dpal dpe med lhun gyi grub pa'i gtsug lag khang du/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal bi kram la shI la'i mkhas ma chen po paN+Di ta shrI dI paM ka ra rak+Shi te dang / zhang zhung gi lo tsA ba chen po mang 'or ban+de byang chub shes rab kyis nan tan snying por byas nas gtan la phab par bsgyur ba'o/ bstan bcos 'di'i gzhung gi tshad ni bam po drug cu yin no//



tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi 'grel pa las le'u gsum pa'i bshad pa'o/ slob dpon chen po shes rab 'byung gnas sbas pa'i slob ma slob dpon nyi ma sbas pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so//




dpal mkhas pa dza mA ris sbyar pa tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi rgyan gyi TI ka rdzogs so/ bam po brgyad cu rtsa gnyis pa rdzogs so/ /dpal ldan dbang rgyal dbang phyug lta bur 'byor ldan kun la khyab pa yis/ grags pa gsal ldan zla 'dra'i gzhi gyur mchog tu yang dag la gnas pa/ rab dang yid can mkhas pa rnams kyi rtag par shin tu brjod bya gang / sems can don la mngon par dgag pa'i sdom rtson dam pa de'i ngor/ blo bzang gad na blo bzang blo gros bzang po dang / sgra bsgyur rnams kyi rgyan gyur blo ldan bzang po yis/ rnam 'grel dam pa'i rgyan du gyur pa'i TI ka 'di/ snye thang brag sna bkra shis gtsug lag khang du bsgyur/ tshad ma rgyan gyi TI ka paN+Di ta su ma ti dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//

slob dpon chos mchog gis sbyar ba rnam par nges pa'i TI ka 'thad ldan zhes bya ba rdzogs so// bstan bcos chen po don dang tshig tu bcas/ legs rtogs 'gro na nyi bzhin gsal byed pa/ tshul khrims gtsang ma'i dri ngad ldang ba gang / slob dpon chos mchog rtog be ngan 'joms mchog /yang dag don gsal tshad ma'i bstan bcos 'di/ legs par bsgyur las byung ba'i bsod nams gang / des ni log lta'i rgyun phyogs skye bo rnams/ yang dag rigs pa'i lam du 'jug par shog /kha che'i paN+Di ta gzhan la phan pa bzang po la sogs pa dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis grong khyer dpe med du bsgyur ba'o//
tshad ma rnam par nges pa'i 'grel bshad mkhas pa'i grags pas rgya mtsho'i mthas klas par khyab pa/ slob dpon ye shes dpal bzang pos zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /gnas brtan mkhas pa chen pa dz+nyA na shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi brtson 'grus kyis bsgyur/ khyung po mtshan bzhi khams zla hor phrug gis sbyin par bya ba'i chos rnams nye bar sbyar zhing gsal ba btab nas/ gzhung nye bar sbyar te/ brtsams nas bsgyur pa lags so
slob dpon chos mchog gis sbyar pa'i tshad ma rnam par nges pa'i 'grel bshad las/ le'u gnyis pa'o/ 'di la bam po bcu gnyis dang / tshigs bcad sum cu rtsa gnyis yod do//

rigs pa'i thigs pa rgya cher 'grel pa slob ma la phan pa las le'u gsum pa'o/ rgya cher 'grel pa'i gzhung tshad ni/ sh+lo ka chig stong dag dang ni/ de bzhin sh+lo ka sum bcur ni/ yongs su bsdoms te mngon par brjod/ rigs pa'i thigs pa rgya cher 'grel pa slob ma la phan pa zhes bya ba slob dpon 'dul ba'i lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dza na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rigs pa'i thigs pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa slob dpon chos mchog gis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong d+harma A lo kas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti kIrtidanga / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan she rab kyis slad kyi dpe dang gtugs te legs par bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rigs pa'i thigs pa'i phyogs snga ma mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon mang du thos pa ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi shud+d+ha sing+ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal rtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur te gtan la phab pa'o//
rigs pa'i thigs pa'i don bsdus pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tras mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ran dra bo d+hi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
gtan tshigs kyi thigs pa'i brgya cher 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po pradz+nyA warma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa//
gtan tshigs thigs pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa bram ze a tsa Tasa rnam par sbyar ba rdzogs so/ /'dzam gling snying po kha che'i grong khyer du/ mkhas pa'i snying po chos kyi grags pa'i 'grel/ dam chos snying po tshad ma bsgyur ba las/ snying po med pa rnams kyi snying por shog/

'brel pa brtag pa'i rgya cher bshad pa/ slob dpon dul ba'i lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang lo tsA ba ban+de nam mkhas bsgyur ba'o
'brel pa brtag pa'i 'brel pa bram ze shang+ka rA nan+dasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta chen po pa ra ha ta'i zhabs la zhus nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong dga' ba'i rdo rjes bsgyur ba'o//
rgyud gzhan grub pa'i 'grel bshad slob dpon dul ba'i lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi shud+d+ha sing ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dpal rtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rtsod pa'i rigs pa'i 'grel pa don rnam par 'byed pa ces bya ba/ slob dpon chen po shAn+ta rak+Shi tas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dpal tshangs pa'i 'byung gnas bsam yas kyi gtsug lag khang du/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mA ra shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong 'phags pa shes rab dang / 'bro seng dkar gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
slob dpon dul ba lhas mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dmigs pa brtag pa rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon dul ba'i lha shes bya'i dmigs pa mtha'i dag la gzhol ba smra ba'i seng ge mu stegs can glang po che'i glad pa 'gems par mdzad pas sbyar ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAkya seng ha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus nas gtan la phab pa'o//
rigs pa grub pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so// paN+Di ta shrI sing ha pra b+ha dang lo tsA ba dge slong bai ro tsa nas bsgyur pa'o//
thams cad mkhyen pa grub pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa slob dpon dge srungs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so//
phyi rol gyi don grub pa ces bya ba'i tshig le'u byas pa/ slob dpon dge srungs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon chen po dzi na mi tra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
thos pa brtags pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ slob dpon dge srungs kyi mdzad pa rdzogs so//
gzhan sel brtag pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ slob dpon deg srungs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
dbang phyug 'jig pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ slob dpon srungs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
tshad ma brtag pa slob dpon chos mchog gis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon chos mchog gi mdzad pa tshad ma brtag pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
gzhan sel brtag pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ slob dpon deg srungs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//
jig rten pha rol grub pa zhes bya ba slob dpon chos mchog gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /grong khyer chen po dpe med kyi dbus rat+na ra smi'i gtsug lag khang du kha che'i rgyal po shrI ha ri sha de ba'i sku ring la/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po skal ldan rgyal po dang / bod kyi sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba dge slong pa tshab nyi ma grags kis bgyur ba'o//
glegs bam bklag ba'i thabs paN+Di ta dA na shI las rang 'gyur du mdzad pa rdzogs so//
slob dpon chos mchog gis sbyar ba skad cig ma 'jig pa grub pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po skal ldan rgyal po dang / lo tsA ba dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyi bsgyur ba'o//
slob dpon bram ze mu tig bum pas mdzad pa skad cig ma 'jig pa grub pa'i rnam par 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi na ya ka ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong grags 'byor shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//
lhan cig dmigs par nges par grub pa zhes bya ba/ rtsod par smra ba'i mchog slob dpon dpal shes rab 'byung gnas sbas pa'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /bal yul gyi paN+Di ta co ha du shAn+ti b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba 'bro seng dkar dge slong shAkya'i 'od kyis bsgyur pa//
gzhan sel ba grub pa/ dge bsnyen dam pa/ mkhas pa chen po bram ze shang+ka rA nan+dasa mdzad pa rdzogs so// grong khyer depa med du/ kha che'i paN+Di ta ma no ra tha dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan she rab kyis bsgyur ba'o/ bsgyur dpe las gtugs//
'brel ba grub pa slob dpon mkhas pa chen po bram ze'i rigs su sku 'khrungs pa chos kyi grags pa gnyis pa zhes 'jig rten na gtam du grags shing rtog ge pa phal pa'i gzhung 'jig pa dang / thog pa med pa don gyi de kho na rnam par 'jog pa'i blo'i mthu stobs kyis 'gran zla dang bral ba/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa la gces spras su 'dzin pas legs par bshad pa'i ro myong pa la sems gcig tu gzhol ba dge bsnyen dam pa shang+ka rA nan+dasa mdzad pa rdzogs so/ paN+Di ta skal ldan rgyal po dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o
tshigs su bcad pa bcu gcig gis bsdus nas mngon sum dang mi dmigs pa rnam pa gsum sngon du 'gro bas rgyu dang 'bras bu'i ngo bo grub pa zhes bya ba/ mkhas pa chen po dz+nyA na shrI mi tras zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta ku mA ra kla shu dang / lo tsA ba dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur/ slad kyi bal yul kyi paN+Di ta a nan+da shrI dang / lo tsA ba de nyid kyi gtugs shing gtan la phab pa'o
rnam par rig pa tsam nyid du grub pa zhes bya ba mkhas pa chen po rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ bal yul gyi paN+Di ta shAn+ti b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba 'bro dge slong shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o/ slad nas paN+Di ta chen po de nyid dang / klog skya shes rab brtsegs kyis gtan la phab pa//
nang gi khyab pa slob dpon chen po mkhas pa rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mA ra ka la sha dang / dge slong shAkya 'od kyi bsgyur ba'o//
gtan tshigs kyi de kho na nyid bstan pa/ mkhas pa chen po dze ta ri'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta ku ma rA kla shu dang / lo tsA dge slong shAkya 'od kyi bsgyur cing zhus nas gtan la phab pa'o//
chos dang chos can gtan la dbab pa slob dpon dze ga ris mdzad pa rdzogs so//
byis pa 'jug pa'i rtog ge zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po dgra las rgyal bas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po nA ga rak+Shi ta dang / bod kyi sum pa lo tsA ba dpal mchog dang po'i rdo rjes bsgyur ba'o//
dza gat+ta la'i gtsug khang chen po'i mkhas pa chen po dge slong thar pa'i 'byung gnas kyis sbas pas sbyar ba'i rtog ge'i skad du/ gzhan gyi rjes su dpag pa yongs su bcad pa rdzogs so/ /rtog ge'i skad 'di byas nas ni/ bdag gis bsod nams gang bsags pa/ sangs rgyas nyid du ltag bgrod shog rtog ge'i skad rdzogs so/ /tshul 'di ni gang zag dam pa rnam kyi bka' drin la brten nas nang dang phyi'i gzhung lugs du ma rnams la blo'i snang ba cher rgyas pa sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba dbang dge slong dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas paN+Di ta la ma bltos par rang nyid kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
rigs pa'i sbyor ba 'jug pa nyid/ kha che yul gyi mkhas pa che po dngos grub brnyes pa bram ze'i slob dpon chen po rin chen rdo rje'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rigs pa'i sbyor ba zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal rab 'byor zhi ba'i zhal snga nas dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong ting nge 'dzin bzang pos bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//

slob dpon zhi ba 'tsho'i zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa/ de kho na nyid bsdus pa'i tshig le'u byas pa rdzogs so/ /gu ge yul gyi dbyen sa ri bo dge gnas phun tshogs gling du/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal gu NA ka ra shrI b+ha dra'i zhal snga nas dang / sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba chen po dpal lha btsan po shAkya'i dge slong lha bla ma zhi ba 'od kyi zhal snga nas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ grangs can gcer bu bye brag pa dang rgyang 'phren rigs pa can dang sangs rgyas de dag gi phyogs ni/ chu klung pa dang tsa ra ka dang dus smra spyod pa brda sprod zhi ba tshangs dang sna tshogs tshal/ sgra yi tshangs pa rig byed mtha' dang byed brag smra dang mdo sde sems tsam dbu ma de dag gi / bya brag lung bcas shes pa'i spyod yul gang yin 'di ni rtogs nas 'gro la phan phyir bdag gis bsgyur//

de kho na nyid bsdus pa'i dka' 'grel slob dpon chen po ka ma la shI las mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po mkhas pa chen po de ben dra b+ha dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong grags 'byor shes rab kyis bsgyur/ /brtse ldan bde bar gshegs pa'i bka'/ /kun la rab 'byam rtog ge'i gtso/ /chos kyi grags pa gnyis pa des/ /gsal ba'i tshig gi bkod gzhu 'di/ /bdag gzhan gzhung lugs rgya mtsho yis/ /mthar son mkhas pa lha dbang blo/ /bsnyen las grub mtha' mtha' dag la/ /blo yi snang pa thob nas bsgyur/ /sngon gyi sgyur byed mkhas rnams kyis/ /ji lta'i bgrod lam tshe rnams kyis/ /'bad pas mthong bar ma gyur gang / /ci zhig ltar te bdag gis te/ /bdag ni brtson dang mi ldan zhing / /shes rab lhag pa med mod kyang / /'di ltar don dang rjes mthun zhing / /tshig gi sdeb sbyor rab gsal ba/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas kyis byin rlabs sam/ /skye ba gzhan du goms par la/ /'on kyang brtson 'grus brtsams rnams kyis/ /nyes pa dor la legs pa long / /dpal ldan rigs gsum mgon po'i rgyud/ /stod ris mun pa'i snang gyur pa/ /rje rgyal byang chub sems dpa'i dbon/ brtan zhin mi 'gyur gzi brjid ldan/ /dgongs zab dam pa'i lam la dgyis/ /mtha' bzhi'i rgyal phran zil gnon pa/ /mnga' bdag dbang phyug dam ba'i rje/ /bsod nams rtse yis bkas bskus nas/ /gzhung lugs ngan pa kun 'joms shing / /bde gshegs bstan pa gsal byed pa/ /dpal ldan pad+ma'i dang tshul gyis/ /don chen ldan pa'i bstan bcos 'di //bsgyur pa'i dge bas bdag gzhan kun/ /lta ngan thams cad rab bcom nas/ /bkur bar dka' pa'i sangs rgyas kyi/ /bstan pa yin rings 'dzin par shog /'di tshigs su bcad pa khri brgyad stong yod/ /bam po drug cur byaso//

ces pa yangs pa dang dri ma med pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba/ tshad ma kun las btus pa'i 'grel bshad/ byung chub sems dpa'i yul pa slob dpon rgyal ba'i dbang po'i blo gros kyi zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /sh+lo ka stong phrag dgu po'o zhes rgya dpe'i mjug tu 'byung ngo / tshul 'di ni chos kyi rje shong ston lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis legs par bshad pa'i srol la sogs pa la brten nas legs par sbyar ba brda sprod pa'i tshul la blo'i snang ba cher rgyas pa dbang lo tsA ba dge slong dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas/ paN+Di ta la ma bltos par/ rang nyid kyis rgya dpe la bltas nas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ /dpal ldan rgyal ba'i dbang po'i bstan pa'i khang bzang phab bde'i mdzad ldan dam pa'i sgo 'phang mchog /dpal ldan phyogs kyi glang po'i gzhung lugs rang gi sde bas brtogs pa'i rtog ge ngan sel zhing / /rgyal ba rgyal dpog rkang mig gzigs zan ser skya 'jig rten mig gi rjes su 'jug rnams kyi/ rtog ge ngan pa rmeg med byed de'i 'grel bshad mchog 'dir sngon med bsgyur zhing zhu chen byas/ /gzhung 'grel 'grel bshad bcas pa rnams/ /tshig brling don yang gting dpag dka'/ /de slad legs par rab 'bad kyang / 'di la 'khrul med shin tu dkon/ /'phags blo ma thob blo gros skyon/ /rnam g.yeng le lo sbyor ba'i skyon/ /mkhas las ma thos skal ba'i skyon/ /'di yis skyon ldan bzod par mdzod/ /blo mchog sbyor ba rab rgyas shing / /gzu bor gnas pa'i dge mtshan ldan/ /legs bshad don gnyer dus skabs can/ de rnams rigs pa'i dga' ston mdzod/ /'dir 'bad dge bas 'gro ba kun/ /rigs pa dam pa'i dpung bsags te/ /bdud dang mu stegs kun bcom nas/ /rgyal ba'i dbang po myur thob shog/
lung du ston pa tsan+d+ra pa'i mdo 'i le'u drug pa rdzogs so/ /brda sprod pa tsan+d+ra pa'i mdo zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mi zhabs kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so// skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis legs par bsgyur ba las/ slar yang dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
lung du ston pa tsan+d+ra pa'i mdo 'i le'u drug pa rdzogs so/ /brda sprod pa tsan+d+ra pa'i mdo zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mi zhabs kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa rdzogs so/ bal po'i paN+Di ta chen po sgra pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor ltar bu bram ze chen po dze ta kar+Na'i zhal snga nas legs par mnyan te/ lo tsA ba shAkyi dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ dpal thar pa gling gi gtsug lag khang du legs par bsgyur pa'o// sa steng su nyi zla ltar grags par gyur cig
nye bar bsgyur pa nyi shu pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /sgra chen po paN+Di ta dzi ta kar+Na'i zhal snga nas legs par mnyan te/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ dpal thar pa gling gi gtsug lag khang du legs par bsgyur pa'o//
lung du ston pa'i yi ge'i mdo/ slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mas mdzad pa yongs su rdzogs so/ /legs par sbyar pa saM skr-i ti'i tshul cung zad khong du chud pa'i shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ dpal 'byor du ma la dbang thob cing / brtse ba dang dul ba la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan gyis chos dang ldan pa'i slob dpon lha'i sku mkhar gdung phubs su bsgyur ba'o//
brda sprod pa tsan+d+ra pa'i yi ge'i mdo'i 'grel pa sh+lo ka brgya bcu dgu pa rdzogs so/ /slob dpon chos skyong gis mdzad pa'o/ gnas chen po nye ba'i 'thung gcod bal po yam bu'i grong khyer gyi 'khor chen po yul skra khar sgra'i mkhan po chen po dzai tra kar+Na'i zhal snga nas legs par mnyan nas/ rtsa ba gung thang gi sa cha slob dpon lha'i sku mkhar gdung phugs su bsgyur zhing / mkhas pa chen po'i chen po rnams kyis gdan sa gtsug lag khang chen po dpal thar pa'i gling du shAkya'i dge slong nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos legs par bsgyur pa'o//
mdo'i spyir btang ba yang dag par bsdus pa rdzogs so// bal po'i mthil ye rang gi grong khyer du dge slong dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas yang dag pa bsgyur pa'o//
rnam dbye'i tshig le'u byas pa rdzogs so/ /yon tan mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa bla ma dam pa chos kyi rgyal po'i bka' lung gis/ b+ho Ti paN+Di ta yis bskul ba bzhin du bal po'i paN+Di ta dpal sa dbang bzang po'i zhal nas/ bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong shong blo brtan gyis bal po'i mthil du bsgyur ba'o//
ting nga'i mtha' rdzogs so/ /dpal gyi byed pa yin no/ bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas/ bal po'i yul rol pa'i grong khyer du bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
'brel pa mdor bstan pa zhes bya ba/ kA yas+tha tsAM kA dA sa yis mdzad pa rdzogs so/ /stag sde pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyi sras kyi thu bo/ skad gnyis smra ba rnams kyi mchog/ shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis legs par bshad pa'i srol la brten nas legs par sbyar ba brda sprod pa'i tshul cung zad rig pa dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyan tog shing dbon po dang / bde ba chos kyi bzang po la sogs pas mthun rkyen bsgrub pa la brten nas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
tsan+dra pa'i byings kyi mdo rdzogs so// 'di ni lung ston pa tsan+dra pa'i byings kyi dpiung gnyen slob dpon zla ba gang bas mdzad pa las btus te/ dpal e chos 'byung ba'i gtsug lag khang chen por/ lo tsA ba thugs rje dpal bzang pos dga' ba zhes pa chu pho 'brug gi lo'i tha skar gyi zla ba nyer bzhi'i nyin/ skar ma rgyal dang gza' phur bu 'dzom pa'i 'grub sbyor bzang po la rdzogs par bsgyur ba'o //
'brel pa grub pa zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa slob dpon nyi ma'i snying pos mdzad pa rdzogs so// legs par sbyar ba'i skad kyi brda sprod pa'i bstan bcos slob dopn chen po tsan+de go mis mdzad pa'i rje ssu 'brangs te/ byed pa can dang tshig sdud dang / de phan gyi rkyen dang / byings las tshig ting mtha' can sgrub pa dang / byings la ming sgrub pa rnams sde tshan du bsgrigs te gsal bar 'chad pa'i bstan bcos nying zhing rab tu gsal ba paN+Di ta nyi ma'i snying pos mdzad pa 'di/ sa thams cad kyi dbang phyug phun sum tshogs pa'i mkhyen rab dang thugs rje phul du byung ba mnga' ba'i chos kyi rgyal po chen po spyan snga rin po che dpal ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba'i lugs gnyis kyi mdun sa pho brang chen po sne'u gdong rtse'i gtsug lag khang du mthun rkyen rnams legs par stsal nas/ chos rje sprul sku rin po che zhwa dmar cod paN 'dzin pa bzhi pa dpal ldan d+harma kIrti'i dz+nyA na shrI b+ha dra'i zhal snga nsd legs par bsgyur cig ces pa'i bak' lung gnang ba bzhin/ brda sprod pa'i bstan bcos chen po dag thos nas cha shas tsam rig pa'i zhwa lu'u'i btsun pa 'gos lo tsA ba dge slong d+harma pA la b+ha dra zhes bgyi bas g.yag sde lo tsA ba'i phyag dpe las gsar du bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
u Na la sogs pa'i rkang pa gsum pa'i 'grel pa rdzogs so/ u Na la sogs pa'i mdo slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mi mdzad pa'i 'grel pa 'di/ dpal ldan e'i chos grwa chen por lo tsA ba thugs rje dpal bzang pos bsgyur ba'o/ 'grel pa mdzad pa po'i mtshan byad gi rgya dpe ma tshang bas mdzad byad ma chud do//
zhes pa sA d+hu kIrti'i jam dpal gyi sgra brda sprod pa dpal ldan ka lang+gi'i dbang phyug byang chub sems dpa'i yul gyi slob dpon rgyal po'i lhas rnam par bkod pa stong phrag brgyad pa las skabs lnga pa'i rkang pa gnyis pa'i 'grel pa rdzogs so/ /'di ni mkhyen brtse tshad med pa mnga' pa'i bdag nyid/ sprul sku rin po che zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa bzhi pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa spyan snga rin po che'i zhal snga nas bsgyur cig ces bka' stsal zhing mthun rkyen gnang ba las/ zhwa lu lo tsa ba dge slong d+harma pA la b+ha dra zhes bgyi bas dpal kun tu bzang po'i nags khrod gdan sa rin chen thil gyi gzims khang dbu btsugs nas/ dpal gra thang gi gtsugs lag khang du rdzogs par bsgyur ba'o//

ka lA pa'i mdo rdzogs so/ tshul 'di dpal ldan sa skya ru/ blo gros brtan pa gsum pa yis/ dur ga sing ha'i 'grel pa la/ brten nas sgra don je bzhin bsgyur/ 'di na phyogs kyang ma mthong bar/ mun sprul bsgyur dang 'chad byed pa/ de dang skye bo gzhan gyis kyang / 'di don myur du rtogs gyur cig /glo gros bzhin ras yangs pa la/ sgra dang tshad ma'i mig gnyis gsal/ mang du thos pa'i rna ba can/ dbyig gnyen sogs kyi zhal skyen bzhin/ 'on kyang deng dus gangs can 'dir/ khron pa'i rus sbal rang gnas bzhin/ blo chung rang gi blo nus kyis/ cher ngoms rnams kyis brnyas pa'i gnas/ skad gnyis smra ba'i gtsug gi nor bu shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis/ legs bshad lde mig mchog gi legs sbyar rin chen gter gyi kha phye nas/ sna tshogs gzhung lugs legs par rtogs pa'i 'byor par dbang byed 'di tsam zhig /dus 'dir dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa'i yid kyi dal so'i gnas su gyur/ rang gi rtogs pa 'phel dang de 'dra don gnyer ba/ blo ldan gzhan la phan phyir bsgyur bar rtsom pa na/ gzhung lugs nags su rnam dag blo yis rol byed pa/ dpal ldan smra ba'i seng ges bskul ba rdzogs par bsgrubs/ deng sang bstan pa nyams dmas pas/ 'di lta'i tshul la mthun bsgrub pa/ 'jug pa shin tu nyung mod kyi/ shes na mkhas pa'i go 'phang thob/ 'di na mkhas par bya 'dod cing / gang zhig shes nas mkhas 'gyur ba/ 'di dang 'di 'dra'i gzhung mi slob/ de rnams blo ni bems po'am ci/ 'phags blo ma thob blo gro skyon/ mnyan pa ma grub skal pa'i skyon/ yang yang ma bltas brtson 'grus skyon/ des skyon ldan na mkhas bzod mdzod/ 'dir 'bad dge bas 'gro ba kun/ rang rang skad las gsung rab don/ brjod mang de nyid rab rtogs nas/ ngag gi dbang phyug nyid gyur cig/
sgra'i bstan bcos cha bsags kyi mdo'i 'grel pa lo tsA ba chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis ji snyed bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
zhes pa durga sing+hasa mdzad pa'i 'grel par ming bzhi par rkang pa dang po rdzogs so/ /lo tsA ba'i ming tsam 'dzin pa snyoms las pa dge slong dpal ldan bla gros brten pas/ las dang po pa rnams la phan pa'i ched du/ tri lo tsa na dA sa'i dka' 'grel dang btugs nas sgra don ji ltar ba bzhin du legs par/ dpal gnas po che'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
bram ze grags 'byor gyis byas pa'i slob ma la phan pa las/ kun bshad par rkang pa rdzogs so/ /lha bla ma zhi ba 'od kyis zhang zhung gi sa cha/ tho ling gser gyi gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
byings kyi tshogs rdzogs so/ shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ yi ge pa ni yo ga ba grub pa dpal bzang pa'o//
jo bo drag 'byor gyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa slob ma la phan pa kun tu thob po zhes pa'o/ 'di ni chos kyi rje skad gnyis smra ba rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu thub pa'i dbang po dang mkhyen rabs mi gnyis pa dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa'i bka' drin las/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsungs rab dang tha snyad kyi gtsug lag rnams la blo gros rgya cher thob pa/ gangs can gyi khrod du skad gnyis smra ba shAkya'i dge slong byang chub rtse mos dgas po rdzam yul du bsgyur ba rdzogs so//
bya ba dam pa 'di ni gtsug lag khang bzang po/ rnam par gnon pa'i ngang tshul pad+ma'i 'byung gnas kyi/ ngang pa'i rgyal po sgra yi rgya mtsho'i skya ba 'dzin/ mkhas pa dpal ldan 'jam pa'i grags pas byas par gyur/ lo tsA ba'i ming tsam 'dzin pa snyoms las pa/ dge slong dpal ldan blo gros brtan pas/ dpal gnas po che'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba'o//
'di ni paN+Di ta chen po mAM hi ka wis bkod pa ste si la sogs pa'i bya ba rnams rdzogs sio// zhes pa mkhas pa'i dbang po dpal ldan blo gros brtan pa'i legs par bshad pa pha dang / bla ma dam pa chos grags dpal bzang po'i bka' lung dang / mthun rkyen phun sum tshogs pa la brten nas sgra rig pa'i dge slong lo tsA ba blo gros rgyal mtshan dang / blo gros dpal bzang pos legs par bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//
